                   ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Order,"Document Type"::"Return Order"])

                  SalesLineExitPoint(SalesLine,ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnRun,ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1",'');

            // Start PA034350
                  BranchCodeL := '';

            // Stop EU.0145355.145511
            // Stop EU.0104306

            // Start INC
              TempVehJnlLineG.DELETEALL;
            // Stop INC
              InvPostingBuffer[1].DELETEALL;
              DropShipPostBuffer.DELETEALL;

            // Stop PA032071

              SalesLine.SETRANGE("Document No.","No.");

            // Stop PA035901

                          ReturnRcptLine.TESTFIELD("Gen. Bus. Posting Group",SalesLine."Gen. Bus. Posting Group");

                          ReturnRcptLine.TESTFIELD("Variant Code",SalesLine."Variant Code");

                            SalesLine.FIELDERROR("Qty. to Invoice",Text024);

                          QtyToBeInvoicedBase := RemQtyToBeInvoicedBase - SalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive (Base)";
                          IF ABS(QtyToBeInvoiced) >
                             ABS(ReturnRcptLine.Quantity - ReturnRcptLine."Quantity Invoiced")
                          THEN BEGIN

                            QtyToBeInvoicedBase := ReturnRcptLine."Quantity (Base)" - ReturnRcptLine."Qty. Invoiced (Base)";
                          END;
                          RemQtyToBeInvoiced := RemQtyToBeInvoiced - QtyToBeInvoiced;
                          RemQtyToBeInvoicedBase := RemQtyToBeInvoicedBase - QtyToBeInvoicedBase;
                          ReturnRcptLine."Quantity Invoiced" :=
                            ReturnRcptLine."Quantity Invoiced" + QtyToBeInvoiced;
                          ReturnRcptLine."Qty. Invoiced (Base)" :=
                            ReturnRcptLine."Qty. Invoiced (Base)" + QtyToBeInvoicedBase;
                          ReturnRcptLine."Return Qty. Rcd. Not Invd." :=
                            ReturnRcptLine.Quantity - ReturnRcptLine."Quantity Invoiced";
                          ReturnRcptLine.MODIFY;
                          IF SalesLine.Type = SalesLine.Type::Item THEN

                              '');
                        UNTIL (ReturnRcptLine.NEXT = 0) OR (ABS(RemQtyToBeInvoiced) <= ABS(SalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive"));
                      END ELSE
                        ERROR(
                          Text025,
                          SalesLine."Return Receipt Line No.",SalesLine."Return Receipt No.");

                    IF ABS(RemQtyToBeInvoiced) > ABS(SalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive") THEN BEGIN
                      IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN

                      ERROR(Text037);

                  END ELSE BEGIN

                              SalesShptLine."Qty. Invoiced (Base)" - QtyToBeInvoicedBase;

                            SalesShptLine."Open Shipment" := SalesShptLine.Quantity <> SalesShptLine."Quantity Invoiced";

            // Stop INC

            // Start INC
                                '');
            // Stop INC
                          END;
                        UNTIL (SalesShptLine.NEXT = 0) OR (ABS(RemQtyToBeInvoiced) <= ABS(SalesLine."Qty. to Ship"));

                    IF ABS(RemQtyToBeInvoiced) > ABS(SalesLine."Qty. to Ship") THEN BEGIN
                      IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice THEN

                  END;

                  CASE SalesLine.Type OF

                                '');

                        END;

                        ResJnlLine."Total Price" := -SalesLine.Amount;

            // Start INC
                    SalesLine.Type::"Charge (Item)":

                        TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETFILTER("Applies-to Doc. Type",'<>%1',"Document Type");
                        TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",SalesLine."Line No.");
            // Start PA032441
                        IF TempItemChargeAssgntSales.FINDSET THEN

                          REPEAT

                            CASE TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type" OF
                              TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type"::Shipment:
                                PostItemChargePerShpt(SalesLine);
                              TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type"::"Return Receipt":
                                PostItemChargePerRetRcpt(SalesLine);
                            END;
                            TempItemChargeAssgntSales.MARK(TRUE);
                          UNTIL TempItemChargeAssgntSales.NEXT = 0;
                      END;

                  END;
            // Start PA035979
            // Start EU.0120161.122137
                  IF (SalesLine.Type >= SalesLine.Type::"Account (G/L)") AND (SalesLine."Qty. to Invoice" <> 0) AND
            // Start INC
                     NOT InternalCustomerG
            // Stop PA035979
            // Stop INC
                  THEN BEGIN
            // Stop EU.0120161.122137
                    // Copy Sales to buffer
                    IF (SalesLine."Gen. Bus. Posting Group" <> GenPostingSetup."Gen. Bus. Posting Group") OR
                       (SalesLine."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" <> GenPostingSetup."Gen. Prod. Posting Group")
                    THEN
                      GenPostingSetup.GET(SalesLine."Gen. Bus. Posting Group",SalesLine."Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
            // Start INC
                    ItemChargeAssignmPostedL := FALSE;
                    IF (SalesLine.Type = SalesLine.Type::"Charge (Item)") AND
                       (GLSetup."Charge (Item) Dimension" = GLSetup."Charge (Item) Dimension"::"Item Ledger")

                IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN BEGIN
                  VehicleOptionInvG.RESET;
                  VehicleOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
                  VehicleOptionInvG.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
            // Start PA032990
                  IF VehicleOptionInvG.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            // Stop PA032990
                    REPEAT
                      PostedVehicleOptionInvG.TRANSFERFIELDS(VehicleOptionInvG);
                      PostedVehicleOptionInvG."Document Type" := PostedVehicleOptionInvG."Document Type"::"Posted Invoice";
                      PostedVehicleOptionInvG."Veh. Order No." := PostedVehicleOptionInvG."Document No.";
                      PostedVehicleOptionInvG."Document No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
                      PostedVehicleOptionInvG.INSERT;
                    UNTIL VehicleOptionInvG.NEXT = 0;
                    VehicleOptionInvG.DELETEALL;
                  END;
                END;
                OrderItemPriceCalcG.RESET;
                OrderItemPriceCalcG.SETRANGE("Order Type",OrderItemPriceCalcG."Order Type"::"Sales Order");
                OrderItemPriceCalcG.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
                OrderItemPriceCalcG.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
            // Start PA032990
                IF NOT OrderItemPriceCalcG.ISEMPTY THEN
            // Stop PA032990
                  OrderItemPriceCalcG.DELETEALL;
                SalDocumentTextG.RESET;
                SalDocumentTextG.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
                SalDocumentTextG.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
            // Start PA032990
                IF NOT SalDocumentTextG.ISEMPTY THEN
            // Stop PA032990
                  SalDocumentTextG.DELETEALL;
                SalDiffTextG.RESET;
                SalDiffTextG.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
                SalDiffTextG.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
            // Start PA035134
                IF NOT SalDiffTextG.ISEMPTY THEN
            // Stop PA035134
                  SalDiffTextG.DELETEALL;

            // Start PA033985
                SalesIncentiveLineL.Area := SalesIncentiveLineL.Area::Sale;
                SalesIncentiveLineL."Document Type" := SalesIncentiveLineL."Document Type"::Invoice;
                SalesIncentivePostG.DeleteSalesIncentives(SalesIncentiveLineL.Area,
                  SalesHeader."Document Type",
                  SalesHeader."No.",
                  SalesIncentiveLineL.Area,
                  SalesIncentiveLineL."Document Type",
                  SalesInvHeader."No.");
            // Stop PA033985
              END;

            // Start PA036544
              EPRecRef2G.GETTABLE(SalesHeader);
              SalesInvoiceHeaderExitPoint(SalesInvHeader,ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnRun,ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 10",'');
            // Stop PA036544

              COMMIT;
            // Start INC
              IF RMSetupG.GET THEN
                IF RMSetupG."Create To-Do when Posting" THEN BEGIN
            // Stop INC
            // Start PA035817.28015
                  IF GUIALLOWED THEN
            // Stop PA035817.28015
                    Window.UPDATE(1, C_INC016);
                  IF Invoice AND (SalesHeader."Document Type" IN [
                     SalesHeader."Document Type"::Order,
                     SalesHeader."Document Type"::Invoice])
                  THEN
                    IF NOT ContactMgtCreateActivitiesG.RUN(SalesInvHeader) THEN
                      MESSAGE(C_INC017);
                END;
              COMMIT;
              CLEAR(GenJnlPostLine);
              CLEAR(ResJnlPostLine);
            // Start PA031882
            // Stop PA031882
              CLEAR(ItemJnlPostLine);

              ServSalesPostG.DeletedPackageNeutralLedger;
              CLEAR(ServSalesPostG);

            // Start INC
              DelWtyClaims;
            // Stop INC

            // Start PA033484
              IF ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::Service) AND
                 ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo")
              THEN
            // Start EU.0012448.13245
                ReverseVehicleLedgEntries("Service Order No.");
            // Stop EU.0012448.13245
            // Stop PA033484

            // Start PA035817.28015
              IF GUIALLOWED THEN
            // Stop PA035817.28015
                Window.CLOSE;
            // Start PA032441
              IF Invoice AND ("Bill-to IC Partner Code" <> '') THEN
                IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Order,"Document Type"::Invoice] THEN
                  ICInOutBoxMgt.CreateOutboxSalesInvTrans(SalesInvHeader)
                ELSE
                  ICInOutBoxMgt.CreateOutboxSalesCrMemoTrans(SalesCrMemoHeader);
            // Stop PA032441
            END;
            // Start PA032441
            UpdateAnalysisView.UpdateAll(0,TRUE);
            // Stop PA032441

            // Start PA036875.38906
            UpdateItemAnalysisView.UpdateAll(0, TRUE);
            // Stop PA036875.38906

            Rec := SalesHeader;

            // Start INC
            // Stop INC

            // Start PA036544
            SalesHeaderExitPoint(Rec,ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnRun,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'');
            // Stop PA036544
          END;

  }
  CODE

    PROCEDURE SetPostingDate@1(NewReplacePostingDate@1000 : Boolean;NewReplaceDocumentDate@1001 : Boolean;NewPostingDate@1002 : Date);
    BEGIN
      PostingDateExists := TRUE;
      ReplacePostingDate := NewReplacePostingDate;
      ReplaceDocumentDate := NewReplaceDocumentDate;
      PostingDate := NewPostingDate;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE PostItemJnlLine@2(SalesLine@1000 : Record 37;QtyToBeShipped@1001 : Decimal;QtyToBeShippedBase@1002 : Decimal;QtyToBeInvoiced@1003 : Decimal;QtyToBeInvoicedBase@1004 : Decimal;ItemLedgShptEntryNo@1005 : Integer;ItemChargeNo@1006 : Code[20]) : Integer;
    VAR
      ItemChargeSalesLine@1008 : Record 37;
      OriginalItemJnlLine@1013 : Record 83;
      ShipToAddress@1015 : Record 222;
      _INCADEA_@1101342643 : Integer;
      LocationL@1109400008 : Record 14;
      OrderItemPriceCalc@1109400005 : Record 5025809;
      ItemLedgEntry@1109400000 : Record 32;
      ItemJnlPostLineL@1119418000 : Codeunit 22;
      UnitPrice1@1109400006 : Decimal;
      UnitPrice2@1109400007 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      WITH SalesLine DO BEGIN
      // Stop INC
        IF (SalesHeader."Document Type" = SalesHeader."Document Type"::Invoice) AND
           ("Service Order No." <> '') AND ("Service Order Line No." <> 0) AND (QtyToBeInvoiced <> 0)
        THEN
          EXIT;
        // Do not post Service Credit Memo here, it will be posted over CU 5025645!!
        IF (SalesHeader."Document Type" = SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo") AND
           ("Service Order No." <> '') AND ("Service Order Line No." <> 0)
        THEN
          EXIT;
        ItemJnlLine.INIT;
        ItemJnlLine."Posting Date" := SalesHeader."Posting Date";
        ItemJnlLine."Document Date" := SalesHeader."Document Date";
        ItemJnlLine."Source Posting Group" := SalesHeader."Customer Posting Group";
        ItemJnlLine."Salespers./Purch. Code" := SalesHeader."Salesperson Code";
      // Start PA036728
        ItemJnlLine."Salesperson Code 2" := SalesHeader."Salesperson Code 2";
      // Stop PA036728
        ItemJnlLine."Country Code" := SalesHeader."VAT Country Code";
      // Start PA032441
        IF SalesHeader."Ship-to Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
          ShipToAddress.GET("Sell-to Customer No.",SalesHeader."Ship-to Code");
          ItemJnlLine."Country Code" := ShipToAddress."Country Code";
        END ELSE
          ItemJnlLine."Country Code" := SalesHeader."Sell-to Country Code";
      // Stop PA032441
        ItemJnlLine."Reason Code" := SalesHeader."Reason Code";
        ItemJnlLine."Posting No. Series" := SalesHeader."Posting No. Series";
        ItemJnlLine."Item No." := "No.";
        ItemJnlLine."Item Type" := "Item Type";
        ItemJnlLine."Item Group Code" := "Item Group Code";
        ItemJnlLine."Customer Group Code" := "Customer Group Code";
        ItemJnlLine."Purch. Order Type" := SalesHeader."Purch. Order Type";
      // Start INC
        IF (Type <> Type::"Charge (Item)") AND ("Vehicle Status" <> "Vehicle Status"::" ") THEN
      // Stop INC
          ItemJnlLine."Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status";
        ItemJnlLine.Description := Description;
        ItemJnlLine."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
        ItemJnlLine."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := "Shortcut Dimension 2 Code";
      // Start PA035597
        ItemJnlLine."Dimension Set ID" := "Dimension Set ID";
      // Stop PA035597
        ItemJnlLine."Location Code" := "Location Code";
      // Start PA032441
        ItemJnlLine."Bin Code" := "Bin Code";
        ItemJnlLine."Variant Code" := "Variant Code";
      // Stop PA032441
        ItemJnlLine."Inventory Posting Group" := "Posting Group";
        ItemJnlLine."Gen. Bus. Posting Group" := "Gen. Bus. Posting Group";
        ItemJnlLine."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" := "Gen. Prod. Posting Group";
        ItemJnlLine."Applies-to Entry" := "Appl.-to Item Entry";
        ItemJnlLine."Serial No." := "Serial No.";
        ItemJnlLine."Transaction Type" := "Transaction Type";
        ItemJnlLine."Transport Method" := "Transport Method";
        ItemJnlLine."Entry/Exit Point" := "Exit Point";
        ItemJnlLine.Area := Area;
        ItemJnlLine."Transaction Specification" := "Transaction Specification";
        ItemJnlLine."Drop Shipment" := "Drop Shipment";
        ItemJnlLine."Entry Type" := ItemJnlLine."Entry Type"::Sale;
        ItemJnlLine."Variant Code" := "Variant Code";
      // Start PA036838
        IF "Document Type" <> "Document Type"::Invoice THEN
          ItemJnlLine."Order Line No." := "Line No."
        ELSE
          ItemJnlLine."Order Line No." := "Order Line No.";
        ItemJnlLine."Document Line No." := "Line No.";
      // Stop PA036838
      // Start INC
        IF ItemLedgShptEntryNo = 0 THEN
          ItemJnlLine."Book No." := "Book No."
        ELSE BEGIN
          ItemLedgEntry.GET(ItemLedgShptEntryNo);
          ItemJnlLine."Book No." := ItemLedgEntry."Book No."
        END;
      // Stop INC
        ItemJnlLine."Bin Code" := "Bin Code";
        ItemJnlLine."Unit of Measure Code" := "Unit of Measure Code";
        ItemJnlLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure" := "Qty. per Unit of Measure";
      // Start PA032441
        ItemJnlLine."Return Reason Code" := "Return Reason Code";
        ItemJnlLine."Order Date" := SalesHeader."Order Date";
      // Stop PA032441
      // Start PA032651
        IF QtyToBeShipped = 0 THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032651
          ItemJnlLine."Document No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
          ItemJnlLine."External Document No." := GenJnlLineExtDocNo;
      // Start PA032441
          ItemJnlLine."Posting No. Series" := SalesHeader."Posting No. Series";
      // Stop PA032441
      // Start PA032651
          IF QtyToBeInvoiced <> 0 THEN
            ItemJnlLine."Invoice No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
      // Stop PA032651
        END ELSE BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA036547
          IF SalesHeader."Document Type" IN [
             SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Return Order",
             SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]
      // Stop PA036547
      THEN BEGIN
            ItemJnlLine."Document No." := ReturnRcptHeader."No.";
            ItemJnlLine."External Document No." := ReturnRcptHeader."External Document No.";
      // Start PA032441
            ItemJnlLine."Posting No. Series" := ReturnRcptHeader."No. Series";
      // Stop PA032441
          END ELSE BEGIN
      // Stop INC
            ItemJnlLine."Document No." := SalesShptHeader."No.";
            ItemJnlLine."External Document No." := SalesShptHeader."External Document No.";
      // Start PA032441
            ItemJnlLine."Posting No. Series" := SalesShptHeader."No. Series";
      // Stop PA032441
          END;
      // Start PA032651
          IF QtyToBeInvoiced <> 0 THEN BEGIN
            ItemJnlLine."Invoice No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
            ItemJnlLine."External Document No." := GenJnlLineExtDocNo;
            IF ItemJnlLine."Document No." = '' THEN
              ItemJnlLine."Document No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
            ItemJnlLine."Posting No. Series" := SalesHeader."Posting No. Series";
          END;
      // Stop PA032651
        END;
        ItemJnlLine.Quantity := -QtyToBeShipped;
        ItemJnlLine."Quantity (Base)" := -QtyToBeShippedBase;
        ItemJnlLine."Invoiced Quantity" := -QtyToBeInvoiced;
        ItemJnlLine."Invoiced Qty. (Base)" := -QtyToBeInvoicedBase;
        ItemJnlLine."Unit Cost" := "Unit Cost (LCY)";
        ItemJnlLine."Source Currency Code" := SalesHeader."Currency Code";
        ItemJnlLine."Source Currency Unit Cost" := "Unit Cost";
      // Start INC
        ItemJnlLine."Value Entry Type" := ItemJnlLine."Value Entry Type"::"Direct Cost";
        IF ItemChargeNo <> '' THEN BEGIN
          ItemJnlLine."Item Charge No." := ItemChargeNo;
          "Qty. to Invoice" := QtyToBeInvoiced;
        END ELSE
          ItemJnlLine."Applies-from Entry" := "Appl.-from Item Entry";
      // Stop INC
        IF "Qty. to Invoice" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
          ItemJnlLine.Amount :=
            -ROUND(
              Amount *
              (QtyToBeInvoiced / "Qty. to Invoice"));
          ItemJnlLine."Discount Amount" :=
            -ROUND(
              ("Line Discount Amount" + "Inv. Discount Amount") *
              (QtyToBeInvoiced / "Qty. to Invoice"));
          IF QtyToBeInvoiced <> 0 THEN BEGIN
            ItemJnlLine."Invoice Discount" := ABS(ROUND(("Inv. Discount Amount" / QtyToBeInvoiced),0.00001));
            UnitPrice1 := ABS(ROUND((ItemJnlLine.Amount / QtyToBeInvoiced),0.00001)) + ItemJnlLine."Invoice Discount";
          END ELSE BEGIN
            ItemJnlLine."Invoice Discount" := ABS("Inv. Discount Amount");
            UnitPrice1 := ABS(ItemJnlLine.Amount) + ItemJnlLine."Invoice Discount";
          END;
          IF "Quantity Disc. %" <> 0 THEN
            ItemJnlLine."Quantity Discount" := (ROUND((UnitPrice1 * 100) /
              (100 - "Quantity Disc. %"),0.00001) - UnitPrice1);
          IF QtyToBeInvoiced <> 0 THEN
            ItemJnlLine."Sales Discount" :=
              ABS(
                ROUND(
                  (ItemJnlLine."Discount Amount" / QtyToBeInvoiced),0.00001)) -
                  ItemJnlLine."Quantity Discount" - ItemJnlLine."Invoice Discount"
          ELSE
            ItemJnlLine."Sales Discount" :=
              ABS(ItemJnlLine."Discount Amount") - ItemJnlLine."Quantity Discount" - ItemJnlLine."Invoice Discount";
          IF OrderItemPriceCalc.GET(
             OrderItemPriceCalc."Order Type"::"Sales Order","Document Type","Document No.","Line No.")
          THEN BEGIN
            ItemJnlLine."Sales Discount" := ItemJnlLine."Sales Discount" - OrderItemPriceCalc."Manual Price Adjustment";
            UnitPrice2 := UnitPrice1 + ItemJnlLine."Quantity Discount" + ItemJnlLine."Sales Discount";
            IF OrderItemPriceCalc."Price Calc. Surcharge %" <> 0 THEN
              ItemJnlLine."Sales Surcharge" :=
                ROUND(
                  (UnitPrice2 * OrderItemPriceCalc."Price Calc. Surcharge %" ) /
                  (100 + OrderItemPriceCalc."Price Calc. Surcharge %" ),0.00001);
          END;
        END;
        ItemJnlLine."Source Type" := ItemJnlLine."Source Type"::Customer;
        ItemJnlLine."Source No." := "Sell-to Customer No.";
      // Start PA032441
        ItemJnlLine."Source Code" := SrcCode;
      // Stop PA032441
        ItemJnlLine."Item Shpt. Entry No." := ItemLedgShptEntryNo;
        ItemJnlLine.Reserve := Reserve;

        IF Item.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
          ItemJnlLine."Main Group Code" := Item."Main Group Code";
          ItemJnlLine."Subgroup Code" := Item."Subgroup Code";
          ItemJnlLine."Line Group Code" := Item."Line Group Code";
        END;
        IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases" THEN
          ItemJnlLine."Main Area" := ItemJnlLine."Main Area"::"Parts Sales & Purchases";
        IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
          ItemJnlLine."Main Area" := ItemJnlLine."Main Area"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases";
        IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::Service THEN
          ItemJnlLine."Main Area" := ItemJnlLine."Main Area"::Service;
        ItemJnlLine."Source No. (Payment)" := "Bill-to Customer No.";
        IF "Quantity Shipped" = 0 THEN BEGIN
          ItemJnlLine."Qty. on First Purchase" := ItemJnlLine.Quantity;
          ItemJnlLine."Total Qty. First Receipt" := Quantity;
        END;
      // Start INC
      // Start PA037799
        IF ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Order, "Document Type"::"Credit Memo", "Document Type"::"Return Order"]) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA037799
      // Start PA033115
      // Stop PA033115
      // Stop INC
          ItemJnlLine."Order Date" := SalesHeader."Order Date";
      // Start PA037799
          IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order THEN
            ItemJnlLine."Order No." := SalesHeader."No."
          ELSE
            ItemJnlLine."Order No." := "Order No.";
      // Stop PA037799

        END;
      // Start PA032990.BMW
        IF LocationL.GET(SalesLine."Location Code") THEN
          ItemJnlLine."Branch Code" := LocationL."Branch Code"
        ELSE
          ItemJnlLine."Branch Code" := CurrBranchCodeG;
      // Stop PA032990.BMW


        ItemJnlLine."Disable for Requisition" := "Disable for Requisition";

      // Start INC
        IF Type <> Type::"Charge (Item)" THEN BEGIN
          ItemJnlLine.VIN := VIN;
          IF IsImporter THEN
            ItemJnlLine."Factory No." := SalesLine."Factory No.";
          ItemJnlLine."Book No." := "Book No.";
        END;
      // Stop INC
      // Start PA041023
        IF ItemJnlLine.VIN = '' THEN BEGIN
          ItemJnlLine.VIN := SalesLine."Supply VIN";
          ItemJnlLine."License No." := SalesLine."Reference License No.";
        END;
      // Stop PA041023

      // Start PA031882
        IF (SalesSetup."Exact Cost Reversing Mandatory") AND (Type = Type::Item) AND
           NOT Item."No Inventory Tracking"
        THEN
          IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN BEGIN
            IF Quantity > 0 THEN
              TESTFIELD("Appl.-from Item Entry");
          END ELSE BEGIN
            IF Quantity < 0 THEN
              TESTFIELD("Appl.-from Item Entry");
          END;
        IF ("Reserved Qty. (Base)" <> 0) AND (QtyToBeShippedBase <> 0) THEN BEGIN
          ReservMgtG.TransferSalesLineToItemJnlLine(SalesLine,ItemJnlLine,QtyToBeShippedBase);
        END;
      // Start PA035597
      // Stop PA035597
        OriginalItemJnlLine := ItemJnlLine;
        UpdateVehicleOwnOptions(SalesLine);
      // Start INC
        ItemJnlPostLineL.RUN(ItemJnlLine);
      // Stop INC

        IF (Type = Type::Item) AND SalesHeader.Invoice THEN BEGIN
          ClearItemChargeAssgntFilter;
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETCURRENTKEY(
            "Applies-to Doc. Type","Applies-to Doc. No.","Applies-to Doc. Line No.");
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Type","Document Type");
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. No.","Document No.");
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Line No.","Line No.");
      // Start PA032441
          IF TempItemChargeAssgntSales.FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA032441
            REPEAT
              TESTFIELD("Allow Item Charge Assignment");
              GetItemChargeLine(ItemChargeSalesLine);
              ItemChargeSalesLine.CALCFIELDS("Qty. Assigned");
              OriginalItemJnlLine."Item Shpt. Entry No." := ItemJnlLine."Item Shpt. Entry No.";
              PostItemChargePerOrder(OriginalItemJnlLine,ItemChargeSalesLine);
              TempItemChargeAssgntSales.MARK(TRUE);
            UNTIL TempItemChargeAssgntSales.NEXT = 0;
        END;
      // Stop PA031882
      // Start INC
      END;
      IF ItemLedgShptEntryNo = 0 THEN
        LastItemLedgEntrNoG := ItemJnlLine."Item Shpt. Entry No."
      ELSE
        LastItemLedgEntrNoG := ItemLedgShptEntryNo;
      // Stop INC
      EXIT(ItemJnlLine."Item Shpt. Entry No.");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE PostItemChargePerOrder@5801(ItemJnlLine2@1001 : Record 83;ItemChargeSalesLine@1002 : Record 37);
    VAR
      QtyToInvoice@1004 : Decimal;
      ItemJnlPostLineL@1109400000 : Codeunit 22;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      WITH TempItemChargeAssgntSales DO BEGIN
      // Start PA031882
      // Stop PA031882
        SalesLine.TESTFIELD("Allow Item Charge Assignment",TRUE);
        ItemJnlLine2."Document No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
        ItemJnlLine2."External Document No." := GenJnlLineExtDocNo;
        ItemJnlLine2."Item Charge No." := "Item Charge No.";
      // Start PA032441
        ItemJnlLine2.Description := ItemChargeSalesLine.Description;
      // Stop PA032441
        ItemJnlLine2."Unit of Measure Code" := '';
        ItemJnlLine2."Qty. per Unit of Measure" := 1;
        ItemJnlLine2."Applies-from Entry" := 0;
        IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
          QtyToInvoice :=
            CalcQtyToInvoice(SalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive (Base)",SalesLine."Qty. to Invoice (Base)")
        ELSE
          QtyToInvoice :=
            CalcQtyToInvoice(SalesLine."Qty. to Ship (Base)",SalesLine."Qty. to Invoice (Base)");
        IF ItemJnlLine2."Invoiced Quantity" = 0 THEN BEGIN
          ItemJnlLine2."Invoiced Quantity" := ItemJnlLine2.Quantity;
          ItemJnlLine2."Invoiced Qty. (Base)" := ItemJnlLine2."Quantity (Base)";
        END;
      // Start PA036838
        ItemJnlLine2."Document Line No." := ItemChargeSalesLine."Line No.";
        IF  ItemChargeSalesLine."Document Type" <>  ItemChargeSalesLine."Document Type"::Invoice THEN
          ItemJnlLine."Order Line No." :=  ItemChargeSalesLine."Line No."
        ELSE
          ItemJnlLine."Order Line No." :=  ItemChargeSalesLine."Order Line No.";
      // Stop PA036838

        ItemJnlLine2.Amount := "Amount to Assign" * ItemJnlLine2."Invoiced Qty. (Base)" / QtyToInvoice;
        IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
          ItemJnlLine2.Amount := -ItemJnlLine2.Amount;
        ItemJnlLine2."Source Currency Unit Cost" :=
          ROUND(ItemJnlLine2.Amount / ItemJnlLine2."Invoiced Qty. (Base)",
          Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
        IF SalesHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN
          ItemJnlLine2.Amount :=
            CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
              UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",ItemJnlLine2.Amount,SalesHeader."Currency Factor");
        ItemJnlLine2.Amount := ROUND(ItemJnlLine2.Amount);
        ItemJnlLine2."Unit Cost" := ROUND(
          ItemJnlLine2.Amount / ItemJnlLine2."Invoiced Qty. (Base)",GLSetup."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
        ItemJnlLine2."Applies-to Entry" := ItemJnlLine2."Item Shpt. Entry No.";

        IF SalesHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN
          ItemJnlLine2."Discount Amount" := ROUND(
            CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
              UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
              ItemChargeSalesLine."Inv. Discount Amount" * ItemJnlLine2."Invoiced Qty. (Base)" /
              ItemChargeSalesLine."Quantity (Base)" * "Qty. to Assign"  / QtyToInvoice,
              SalesHeader."Currency Factor"),GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision")
        ELSE
          ItemJnlLine2."Discount Amount" := ROUND(
            ItemChargeSalesLine."Inv. Discount Amount" * ItemJnlLine2."Invoiced Qty. (Base)" /
            ItemChargeSalesLine."Quantity (Base)" * "Qty. to Assign" / QtyToInvoice,
            GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision");

        ItemJnlLine2."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := ItemChargeSalesLine."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
        ItemJnlLine2."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := ItemChargeSalesLine."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code";
      // Start PA035597
        ItemJnlLine2."Dimension Set ID" := ItemChargeSalesLine."Dimension Set ID";
      // Stop PA035597
        ItemJnlLine2."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" := ItemChargeSalesLine."Gen. Prod. Posting Group";
      // Start PA035597
      // Stop PA035597
      // Start PA036549.33813
        ItemJnlPostLineL.RUN(ItemJnlLine2);
      // Stop PA036549.33813

      // Start PA035473
        IF SalesLine.VIN <> '' THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA035473
          InsertTempVehJnlLine(
            ItemChargeSalesLine,
            "Item Charge No.",
            ItemJnlLine2.VIN,ItemJnlLine2."Book No.",SalesLine."Branch Book No.",
            ItemJnlLine2.Amount,ItemJnlLine2."Invoiced Quantity",
            ItemJnlLine2."Applies-to Entry",
            ItemJnlLine2."Applies-to Value Entry");
      // Start PA035473
          InsertTempSalIncVehJnlLine(
            ItemChargeSalesLine,
            "Item Charge No.",
            ItemJnlLine2.VIN,
            ItemJnlLine2."Book No.",
            SalesLine."Branch Book No.",
            ItemJnlLine2.Amount);
        END;
      // Stop PA035473

      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE PostItemChargePerShpt@5807(SalesLine@1000 : Record 37);
    VAR
      SalesShptLine@1003 : Record 111;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF NOT SalesShptLine.GET(
         TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No.",TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No.")
      THEN
        ERROR(Text013);
      // Start PA031882
      // Stop PA031882
      SalesShptLine.TESTFIELD("Item Shpt. Entry No.");
      PostItemCharge(SalesLine,
        SalesShptLine."Item Shpt. Entry No.",SalesShptLine."Quantity (Base)",
        TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Amount to Assign",
        TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. to Assign");

      // Start PA035473
      IF SalesShptLine.VIN <> '' THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA035473
        InsertTempVehJnlLine(
          SalesLine,
          SalesLine."No.",
          SalesShptLine.VIN,SalesShptLine."Book No.",SalesShptLine."Branch Book No.",
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Amount to Assign",
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. to Assign",
          SalesShptLine."Item Shpt. Entry No.",
          ItemJnlLine."Applies-to Value Entry");
      // Start PA035473
        InsertTempSalIncVehJnlLine(
          SalesLine,
          SalesLine."No.",
          SalesShptLine.VIN,
          SalesShptLine."Book No.",
          SalesShptLine."Branch Book No.",
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Amount to Assign");
      END;
      // Stop PA035473

      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE PostItemChargePerRetRcpt@5810(SalesLine@1000 : Record 37);
    VAR
      ReturnRcptLine@1002 : Record 6661;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF NOT ReturnRcptLine.GET(
         TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No.",TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No.")

      // Start PA035473

      // Stop PA035473
        InsertTempVehJnlLine(
          SalesLine,
          SalesLine."No.",
          ReturnRcptLine.VIN,ReturnRcptLine."Book No.",ReturnRcptLine."Branch Book No.",
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Amount to Assign",
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. to Assign",
          ReturnRcptLine."Item Rcpt. Entry No.",
          ItemJnlLine."Applies-to Value Entry");
      // Start PA035473
        InsertTempSalIncVehJnlLine(
          SalesLine,
          SalesLine."No.",
          ReturnRcptLine.VIN,
          ReturnRcptLine."Book No.",
          ReturnRcptLine."Branch Book No.",
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Amount to Assign");
      END;
      // Stop PA035473
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE PostAssocItemJnlLine@3(QtyToBeShipped@1000 : Decimal;QtyToBeShippedBase@1001 : Decimal) : Integer;
    VAR
      ItemJnlPostLineL@1109400000 : Codeunit 22;
    BEGIN
      PurchOrderHeader.GET(
        PurchOrderHeader."Document Type"::Order,
        SalesLine."Purchase Order No.");
      PurchOrderLine.GET(
        PurchOrderLine."Document Type"::Order,
        SalesLine."Purchase Order No.",SalesLine."Purch. Order Line No.");

      ItemJnlLine.INIT;
      ItemJnlLine."Source Posting Group" := PurchOrderHeader."Vendor Posting Group";
      ItemJnlLine."Salespers./Purch. Code" := PurchOrderHeader."Purchaser Code";
      ItemJnlLine."Country Code" := PurchOrderHeader."VAT Country Code";
      ItemJnlLine."Reason Code" := PurchOrderHeader."Reason Code";
      ItemJnlLine."Posting No. Series" := PurchOrderHeader."Posting No. Series";
      ItemJnlLine."Item No." := PurchOrderLine."No.";
      ItemJnlLine.Description := PurchOrderLine.Description;
      ItemJnlLine."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := PurchOrderLine."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      ItemJnlLine."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := PurchOrderLine."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code";
      // Start PA035597
      ItemJnlLine."Dimension Set ID" := PurchOrderLine."Dimension Set ID";
      // Stop PA035597
      ItemJnlLine."Location Code" := PurchOrderLine."Location Code";
      ItemJnlLine."Inventory Posting Group" := PurchOrderLine."Posting Group";
      ItemJnlLine."Gen. Bus. Posting Group" := PurchOrderLine."Gen. Bus. Posting Group";
      ItemJnlLine."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" := PurchOrderLine."Gen. Prod. Posting Group";
      ItemJnlLine."Applies-to Entry" := PurchOrderLine."Appl.-to Item Entry";
      ItemJnlLine."Serial No." := PurchOrderLine."Serial No.";
      ItemJnlLine."Transaction Type" := PurchOrderLine."Transaction Type";
      ItemJnlLine."Transport Method" := PurchOrderLine."Transport Method";
      ItemJnlLine."Entry/Exit Point" := PurchOrderLine."Entry Point";
      ItemJnlLine.Area := PurchOrderLine.Area;
      ItemJnlLine."Transaction Specification" := PurchOrderLine."Transaction Specification";
      ItemJnlLine."Drop Shipment" := PurchOrderLine."Drop Shipment";
      ItemJnlLine."Posting Date" := SalesHeader."Posting Date";
      ItemJnlLine."Document Date" := SalesHeader."Document Date";
      ItemJnlLine."Entry Type" := ItemJnlLine."Entry Type"::Purchase;
      ItemJnlLine."Document No." := PurchOrderHeader."No.";
      ItemJnlLine."External Document No." := PurchOrderHeader."Receiving No.";
      ItemJnlLine.Quantity := QtyToBeShipped;
      ItemJnlLine."Quantity (Base)" := QtyToBeShippedBase;
      ItemJnlLine."Invoiced Quantity" := 0;
      ItemJnlLine."Invoiced Qty. (Base)" := 0;
      // Start PA036838
      ItemJnlLine."Document Line No." := PurchOrderLine."Line No.";
      IF  PurchOrderLine."Document Type" <>  PurchOrderLine."Document Type"::Invoice THEN
        ItemJnlLine."Order Line No." :=  PurchOrderLine."Line No."
      ELSE
        ItemJnlLine."Order Line No." :=  PurchOrderLine."Order Line No.";
      // Stop PA036838
      ItemJnlLine."Unit Cost" := PurchOrderLine."Unit Cost (LCY)";
      ItemJnlLine."Source Currency Code" := SalesHeader."Currency Code";
      ItemJnlLine."Source Currency Unit Cost" := PurchOrderLine."Unit Cost";
      ItemJnlLine."Source Type" := ItemJnlLine."Source Type"::Vendor;
      ItemJnlLine."Source No." := PurchOrderLine."Buy-from Vendor No.";
      // Start PA032441
      ItemJnlLine."Source Code" := SrcCode;
      // Stop PA032441
      ItemJnlLine."Variant Code" := PurchOrderLine."Variant Code";
      ItemJnlLine."Book No." := PurchOrderLine."Book No.";
      ItemJnlLine."Bin Code" := PurchOrderLine."Bin Code";
      ItemJnlLine."Prod. Order No." := PurchOrderLine."Prod. Order No.";
      ItemJnlLine."Unit of Measure Code" := PurchOrderLine."Unit of Measure Code";
      ItemJnlLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure" := PurchOrderLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure";
      ItemJnlLine."Applies-to Entry" := 0;
      ItemJnlLine.Reserve := PurchOrderLine.Reserve;
      ItemJnlLine."Branch Code" := CurrBranchCodeG;
      // Start PA035597
      // Stop PA035597
      // Start PA036549.33813
      ItemJnlPostLineL.RUN(ItemJnlLine);
      // Stop PA036549.33813
      EXIT(ItemJnlLine."Item Shpt. Entry No.");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateAssocOrder@4();
    BEGIN
      DropShipPostBuffer.RESET;
      // Start PA032441
      IF DropShipPostBuffer.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT;
      DropShipPostBuffer.FINDSET;
      // Stop PA032441
      REPEAT
        PurchOrderHeader.GET(
          PurchOrderHeader."Document Type"::Order,
          DropShipPostBuffer."Order No.");
        PurchOrderHeader."Last Receiving No." := PurchOrderHeader."Receiving No.";
        PurchOrderHeader."Receiving No." := '';
        PurchOrderHeader.MODIFY;
        DropShipPostBuffer.SETRANGE("Order No.",DropShipPostBuffer."Order No.");
        REPEAT
          PurchOrderLine.GET(
            PurchOrderLine."Document Type"::Order,
            DropShipPostBuffer."Order No.",DropShipPostBuffer."Order Line No.");
          PurchOrderLine."Quantity Received" := PurchOrderLine."Quantity Received" + DropShipPostBuffer.Quantity;
          PurchOrderLine."Qty. Received (Base)" := PurchOrderLine."Qty. Received (Base)" + DropShipPostBuffer."Quantity (Base)";
          PurchOrderLine.InitOutstanding;
          PurchOrderLine.InitQtyToReceive;
          PurchOrderLine.MODIFY;
        UNTIL DropShipPostBuffer.NEXT = 0;
        PurchOrderHeader.UpdateStatus;
        PurchOrderHeader.MODIFY;
        DropShipPostBuffer.SETRANGE("Order No.");
      UNTIL DropShipPostBuffer.NEXT = 0;
      DropShipPostBuffer.DELETEALL;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateAssocLines@5(VAR SalesOrderLine@1000 : Record 37);
    BEGIN
      PurchOrderLine.GET(
        PurchOrderLine."Document Type"::Order,
        SalesOrderLine."Purchase Order No.",SalesOrderLine."Purch. Order Line No.");
      PurchOrderLine."Sales Order No." := '';
      PurchOrderLine."Sales Order Line No." := 0;
      PurchOrderLine.MODIFY;
      SalesOrderLine."Purchase Order No." := '';
      SalesOrderLine."Purch. Order Line No." := 0;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdInvPostingBuffer@6();
    VAR
      TempDimBuf@1000 : TEMPORARY Record 360;
      EntryNo@1001 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA032441
      // Start PA035597
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."Dimension Set ID" := SalesLine."Dimension Set ID";

      DimMgt.UpdateGlobalDimFromDimSetID(InvPostingBuffer[1]."Dimension Set ID",
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Global Dimension 1 Code",InvPostingBuffer[1]."Global Dimension 2 Code");
      // Stop PA035597
      IF InvPostingBuffer[1].Type = InvPostingBuffer[1].Type::"Fixed Asset" THEN BEGIN
        FALineNo := FALineNo + 1;
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Fixed Asset Line No." := FALineNo;
      END;
      // Stop PA032441
      InvPostingBuffer[1].FillCombinedKey;
      InvPostingBuffer[2] := InvPostingBuffer[1];
      IF InvPostingBuffer[2].FIND THEN BEGIN
        InvPostingBuffer[2].Amount := InvPostingBuffer[2].Amount + InvPostingBuffer[1].Amount;
        InvPostingBuffer[2]."VAT Amount" :=
          InvPostingBuffer[2]."VAT Amount" + InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Amount";
      // Start PA032441
      // Stop PA032441
        InvPostingBuffer[2]."VAT Base Amount" :=
          InvPostingBuffer[2]."VAT Base Amount" + InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Base Amount";
      // Start PA032441
        InvPostingBuffer[2]."Amount (ACY)" :=
          InvPostingBuffer[2]."Amount (ACY)" + InvPostingBuffer[1]."Amount (ACY)";
        InvPostingBuffer[2]."VAT Amount (ACY)" :=
          InvPostingBuffer[2]."VAT Amount (ACY)" + InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Amount (ACY)";
        InvPostingBuffer[2]."VAT Base Amount (ACY)" :=
          InvPostingBuffer[2]."VAT Base Amount (ACY)" +
          InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Base Amount (ACY)";
      // Stop PA032441
      // Start EU.0104306
        InvPostingBuffer[2]."VAT Difference" := InvPostingBuffer[2]."VAT Difference" + InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Difference";
      // Stop EU.0104306
        InvPostingBuffer[2].Quantity :=
          InvPostingBuffer[2].Quantity + InvPostingBuffer[1].Quantity;
        IF NOT InvPostingBuffer[1]."System-Created Entry" THEN
          InvPostingBuffer[2]."System-Created Entry" := FALSE;
        InvPostingBuffer[2]."Exch. Parts Tax Base" :=
          InvPostingBuffer[2]."Exch. Parts Tax Base" + InvPostingBuffer[1]."Exch. Parts Tax Base";
        InvPostingBuffer[2]."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" :=
          InvPostingBuffer[2]."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" + InvPostingBuffer[1]."Exch. Parts Tax Amount";
        InvPostingBuffer[2]."Orig. Exch. Parts VAT Tax Base" :=
          InvPostingBuffer[2]."Orig. Exch. Parts VAT Tax Base" + InvPostingBuffer[1]."Orig. Exch. Parts VAT Tax Base";
        InvPostingBuffer[2]."Orig. Exch. Parts VAT Amount" :=
          InvPostingBuffer[2]."Orig. Exch. Parts VAT Amount" + InvPostingBuffer[1]."Orig. Exch. Parts VAT Amount";

        InvPostingBuffer[2].MODIFY;
      END ELSE
        InvPostingBuffer[1].INSERT;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE PostDiscount@7(GLAccNo@1109400000 : Code[20];DiscountAmount@1109400001 : Decimal;SrcCurrDiscountAmount@1109400002 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      WITH GenJnlLine DO BEGIN
        "Gen. Posting Type" := 0; // None
        "Gen. Bus. Posting Group" := '';
        "Gen. Prod. Posting Group" := '';
        "VAT Bus. Posting Group" := '';
        "VAT Prod. Posting Group" := '';
        "EU 3-Party Trade" := FALSE;
        "VAT Calculation Type" := "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT";
        "Sell-to/Buy-from No." := '';
        "VAT Amount" := 0;
        "Account No." := GLAccNo;
        Amount := -DiscountAmount;
        "Amount (LCY)" := 0;
        "Source Currency Code" := SalesHeader."Currency Code";
        "Source Currency Amount" := -SrcCurrDiscountAmount;
        "Source Curr. VAT Amount" := 0;
        "System-Created Entry" := TRUE;
        "Branch Code" := CurrBranchCodeG;
        GenJnlPostLine.RUN(GenJnlLine);
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetCurrency@17();
    BEGIN
      WITH SalesHeader DO
        IF "Currency Code" = '' THEN
          Currency.InitRoundingPrecision
        ELSE BEGIN
          Currency.GET("Currency Code");
          Currency.TESTFIELD("Amount Rounding Precision");
        END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DivideAmount@8(SalesLineQty@1001 : Decimal;VAR SalesLineP@14535500 : Record 37);
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0145355.145511
      WITH SalesLineP DO BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0145355.145511
        Amount := Amount * SalesLineQty / Quantity;
        "VAT Base Amount" := "VAT Base Amount" * SalesLineQty / Quantity;
        "Exch. Parts Tax Base" := "Exch. Parts Tax Base" * SalesLineQty / Quantity;
        "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" := "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" * SalesLineQty / Quantity;
        IF ("VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax") AND
           (Quantity <> "Qty. to Invoice")
      // Start PA032441
      // Stop PA032441
        THEN
          "Amount Including VAT" :=
            Amount +
            SalesTaxCalculateG.CalculateTax(
              "Tax Area Code","Tax Group Code","Tax Liable",
              SalesHeader."Posting Date","VAT Base Amount",SalesLineQty,SalesHeader."Currency Factor")
        ELSE
          "Amount Including VAT" := "Amount Including VAT" * SalesLineQty / Quantity;
        "Line Discount Amount" := "Line Discount Amount" * SalesLineQty / Quantity;
        "Inv. Discount Amount" := "Inv. Discount Amount" * SalesLineQty / Quantity;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE RoundAmount@9(SalesLineQty@1000 : Decimal;VAR GlobTotalSalesLineP@10430606 : Record 37;VAR GlobTotalSalesLineLCYP@10430605 : Record 37);
    VAR
      NoVAT@1001 : Boolean;
      "__ INCADEA __"@10430601 : Integer;
      OrgTotalSalesLine@10430603 : Record 37;
      TotalSalesLine@10430602 : Record 37;
      TotalSalesLineLCY@10430600 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function uses the OrgTotalSalesLine, TotalSalesLine and TotalSalesLineLCY variable locally!
      // @ The content of these variables are separated by VAT %.
      // @ param GlobTotalSalesLineP = Global instance of TotalSalesLine
      // @ param GlobTotalSalesLineLCYP = Global instance of TotalSalesLineLCY
      // Start EU.0104306
      WITH SalesLine DO BEGIN
        IF RoundingLineInserted THEN BEGIN
          OrgTotalSalesLine := GlobTotalSalesLineP;
          TotalSalesLine := GlobTotalSalesLineP;
          TotalSalesLineLCY := GlobTotalSalesLineLCYP;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          GetTotalSalesLineByVAT(SalesLine, OrgTotalSalesLine, 10000);
          GetTotalSalesLineByVAT(SalesLine, TotalSalesLine, 20000);
          GetTotalSalesLineByVAT(SalesLine, TotalSalesLineLCY, 30000);
        END;
        // EnhancedAmountRounding function replaces original Incadea function RoundAmount
        IF GLSetup.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(SalesHeader."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN BEGIN
          EnhancedAmountRounding(GlobTotalSalesLineP, SalesLineQty, OrgTotalSalesLine, TotalSalesLine, TotalSalesLineLCY);
        END ELSE BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0104306
      // Start PA040837
          IncrAmount(OrgTotalSalesLine, TRUE);
      // Stop PA040837
          NoVAT := Amount = "Amount Including VAT";
          "Amount Including VAT" :=
            ROUND(OrgTotalSalesLine."Amount Including VAT",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
            TotalSalesLine."Amount Including VAT";
      // Start INC
          IF NoVAT AND ("VAT Base Amount" <> 0) AND
             ("VAT Calculation Type" <> SalesLine."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax")
          THEN BEGIN
      // Stop INC
            Amount := "Amount Including VAT";
            "VAT Base Amount" := "Amount Including VAT";
          END ELSE BEGIN
            Amount :=
              ROUND(OrgTotalSalesLine.Amount,Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
              TotalSalesLine.Amount;
            "VAT Base Amount" :=
              ROUND(OrgTotalSalesLine."VAT Base Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
              TotalSalesLine."VAT Base Amount";
          END;
          "Line Discount Amount" :=
            ROUND(OrgTotalSalesLine."Line Discount Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
            TotalSalesLine."Line Discount Amount";
          "Inv. Discount Amount" :=
            ROUND(OrgTotalSalesLine."Inv. Discount Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
            TotalSalesLine."Inv. Discount Amount";
          "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" :=
            ROUND(OrgTotalSalesLine."Exch. Parts Tax Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
            TotalSalesLine."Exch. Parts Tax Amount";
          "Exch. Parts Tax Base" :=
            ROUND(OrgTotalSalesLine."Exch. Parts Tax Base",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
            TotalSalesLine."Exch. Parts Tax Base";
          IncrAmount(TotalSalesLine, FALSE);
      // Start PA040837
      // Start EU.0104306
          IncrAmount(GlobTotalSalesLineP, FALSE);
      // Stop PA040837
          Increment(GlobTotalSalesLineP."Net Weight",ROUND(SalesLineQty * "Net Weight",0.00001));
          Increment(GlobTotalSalesLineP."Gross Weight",ROUND(SalesLineQty * "Gross Weight",0.00001));
          Increment(GlobTotalSalesLineP."Unit Volume",ROUND(SalesLineQty * "Unit Volume",0.00001));
          Increment(GlobTotalSalesLineP.Quantity,SalesLineQty);
          IF "Units per Parcel" > 0 THEN
            Increment(
              GlobTotalSalesLineP."Units per Parcel",
      // Stop EU.0104306
              ROUND(SalesLineQty / "Units per Parcel",1,'>'));

          TempSalesLine := SalesLine;
          SrcCurrSalesLine := SalesLine;

          IF SalesHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
            IF SalesHeader."Document Type" = SalesHeader."Document Type"::Quote THEN
              UseDate := WORKDATE
            ELSE
              UseDate := SalesHeader."Posting Date";
            NoVAT := Amount = "Amount Including VAT";
            "Amount Including VAT" :=
              ROUND(
                CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                  UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                  TotalSalesLine."Amount Including VAT",SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                  TotalSalesLineLCY."Amount Including VAT";
            IF NoVAT THEN
              Amount := "Amount Including VAT"
            ELSE
              Amount :=
                ROUND(
                  CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                    UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                    TotalSalesLine.Amount,SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                    TotalSalesLineLCY.Amount;
            "Line Discount Amount" :=
              ROUND(
                CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                  UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                  TotalSalesLine."Line Discount Amount",SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                  TotalSalesLineLCY."Line Discount Amount";
            "Inv. Discount Amount" :=
              ROUND(
                CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                  UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                  TotalSalesLine."Inv. Discount Amount",SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                  TotalSalesLineLCY."Inv. Discount Amount";
            "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" :=
              ROUND(
                CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                  UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                  TotalSalesLine."Exch. Parts Tax Amount",SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                  TotalSalesLineLCY."Exch. Parts Tax Amount";
            "Exch. Parts Tax Base" :=
              ROUND(
                CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                  UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                  TotalSalesLine."Exch. Parts Tax Base",SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                  TotalSalesLineLCY."Exch. Parts Tax Base";
          END;
      // Start EU.0104306
        END;
        IncrAmount(TotalSalesLineLCY, FALSE);
      // Start PA040837
        IncrAmount(GlobTotalSalesLineLCYP, FALSE);
      // Stop PA040837
        Increment(GlobTotalSalesLineLCYP."Unit Cost (LCY)",ROUND(SalesLineQty * "Unit Cost (LCY)"));
      END;
      IF NOT RoundingLineInserted THEN BEGIN
        SetTotalSalesLineByVAT(OrgTotalSalesLine);
        SetTotalSalesLineByVAT(TotalSalesLine);
        SetTotalSalesLineByVAT(TotalSalesLineLCY);
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ReverseAmount@10(VAR SalesLine@1000 : Record 37);
    BEGIN
      WITH SalesLine DO BEGIN
        "Qty. to Ship" := -"Qty. to Ship";
        "Qty. to Ship (Base)" := -"Qty. to Ship (Base)";
      // Start INC
        "Return Qty. to Receive" := -"Return Qty. to Receive";
        "Return Qty. to Receive (Base)" := -"Return Qty. to Receive (Base)";
      // Stop INC
        "Qty. to Invoice" := -"Qty. to Invoice";
        "Qty. to Invoice (Base)" := -"Qty. to Invoice (Base)";
        Amount := -Amount;
        "VAT Base Amount" := -"VAT Base Amount";
        "Amount Including VAT" := -"Amount Including VAT";
        "Line Discount Amount" := -"Line Discount Amount";
        "Inv. Discount Amount" := -"Inv. Discount Amount";
      // Start EU.0104306
        "Original Amount" := -"Original Amount";
        "Original Amount Incl. VAT" := -"Original Amount Incl. VAT";
        "VAT Difference Amount" := -"VAT Difference Amount";
      // Stop EU.0104306
        "Exch. Parts Tax Base" := -"Exch. Parts Tax Base";
        "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" := -"Exch. Parts Tax Amount";
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InvoiceRounding@12(UseTempData@1000 : Boolean;BiggestLineNo@1004 : Integer);
    VAR
      InvoiceRoundingAmount@1001 : Decimal;
      SalesLineL@1109400000 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA032441
      Currency.TESTFIELD("Invoice Rounding Precision");
      // Stop PA032441
      InvoiceRoundingAmount :=
        -ROUND(
          TotalSalesLine."Amount Including VAT" -
          ROUND(
            TotalSalesLine."Amount Including VAT",
            Currency."Invoice Rounding Precision",
      // Start PA032441
            Currency.InvoiceRoundingDirection),
      // Stop PA032441
            Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");

      // Start PA036544
      ExitPointParamG."Decimal 1" := InvoiceRoundingAmount;
      EPRecRef2G.GETTABLE(Currency);
      SalesLineExitPoint(TotalSalesLine,ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1",'');
      InvoiceRoundingAmount := ExitPointParamG."Decimal 1";
      // Stop PA036544

      IF InvoiceRoundingAmount <> 0 THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA032651
        IF SalesHeader."Customer Posting Group" = '' THEN BEGIN
          CustSetupG.GET();
          CustPostingGr.GET(CustSetupG."Customer Posting Group")
        END ELSE
      // Stop PA032651
          CustPostingGr.GET(SalesHeader."Customer Posting Group");
        CustPostingGr.TESTFIELD("Invoice Rounding Account");
      // Start PA037802.37581
        SalesLineL := SalesLine;
      // Stop PA037802.37581
      // Start PA032441
        WITH SalesLine DO BEGIN
      // Stop PA032441
          INIT;
      // Start PA042077
      // Start PA045261
          BiggestLineNo := BiggestLineNo + 10000;
      // Stop PA045261
      // Stop PA042077
          "Line No." := 0;
          "System-Created Entry" := TRUE;
      // Start PA032441
          IF UseTempData THEN BEGIN
            "Line No." := 0;
            Type := Type::"Account (G/L)";
      // Start PA037802.37581
            StatusUpdateSet(UseTempData);
            DefNotToOption(UseTempData);
            SalesLine.SkipDimensionUpdate(UseTempData);
      // Stop PA037802.37581
          END ELSE BEGIN
      // Start PA045261
            "Line No." := BiggestLineNo;
      // Stop PA045261
            VALIDATE(Type,Type::"Account (G/L)");
          END;
      // Stop PA032441
      // Start PA037802.37581
      // Start PA039974
          "Order Type" := SalesHeader."Order Type";
          "Vehicle Status" := SalesLineL."Vehicle Status";
          "Currency Rounding Position" := TRUE;
      // Stop PA039974
      // Stop PA037802.37581
          VALIDATE("No.",CustPostingGr."Invoice Rounding Account");
          VALIDATE(Quantity,1);
      // Start PA032441
          IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
            VALIDATE("Return Qty. to Receive",Quantity)
          ELSE
            VALIDATE("Qty. to Ship",Quantity);
          IF SalesHeader."Prices Including VAT" THEN
            VALIDATE("Unit Price",InvoiceRoundingAmount)
          ELSE
      // Stop PA032441
            VALIDATE(
              "Unit Price",
              ROUND(
                InvoiceRoundingAmount /
                (1 + (1 - SalesHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100) * "VAT %" / 100),
                Currency."Amount Rounding Precision"));
      // Start PA032441
          VALIDATE("Amount Including VAT",InvoiceRoundingAmount);
      // Stop PA032441
      // Start PA045261
          "Line No." := BiggestLineNo;
      // Stop PA045261
      // Start PA035597
      // Stop PA035597
      // Start PA032441
          LastLineRetrieved := FALSE;
          RoundingLineInserted := TRUE;
      // Start PA032441
          RoundingLineNo := "Line No.";
      // Stop PA032441
        END;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE IncrAmount@13(VAR TotalSalesLine@1000 : Record 37;UseRoundedAmountInclVATP@1109400001 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF SalesLineExitPoint(SalesLine, ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'IncrAmount') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544

      WITH SalesLine DO BEGIN
      // Start PA033995.I000900
      // Start PA033352
        Increment(TotalSalesLine.Amount,Amount);
        Increment(TotalSalesLine."VAT Base Amount","VAT Base Amount");
      // Start PA040837
        IF NOT UseRoundedAmountInclVATP THEN
          Increment(TotalSalesLine."Amount Including VAT","Amount Including VAT")
        ELSE
          Increment(TotalSalesLine."Amount Including VAT", CalcVATAmountUnrounded(SalesLine));
      // Stop PA040837
        Increment(TotalSalesLine."Line Discount Amount","Line Discount Amount");
        Increment(TotalSalesLine."Inv. Discount Amount","Inv. Discount Amount");
      // Start PA042968
        IF NOT UseRoundedAmountInclVATP THEN BEGIN
          Increment(TotalSalesLine."Exch. Parts Tax Base","Exch. Parts Tax Base");
          Increment(TotalSalesLine."Exch. Parts Tax Amount","Exch. Parts Tax Amount");
        END ELSE BEGIN
          Increment(TotalSalesLine."Exch. Parts Tax Base", CalcOriginalAmount(SalesLine) * "Exch. Parts Tax %" / 100);
          Increment(TotalSalesLine."Exch. Parts Tax Amount", "Exch. Parts Tax Base" * "Exch. Parts VAT %" / 100);
        END;
      // Stop PA042968
      // Stop PA033352
      // Stop PA033995.I000900
      END;

      // Start PA036544
      SalesLineExitPoint(SalesLine,ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'IncrAmount');
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE Increment@14(VAR Number@1000 : Decimal;Number2@1001 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      Number := Number + Number2;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetSalesLines@16(VAR NewSalesHeader@1000 : Record 36;VAR NewSalesLine@1001 : Record 37;QtyType@1002 : 'General,Invoicing,Shipping');
    VAR
      OldSalesLine@1003 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      SalesHeader := NewSalesHeader;
      SumSalesLines2(NewSalesLine,OldSalesLine,QtyType,TRUE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetSalesLinesTemp@33(VAR NewSalesHeader@1000 : Record 36;VAR NewSalesLine@1001 : Record 37;VAR OldSalesLine@1002 : Record 37;QtyType@1003 : 'General,Invoicing,Shipping');
    BEGIN
      SalesHeader := NewSalesHeader;
      OldSalesLine.SetSalesHeader(NewSalesHeader);
      SumSalesLines2(NewSalesLine,OldSalesLine,QtyType,TRUE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE SumSalesLines@15(VAR NewSalesHeader@1000 : Record 36;QtyType@1001 : 'General,Invoicing,Shipping';VAR NewTotalSalesLine@1002 : Record 37;VAR NewTotalSalesLineLCY@1003 : Record 37;VAR VATAmount@1004 : Decimal;VAR VATAmountText@1005 : Text[30];VAR ProfitLCY@1006 : Decimal;VAR ProfitPct@1007 : Decimal;VAR ExchPartTaxP@1109400008 : Decimal);
    VAR
      OldSalesLine@1008 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      IF (NewTotalSalesLine.GETFILTERS <> '') THEN BEGIN
        OldSalesLine.COPYFILTERS(NewTotalSalesLine);
        NewTotalSalesLine.RESET;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
      SumSalesLinesTemp(
        NewSalesHeader,OldSalesLine,QtyType,NewTotalSalesLine,NewTotalSalesLineLCY,
        VATAmount,VATAmountText,ProfitLCY,ProfitPct,ExchPartTaxP);
    END;

    PROCEDURE SumSalesLinesTemp@25(VAR NewSalesHeader@1000 : Record 36;VAR OldSalesLine@1001 : Record 37;QtyType@1002 : 'General,Invoicing,Shipping';VAR NewTotalSalesLine@1003 : Record 37;VAR NewTotalSalesLineLCY@1004 : Record 37;VAR VATAmount@1005 : Decimal;VAR VATAmountText@1006 : Text[30];VAR ProfitLCY@1007 : Decimal;VAR ProfitPct@1008 : Decimal;VAR ExchPartTaxP@1109400009 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      WITH SalesHeader DO BEGIN
        SalesHeader := NewSalesHeader;
        SumSalesLines2(SalesLine,OldSalesLine,QtyType,FALSE);
      // Start EU.0104306
        IF GLSetup.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(SalesHeader."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0145355.145511
          TotalSalesLine.Amount := SalesBillVATCalculation(QtyType, SalesHeader,VATDistributionBufferG[1],Currency."Amount Rounding Precision",FALSE,TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0145355.145511
          TotalSalesLineLCY.Amount := TotalSalesLine.Amount;
        END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
        ProfitLCY := TotalSalesLineLCY.Amount - TotalSalesLineLCY."Unit Cost (LCY)";
        IF TotalSalesLineLCY.Amount = 0 THEN
          ProfitPct := 0
        ELSE
          ProfitPct := ROUND(ProfitLCY / TotalSalesLineLCY.Amount * 100,0.1);
        VATAmount := TotalSalesLine."Amount Including VAT" - TotalSalesLine.Amount;
        ExchPartTaxP := TotalSalesLine."Exch. Parts Tax Amount";
        IF TotalSalesLine."VAT %" = 0 THEN
      // Start PA032441
          VATAmountText := Text016
      // Stop PA032441
        ELSE
      // Start PA032441
          VATAmountText := STRSUBSTNO(Text017,TotalSalesLine."VAT %");
      // Stop PA032441
        NewTotalSalesLine := TotalSalesLine;
        NewTotalSalesLineLCY := TotalSalesLineLCY;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SumSalesLines2@11(VAR NewSalesLine@1000 : Record 37;VAR OldSalesLine@1001 : Record 37;QtyType@1002 : 'General,Invoicing,Shipping';InsertSalesLine@1003 : Boolean);
    VAR
      SalesLineQty@1004 : Decimal;
      BiggestLineNo@1005 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      WITH SalesHeader DO BEGIN
        GetGLSetup;
        SalesSetup.GET;
        GetCurrency;
      // Start EU.0104306
        VATDistributionBufferG[1].DELETEALL;
      // Stop EU.0104306
        OldSalesLine.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        OldSalesLine.SETRANGE("Document No.","No.");
        RoundingLineInserted := FALSE;
      // Start PA032990
        IF OldSalesLine.FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA032990
          REPEAT
            IF NOT RoundingLineInserted THEN
              SalesLine := OldSalesLine;
            CASE QtyType OF
              QtyType::General:
                SalesLineQty := SalesLine.Quantity;
              QtyType::Invoicing:
                SalesLineQty := SalesLine."Qty. to Invoice";
              QtyType::Shipping:
      // Start INC
                BEGIN
                  IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
                    SalesLineQty := SalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive"
                  ELSE
                    SalesLineQty := SalesLine."Qty. to Ship";
                END;
      // Stop INC
            END;
            IF SalesLineQty <> 0 THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0145355.145511
              DivideAmount(SalesLineQty, SalesLine);
      // Stop EU.0145355.145511
              IF (SalesLine.Amount <> 0) AND NOT RoundingLineInserted THEN
                IF TotalSalesLine.Amount = 0 THEN
                  TotalSalesLine."VAT %" := SalesLine."VAT %"
                ELSE
                  IF TotalSalesLine."VAT %" <> SalesLine."VAT %" THEN
                    TotalSalesLine."VAT %" := 0;
      // Start EU.0104306
              RoundAmount(SalesLineQty, TotalSalesLine, TotalSalesLineLCY);
      // Stop EU.0104306
              SalesLine := TempSalesLine;
            END;
            IF InsertSalesLine THEN BEGIN
              NewSalesLine := SalesLine;
              NewSalesLine.INSERT;
            END;
            IF RoundingLineInserted THEN
              LastLineRetrieved := TRUE
            ELSE BEGIN
      // Start PA045261
              BiggestLineNo := MAX(BiggestLineNo,OldSalesLine."Line No.");
      // Start EU.0104306
              LastLineRetrieved := GetNextSalesline(OldSalesLine);
      // Stop EU.0104306
              IF LastLineRetrieved AND SalesSetup."Invoice Rounding" THEN
      // Start PA032441
                InvoiceRounding(TRUE,BiggestLineNo);
      // Stop PA032441
      // Stop PA045261
            END;
          UNTIL LastLineRetrieved;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE TestDeleteHeader@19(SalesHeader@1000 : Record 36;VAR SalesShptHeader@1001 : Record 110;VAR SalesInvHeader@1002 : Record 112;VAR SalesCrMemoHeader@1003 : Record 114;VAR ReturnRcptHeader@1004 : Record 6660);
    BEGIN
      WITH SalesHeader DO BEGIN
        CLEAR(SalesShptHeader);
        CLEAR(SalesInvHeader);
        CLEAR(SalesCrMemoHeader);
        CLEAR(ReturnRcptHeader);
        SalesSetup.GET;

        SourceCodeSetup.GET;
        SourceCodeSetup.TESTFIELD("Deleted Document");
        SourceCode.GET(SourceCodeSetup."Deleted Document");

        IF ("Shipping No. Series" <> '') AND ("Shipping No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
          SalesShptHeader.TRANSFERFIELDS(SalesHeader);
          SalesShptHeader."No." := "Shipping No.";
          SalesShptHeader."Posting Date" := TODAY;
          SalesShptHeader."User ID" := USERID;
          SalesShptHeader."Source Code" := SourceCode.Code;
        END;

      // Start INC
        IF ("Return Receipt No. Series" <> '') AND ("Return Receipt No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
          ReturnRcptHeader.TRANSFERFIELDS(SalesHeader);
          ReturnRcptHeader."No." := "Return Receipt No.";
          ReturnRcptHeader."Posting Date" := TODAY;
          ReturnRcptHeader."User ID" := USERID;
          ReturnRcptHeader."Source Code" := SourceCode.Code;
        END;
      // Stop INC

        IF ("Posting No. Series" <> '') AND
           (("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Order,"Document Type"::Invoice]) AND
            ("Posting No." <> '') OR
            ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice) AND
            ("No. Series" = "Posting No. Series"))
        THEN BEGIN
          SalesInvHeader.TRANSFERFIELDS(SalesHeader);
          IF "Posting No." <> '' THEN
            SalesInvHeader."No." := "Posting No.";
          IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice THEN BEGIN
            SalesInvHeader."Pre-Assigned No. Series" := "No. Series";
            SalesInvHeader."Pre-Assigned No." := "No.";
          END ELSE BEGIN
            SalesInvHeader."Pre-Assigned No. Series" := '';
            SalesInvHeader."Pre-Assigned No." := '';
            SalesInvHeader."Order No. Series" := "No. Series";
            SalesInvHeader."Order No." := "No.";
          END;
          SalesInvHeader."Posting Date" := TODAY;
          SalesInvHeader."User ID" := USERID;
          SalesInvHeader."Source Code" := SourceCode.Code;
        END;

      // Start INC
        IF ("Posting No. Series" <> '') AND
           (("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]) AND
            ("Posting No." <> '') OR
            ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo") AND
            ("No. Series" = "Posting No. Series"))
      // Stop INC
        THEN BEGIN
          SalesCrMemoHeader.TRANSFERFIELDS(SalesHeader);
          IF "Posting No." <> '' THEN
            SalesCrMemoHeader."No." := "Posting No.";
          SalesCrMemoHeader."Pre-Assigned No. Series" := "No. Series";
          SalesCrMemoHeader."Pre-Assigned No." := "No.";
          SalesCrMemoHeader."Posting Date" := TODAY;
          SalesCrMemoHeader."User ID" := USERID;
          SalesCrMemoHeader."Source Code" := SourceCode.Code;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeleteHeader@18(SalesHeader@1000 : Record 36;VAR SalesShptHeader@1001 : Record 110;VAR SalesInvHeader@1002 : Record 112;VAR SalesCrMemoHeader@1003 : Record 114;VAR ReturnRcptHeader@1004 : Record 6660);
    BEGIN
      WITH SalesHeader DO BEGIN
        TestDeleteHeader(SalesHeader,SalesShptHeader,SalesInvHeader,SalesCrMemoHeader,ReturnRcptHeader);
        IF SalesShptHeader."No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
          SalesShptHeader."Completely Invoiced" := TRUE;
          SalesShptHeader.INSERT;
          SalesShptLine.INIT;
          SalesShptLine."Document No." := SalesShptHeader."No.";
          SalesShptLine."Line No." := 10000;
          SalesShptLine.Description := SourceCode.Description;
      // Start PA032990
          SalesShptLine."Order Type" := SalesShptHeader."Order Type";
      // Stop PA032990

          SalesShptLine.INSERT;
        END;

      // Start INC
        IF ReturnRcptHeader."No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
          ReturnRcptHeader.INSERT;
          ReturnRcptLine.INIT;
          ReturnRcptLine."Document No." := ReturnRcptHeader."No.";
          ReturnRcptLine."Line No." := 10000;
          ReturnRcptLine.Description := SourceCode.Description;
      // Start PA032990
          ReturnRcptLine."Order Type" := ReturnRcptHeader."Order Type";
      // Stop PA032990
          ReturnRcptLine.INSERT;
        END;
      // Stop INC

        IF SalesInvHeader."No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
          SalesInvHeader.INSERT;
          SalesInvLine.INIT;
          SalesInvLine."Document No." := SalesInvHeader."No.";
          SalesInvLine."Line No." := 10000;
          SalesInvLine.Description := SourceCode.Description;
      // Start PA032990
          SalesInvLine."Order Type" := SalesInvHeader."Order Type";
      // Stop PA032990
          SalesInvLine.INSERT;
        END;

        IF SalesCrMemoHeader."No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
          SalesCrMemoHeader.INSERT;
          SalesCrMemoLine.INIT;
          SalesCrMemoLine."Document No." := SalesCrMemoHeader."No.";
          SalesCrMemoLine."Line No." := 10000;
          SalesCrMemoLine.Description := SourceCode.Description;
      // Start PA032990
          SalesCrMemoLine."Order Type" := SalesCrMemoHeader."Order Type";
      // Stop PA032990
          SalesCrMemoLine.INSERT;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateBlanketOrderLine@21(SalesLine@1000 : Record 37;Ship@1001 : Boolean;Receive@1006 : Boolean;Invoice@1002 : Boolean);
    VAR
      BlanketOrderSalesLine@1003 : Record 37;
      ModifyLine@1004 : Boolean;
      Sign@1005 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF (SalesLine."Blanket Order No." <> '') AND (SalesLine."Blanket Order Line No." <> 0) AND
         ((Ship AND (SalesLine."Qty. to Ship" <> 0)) OR
      // Start INC
          (Receive AND (SalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive" <> 0)) OR
      // Stop INC
          (Invoice AND (SalesLine."Qty. to Invoice" <> 0)))
      THEN
        IF BlanketOrderSalesLine.GET(
           BlanketOrderSalesLine."Document Type"::"Blanket Order",SalesLine."Blanket Order No.",
           SalesLine."Blanket Order Line No.")
        THEN BEGIN
          BlanketOrderSalesLine.TESTFIELD(Type,SalesLine.Type);
          BlanketOrderSalesLine.TESTFIELD("No.",SalesLine."No.");
          BlanketOrderSalesLine.TESTFIELD("Sell-to Customer No.",SalesLine."Sell-to Customer No.");

          ModifyLine := FALSE;
          CASE SalesLine."Document Type" OF
            SalesLine."Document Type"::Order,
            SalesLine."Document Type"::Invoice:
              Sign := 1;
      // Start INC
            SalesLine."Document Type"::"Return Order",
      // Stop INC
            SalesLine."Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
              Sign := -1;
          END;
          IF Ship THEN BEGIN
            IF BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure" =
               SalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure"
            THEN
              BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Shipped" :=
                BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Shipped" + Sign * SalesLine."Qty. to Ship"
            ELSE
              BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Shipped" :=
                BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Shipped" +
                Sign *
                ROUND(
                  (SalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure" /
                   BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure") *
                  SalesLine."Qty. to Ship",0.00001);
            BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. Shipped (Base)" :=
              BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. Shipped (Base)" + Sign * SalesLine."Qty. to Ship (Base)";
            ModifyLine := TRUE;
          END;
      // Start INC
          IF Receive THEN BEGIN
            IF BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure" =
               SalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure"
            THEN
              BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Shipped" :=
                BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Shipped" + Sign * SalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive"
            ELSE
              BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Shipped" :=
                BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Shipped" +
                Sign *
                ROUND(
                  (SalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure" /
                   BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure") *
                  SalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive",0.00001);
            BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. Shipped (Base)" :=
              BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. Shipped (Base)" + Sign * SalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive (Base)";
            ModifyLine := TRUE;
          END;
      // Stop INC
          IF Invoice THEN BEGIN
            IF BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure" =
               SalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure"
            THEN
              BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Invoiced" :=
                BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Invoiced" + Sign * SalesLine."Qty. to Invoice"
            ELSE
              BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Invoiced" :=
                BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Invoiced" +
                Sign *
                ROUND(
                  (SalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure" /
                   BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. per Unit of Measure") *
                  SalesLine."Qty. to Invoice",0.00001);
            BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. Invoiced (Base)" :=
              BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. Invoiced (Base)" + Sign * SalesLine."Qty. to Invoice (Base)";
            ModifyLine := TRUE;
          END;

          IF ModifyLine THEN BEGIN
            BlanketOrderSalesLine.InitOutstanding;
            IF (BlanketOrderSalesLine.Quantity * BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Shipped" < 0) OR
               (ABS(BlanketOrderSalesLine.Quantity) < ABS(BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity Shipped"))
            THEN
              BlanketOrderSalesLine.FIELDERROR(
                "Quantity Shipped",STRSUBSTNO(
                  Text018,
                  BlanketOrderSalesLine.FIELDCAPTION(Quantity)));

            IF (BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity (Base)" *
                BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. Shipped (Base)" < 0) OR
               (ABS(BlanketOrderSalesLine."Quantity (Base)") <
                ABS(BlanketOrderSalesLine."Qty. Shipped (Base)"))
            THEN
              BlanketOrderSalesLine.FIELDERROR(
                "Qty. Shipped (Base)",
                STRSUBSTNO(
                  Text018,
                  BlanketOrderSalesLine.FIELDCAPTION("Quantity (Base)")));

            IF ABS(BlanketOrderSalesLine."Outstanding Qty. (Base)") <
               ABS(BlanketOrderSalesLine."Reserved Qty. (Base)")
            THEN
              BlanketOrderSalesLine.FIELDERROR(
                "Reserved Qty. (Base)",
                Text019);
      // Start PA035134
            UpdateTempBlanketOrder(BlanketOrderSalesLine);
      // Stop PA035134
            BlanketOrderSalesLine.MODIFY;
          END;
        END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CopyCommentLines@22(FromDocumentType@1000 : Integer;ToDocumentType@1001 : Integer;FromNumber@1002 : Code[20];ToNumber@1003 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      ServiceCommentLineL@1109400004 : Record 5025626;
    BEGIN
      SalesCommentLine.SETRANGE("Document Type",FromDocumentType);
      SalesCommentLine.SETRANGE("No.",FromNumber);
      // Start PA032441
      IF SalesCommentLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032441
        REPEAT
          SalesCommentLine2 := SalesCommentLine;
          SalesCommentLine2."Document Type" := ToDocumentType;
          SalesCommentLine2."No." := ToNumber;
          SalesCommentLine2.INSERT;
        UNTIL SalesCommentLine.NEXT = 0;
      // Start INC
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF (FromDocumentType = SalesCommentLine."Document Type"::Invoice) AND
           (ToDocumentType = SalesCommentLine."Document Type"::"Posted Invoice")
        THEN BEGIN // 2=Invoice,7=Posted Invoice
          ServiceCommentLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type",ServiceCommentLineL."Document Type"::Order);
      // Start EU.0012448.13245
          ServiceCommentLineL.SETRANGE("No.",SalesHeader."Service Order No.");
      // Stop EU.0012448.13245
      // Start PA032990
          IF ServiceCommentLineL.FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA032990
            REPEAT
              SalesCommentLine2.INIT;
              SalesCommentLine2."Document Type" := ToDocumentType;
              SalesCommentLine2."No." := ToNumber;
      // Start PA035901
              SalesCommentLine2."Document Line No." := ServiceCommentLineL."Document Line No.";
      // Stop PA035901
              SalesCommentLine2."Line No." := ServiceCommentLineL."Line No.";
              SalesCommentLine2.Date := ServiceCommentLineL.Date;
              SalesCommentLine2.Code := ServiceCommentLineL.Code;
              SalesCommentLine2.Comment := ServiceCommentLineL.Comment;
              SalesCommentLine2.INSERT;
            UNTIL ServiceCommentLineL.NEXT = 0;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    VAR
      TempDimBuf@1002 : TEMPORARY Record 360;
    BEGIN
      // @ Run General Journal Post Line
