    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckDim@34();
    VAR
      SalesLine2@1001 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA035597
      SalesLine2."Line No." := 0;
      CheckDimValuePosting(SalesLine2);
      CheckDimComb(SalesLine2);

      SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
      SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
      SalesLine2.SETFILTER(Type,'<>%1',SalesLine2.Type::" ");
      IF SalesLine2.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
      // Start PA035804
          IF GLSetup."incadea Dimension Concept" THEN BEGIN
            SalesLine2."Dimension Set ID" :=
              DimMgt.GetDimensionSetIDAdditional(
                SalesLine2."Dimension Set ID",
                SalesLine2."Location Code",
                SalesLine2."Gen. Bus. Posting Group",
      // Start PA035804.26217
                SalesLine2."Gen. Prod. Posting Group",
                SalesHeader."Salesperson Code");
      // Stop PA035804.26217
            SalesLine2.MODIFY;
          END;
      // Stop PA035804

          IF (SalesHeader.Invoice AND (SalesLine2."Qty. to Invoice" <> 0)) OR
             (SalesHeader.Ship AND (SalesLine2."Qty. to Ship" <> 0)) OR
             (SalesHeader.Receive AND (SalesLine2."Return Qty. to Receive" <> 0))
          THEN BEGIN
            CheckDimComb(SalesLine2);
            CheckDimValuePosting(SalesLine2);
          END
        UNTIL SalesLine2.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA035597
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckDimComb@30(SalesLine@1000 : Record 37);
    BEGIN
      // @ Check Dimension Combination
      // Start PA035597
      IF SalesLine."Line No." = 0 THEN
        IF NOT DimMgt.CheckDimIDComb(SalesHeader."Dimension Set ID") THEN
          ERROR(
            Text028,
            SalesHeader."Document Type",SalesHeader."No.",DimMgt.GetDimCombErr);

      IF SalesLine."Line No." <> 0 THEN
        IF NOT DimMgt.CheckDimIDComb(SalesLine."Dimension Set ID") THEN
          ERROR(
            Text029,
            SalesHeader."Document Type",SalesHeader."No.",SalesLine."Line No.",DimMgt.GetDimCombErr);
      // Stop PA035597
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckDimValuePosting@28(VAR SalesLine2@1000 : Record 37);
    VAR
      TableIDArr@1002 : ARRAY [10] OF Integer;
      NumberArr@1003 : ARRAY [10] OF Code[20];
      _INCADEA_@1109400000 : Boolean;
      MakeCodeArrL@1109400001 : ARRAY [10] OF Code[20];
    BEGIN
      // @ Check Dimension Value Posting
      // Start PA032441
      // Start PA036002.26210
      // Stop PA036002.26210

      IF SalesLine2."Line No." = 0 THEN BEGIN
        TableIDArr[1] := DATABASE::Customer;
        NumberArr[1] := SalesHeader."Bill-to Customer No.";
        TableIDArr[2] := DATABASE::"Salesperson/Purchaser";
        NumberArr[2] := SalesHeader."Salesperson Code";
        TableIDArr[3] := DATABASE::Campaign;
        NumberArr[3] := SalesHeader."Campaign No.";
        TableIDArr[4] := DATABASE::"Responsibility Center";
      // Start PA032441
      // Stop PA032441
      // Start PA035597
      // Start PA036002.27362
        IF NOT DimMgt.CheckDimValuePosting(TableIDArr,NumberArr,SalesHeader."Dimension Set ID",MakeCodeArrL) THEN
      // Stop PA036002.27362
      // Stop PA035597
          ERROR(
            Text030,
            SalesHeader."Document Type",SalesHeader."No.",DimMgt.GetDimValuePostingErr);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TableIDArr[1] := DimMgt.TypeToTableID3(SalesLine2.Type);
        NumberArr[1] := SalesLine2."No.";
      // Start PA036002.26567
        TableIDArr[2] := DATABASE::Vehicle;
        NumberArr[2] := SalesLine2.VIN;
        TableIDArr[3] := DATABASE::Labor;
        NumberArr[3] := SalesLine2."Labor No.";
      // Start PA036002.27362
        MakeCodeArrL[3] := SalesLine2."Labor Make Code";
      // Stop PA036002.27362
        TableIDArr[4] := DATABASE::"Service Surcharges Header";
        NumberArr[4] := SalesLine2."Service Surcharge Code";
      // Stop PA036002.26567
      // Start PA032441
      // Stop PA032441
      // Start PA035597
      // Start PA037815
      IF ((SalesLine2.Type = SalesLine2.Type::Item) AND (SalesLine2.VIN <> '') AND (SalesLine2."Order Type" = SalesLine2."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases")) THEN BEGIN
        TableIDArr[1] := 0;
        NumberArr[1] := '';
      END;
      // Stop PA037815
      // Start PA036002.27362
        IF NOT DimMgt.CheckDimValuePosting(TableIDArr,NumberArr,SalesLine2."Dimension Set ID",MakeCodeArrL) THEN
      // Stop PA036002.27362
      // Stop PA035597
          ERROR(
            Text031,
            SalesHeader."Document Type",SalesHeader."No.",SalesLine2."Line No.",DimMgt.GetDimValuePostingErr);
      END;
      // Stop PA032441
    END;

    PROCEDURE CopyAprvlToTempApprvl@149();
    BEGIN
      // @ Copy Aproval To Temp Approval
      // Start PA032441
      TempApprovalEntry.RESET;
      TempApprovalEntry.DELETEALL;
      ApprovalEntry.SETRANGE("Table ID",DATABASE::"Sales Header");
      ApprovalEntry.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
      ApprovalEntry.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
      IF ApprovalEntry.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          TempApprovalEntry.INIT;
          TempApprovalEntry := ApprovalEntry;
          TempApprovalEntry.INSERT;
        UNTIL ApprovalEntry.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Stop PA032441
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DeleteItemChargeAssgnt@5803();
    VAR
      ItemChargeAssgntSales@1000 : Record 5809;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesLine."Document Type");
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesLine."Document No.");
      // Start PA032441
      IF NOT ItemChargeAssgntSales.ISEMPTY THEN
        ItemChargeAssgntSales.DELETEALL;
      // Stop PA032441
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateItemChargeAssgnt@5808();
    VAR
      ItemChargeAssgntSales@1000 : Record 5809;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      WITH TempItemChargeAssgntSales DO BEGIN
        ClearItemChargeAssgntFilter;
        MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
      // Start PA032441
        IF FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA032441
          REPEAT
            ItemChargeAssgntSales.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Document Line No.","Line No.");
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. Assigned" :=
              ItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. Assigned" + "Qty. to Assign";
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. to Assign" := 0;
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Amount to Assign" := 0;
            ItemChargeAssgntSales.MODIFY;
          UNTIL NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateSalesOrderChargeAssgnt@5814(SalesOrderInvLine@1000 : Record 37;SalesOrderLine@1001 : Record 37);
    VAR
      SalesOrderLine2@1002 : Record 37;
      SalesOrderInvLine2@1003 : Record 37;
      SalesShptLine@1004 : Record 111;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      WITH SalesOrderInvLine DO BEGIN
        ClearItemChargeAssgntFilter;
        TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
      // Start PA032441
        IF TempItemChargeAssgntSales.FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA032441
          REPEAT
            IF TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type" = "Document Type" THEN BEGIN
              SalesOrderInvLine2.GET(
                TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type",
                TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No.",
                TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No.");
              IF ((SalesOrderLine."Document Type" = SalesOrderLine."Document Type"::Order) AND
                  (SalesOrderInvLine2."Shipment No." = "Shipment No.")) OR
                 ((SalesOrderLine."Document Type" = SalesOrderLine."Document Type"::"Return Order") AND
                  (SalesOrderInvLine2."Return Receipt No." = "Return Receipt No."))
              THEN BEGIN
                IF SalesOrderLine."Document Type" = SalesOrderLine."Document Type"::Order THEN BEGIN
                  IF NOT
                     SalesShptLine.GET(SalesOrderInvLine2."Shipment No.",SalesOrderInvLine2."Shipment Line No.")
                  THEN
                    ERROR(Text013);
                  SalesOrderLine2.GET(
                    SalesOrderLine2."Document Type"::Order,
                    SalesShptLine."Order No.",SalesShptLine."Order Line No.");
                END ELSE BEGIN
                  IF NOT
                     ReturnRcptLine.GET(SalesOrderInvLine2."Return Receipt No.",SalesOrderInvLine2."Return Receipt Line No.")
                  THEN
                    ERROR(Text037);
                  SalesOrderLine2.GET(
                    SalesOrderLine2."Document Type"::"Return Order",
                    ReturnRcptLine."Return Order No.",ReturnRcptLine."Return Order Line No.");
                END;
                UpdateSalesChargeAssgntLines(
                  SalesOrderLine,
                  SalesOrderLine2."Document Type",
                  SalesOrderLine2."Document No.",
                  SalesOrderLine2."Line No.",
                  TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. to Assign");
              END;
            END ELSE
              UpdateSalesChargeAssgntLines(
                SalesOrderLine,
                TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type",
                TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No.",
                TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No.",
                TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. to Assign");
          UNTIL TempItemChargeAssgntSales.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateSalesChargeAssgntLines@5813(SalesOrderLine@1000 : Record 37;ApplToDocType@1001 : Option;ApplToDocNo@1002 : Code[20];ApplToDocLineNo@1003 : Integer;QtyToAssign@1004 : Decimal);
    VAR
      ItemChargeAssgntSales@1005 : Record 5809;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesOrderLine."Document Type");
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesOrderLine."Document No.");
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",SalesOrderLine."Line No.");
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Type",ApplToDocType);
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. No.",ApplToDocNo);
      ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Line No.",ApplToDocLineNo);
      // Start PA032441
      IF ItemChargeAssgntSales.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032441
        ItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. Assigned" := ItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. Assigned" + QtyToAssign;
        ItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. to Assign" := 0;
        ItemChargeAssgntSales."Amount to Assign" := 0;
        ItemChargeAssgntSales.MODIFY;
      END ELSE
        IF SalesOrderLine."Document Type" <> ApplToDocType THEN BEGIN
          ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Type");
          ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. No.");
          ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Line No.");
      // Start PA032990
          IF ItemChargeAssgntSales.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032990
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. Assigned" :=
              ItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. Assigned" + QtyToAssign;
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. to Assign" :=
              ItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. to Assign" - ItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. Assigned";
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Amount to Assign" := 0;
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type" := TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type";
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No." := TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No.";
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No." := TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No.";
            ItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line Amount" := TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line Amount";
            ItemChargeAssgntSales.MODIFY;
          END;
        END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InsertAssocOrderCharge@45(SalesOrderLine@1000 : Record 37;ApplToDocType@1001 : Option;ApplToDocNo@1002 : Code[20];ApplToDocLineNo@1003 : Integer;LastLineNo@1004 : Integer;ApplToDocLineAmt@1005 : Decimal);
    VAR
      NewItemChargeAssgntSales@1006 : Record 5809;
    BEGIN
      // @ Insert Assoc Order Charge

        INIT;
        "Document Type" := SalesOrderLine."Document Type";
        "Document No." := SalesOrderLine."Document No.";
        "Document Line No." := SalesOrderLine."Line No.";
        "Line No." := LastLineNo + 10000;
        "Item Charge No." := TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Item Charge No.";
        "Item No." := TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Item No.";
        "Qty. Assigned" := TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. to Assign";
        "Qty. to Assign" := 0;
        "Amount to Assign" := 0;
        Description := TempItemChargeAssgntSales.Description;
        "Unit Cost" := TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Unit Cost";
        "Applies-to Doc. Type" := ApplToDocType;
        "Applies-to Doc. No." := ApplToDocNo;
        "Applies-to Doc. Line No." := ApplToDocLineNo;
        "Applies-to Doc. Line Amount" := ApplToDocLineAmt;
        INSERT;
      END;
      // Stop PA032441
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CopyAndCheckItemCharge@5806(SalesHeader@1000 : Record 36);
    VAR
      SalesLine2@1001 : Record 37;
      SalesLine3@1002 : Record 37;
      InvoiceEverything@1004 : Boolean;
      AssignError@1005 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      TempItemChargeAssgntSales.RESET;
      TempItemChargeAssgntSales.DELETEALL;

      // Check for max qty posting
      SalesLine2.RESET;
      SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
      SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
      SalesLine2.SETRANGE(Type,SalesLine2.Type::"Charge (Item)");
      // Start PA032441
      SalesLine2.SETFILTER("Qty. to Invoice",'<>0');
      IF SalesLine2.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT;
      SalesLine2.FINDSET;
      // Stop PA032441
      REPEAT
        ItemChargeAssgntSales.RESET;
        ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesLine2."Document Type");
        ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesLine2."Document No.");
        ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",SalesLine2."Line No.");
        ItemChargeAssgntSales.SETFILTER("Qty. to Assign",'<>0');
      // Start PA032441
        IF ItemChargeAssgntSales.FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA032441
          REPEAT
            TempItemChargeAssgntSales.INIT;
            TempItemChargeAssgntSales := ItemChargeAssgntSales;
            TempItemChargeAssgntSales.INSERT;
          UNTIL ItemChargeAssgntSales.NEXT = 0;

      // Start PA031882
      // Stop PA031882
        IF (SalesLine2."Qty. to Ship" + SalesLine2."Return Qty. to Receive" <> 0) AND
           ((SalesHeader.Ship OR SalesHeader.Receive) OR
           (ABS(SalesLine2."Qty. to Invoice") >
           ABS(SalesLine2."Qty. Shipped Not Invoiced" + SalesLine2."Qty. to Ship") +
           ABS(SalesLine2."Ret. Qty. Rcd. Not Invd.(Base)" + SalesLine2."Return Qty. to Receive")))
        THEN
          SalesLine2.TESTFIELD(Amount);

        IF NOT SalesHeader.Ship THEN
          SalesLine2."Qty. to Ship" := 0;
        IF NOT SalesHeader.Receive THEN
          SalesLine2."Return Qty. to Receive" := 0;
        IF ABS(SalesLine2."Qty. to Invoice") >
           ABS(SalesLine2."Quantity Shipped" + SalesLine2."Qty. to Ship" +
           SalesLine2."Return Qty. Received" + SalesLine2."Return Qty. to Receive" -
           SalesLine2."Quantity Invoiced")
        THEN
          SalesLine2."Qty. to Invoice" :=
            SalesLine2."Quantity Shipped" + SalesLine2."Qty. to Ship" +
            SalesLine2."Return Qty. Received" + SalesLine2."Return Qty. to Receive" -
            SalesLine2."Quantity Invoiced";

        SalesLine2.CALCFIELDS("Qty. to Assign","Qty. Assigned");
        IF ABS(SalesLine2."Qty. to Assign" + SalesLine2."Qty. Assigned") >
           ABS(SalesLine2."Qty. to Invoice" + SalesLine2."Quantity Invoiced")
        THEN
          ERROR(Text032,
            SalesLine2."Qty. to Invoice" + SalesLine2."Quantity Invoiced" -
            SalesLine2."Qty. Assigned",SalesLine2.FIELDCAPTION("Document Type"),
            SalesLine2."Document Type",SalesLine2.FIELDCAPTION("Document No."),
            SalesLine2."Document No.",SalesLine2.FIELDCAPTION("Line No."),
            SalesLine2."Line No.");
        IF SalesLine2.Quantity =
           SalesLine2."Qty. to Invoice" + SalesLine2."Quantity Invoiced"
        THEN BEGIN
          IF SalesLine2."Qty. to Assign" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
            IF SalesLine2.Quantity = SalesLine2."Quantity Invoiced" THEN BEGIN
              TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",SalesLine2."Line No.");
              TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Type",SalesLine2."Document Type");
      // Start PA032441
              IF TempItemChargeAssgntSales.FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA032441
                REPEAT
                  SalesLine3.GET(
                    TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type",
                    TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No.",
                    TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No.");
                  IF SalesLine3.Quantity = SalesLine3."Quantity Invoiced" THEN
                    ERROR(Text034,SalesLine3.TABLECAPTION,
                      SalesLine3.FIELDCAPTION("Document Type"),SalesLine3."Document Type",
                      SalesLine3.FIELDCAPTION("Document No."),SalesLine3."Document No.",
                      SalesLine3.FIELDCAPTION("Line No."),SalesLine3."Line No.");
                UNTIL TempItemChargeAssgntSales.NEXT = 0;
            END;
          END;
          IF SalesLine2.Quantity <> SalesLine2."Qty. to Assign" + SalesLine2."Qty. Assigned" THEN
            AssignError := TRUE;
        END;
      UNTIL SalesLine2.NEXT = 0;

      // Check saleslines
      IF AssignError THEN
        IF SalesHeader."Document Type" IN
           [SalesHeader."Document Type"::Invoice,SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]
        THEN
          InvoiceEverything := TRUE
        ELSE BEGIN
          SalesLine2.RESET;
          SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
          SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
          SalesLine2.SETFILTER(Type,'%1|%2',SalesLine2.Type::Item,SalesLine2.Type::"Charge (Item)");
      // Start EU.0116400.118283
          SalesLine2.SETFILTER("Qty. to Invoice", '<>0');
      // Stop EU.0116400.118283
      // Start PA032441
          IF SalesLine2.FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA032441
            REPEAT
              IF SalesHeader.Ship OR SalesHeader.Receive THEN
                InvoiceEverything :=
                  SalesLine2.Quantity = SalesLine2."Qty. to Invoice" + SalesLine2."Quantity Invoiced"
              ELSE
                InvoiceEverything :=
                  (SalesLine2.Quantity = SalesLine2."Qty. to Invoice" + SalesLine2."Quantity Invoiced") AND
                  (SalesLine2."Qty. to Invoice" =
                   SalesLine2."Qty. Shipped Not Invoiced" + SalesLine2."Ret. Qty. Rcd. Not Invd.(Base)");
            UNTIL (SalesLine2.NEXT = 0) OR (NOT InvoiceEverything);
        END;

      IF InvoiceEverything AND AssignError THEN
        ERROR(Text033);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ClearItemChargeAssgntFilter@27();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Line No.");
      TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Type");
      TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. No.");
      TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Line No.");
      TempItemChargeAssgntSales.MARKEDONLY(FALSE);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetItemChargeLine@5809(VAR ItemChargeSalesLine@1000 : Record 37);
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      WITH TempItemChargeAssgntSales DO BEGIN
        IF (ItemChargeSalesLine."Document Type" <> "Document Type") OR
           (ItemChargeSalesLine."Document No." <> "Document No.") OR
           (ItemChargeSalesLine."Line No." <> "Document Line No.")
        THEN BEGIN
          ItemChargeSalesLine.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Document Line No.");
          IF NOT SalesHeader.Ship THEN
            ItemChargeSalesLine."Qty. to Ship" := 0;
          IF NOT SalesHeader.Receive THEN
            ItemChargeSalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive" := 0;
          IF ABS(ItemChargeSalesLine."Qty. to Invoice") >
             ABS(ItemChargeSalesLine."Quantity Shipped" + ItemChargeSalesLine."Qty. to Ship" +
               ItemChargeSalesLine."Return Qty. Received" + ItemChargeSalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive" -
               ItemChargeSalesLine."Quantity Invoiced")
          THEN
            ItemChargeSalesLine."Qty. to Invoice" :=
              ItemChargeSalesLine."Quantity Shipped" + ItemChargeSalesLine."Qty. to Ship" +
              ItemChargeSalesLine."Return Qty. Received" + ItemChargeSalesLine."Return Qty. to Receive" -
              ItemChargeSalesLine."Quantity Invoiced";
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE OnlyAssgntPosting@36() : Boolean;
    VAR
      SalesLine@1000 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      WITH SalesHeader DO BEGIN
        ItemChargeAssgntOnly := FALSE;
        CopyAndCheckItemCharge(SalesHeader);
        ClearItemChargeAssgntFilter;
        TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETCURRENTKEY("Applies-to Doc. Type");
        TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETFILTER("Applies-to Doc. Type",'<>%1',"Document Type");
        SalesLine.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        SalesLine.SETRANGE("Document No.","No.");
        SalesLine.SETFILTER("Qty. to Assign",'<>0');
      // Start PA032441
        IF SalesLine.FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA032441
          REPEAT
            TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",SalesLine."Line No.");
      // Start PA032441
            ItemChargeAssgntOnly := NOT TempItemChargeAssgntSales.ISEMPTY;
      // Stop PA032441
          UNTIL (SalesLine.NEXT = 0) OR ItemChargeAssgntOnly
        ELSE
          ItemChargeAssgntOnly := FALSE;
      END;
      EXIT(ItemChargeAssgntOnly);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcQtyToInvoice@24(QtyToHandle@1000 : Decimal;QtyToInvoice@1001 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF ABS(QtyToHandle) > ABS(QtyToInvoice) THEN
        EXIT(-QtyToHandle);

      EXIT(-QtyToInvoice);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE PostItemCharge@42(SalesLine@1005 : Record 37;ItemEntryNo@1004 : Integer;QuantityBase@1003 : Decimal;AmountToAssign@1002 : Decimal;QtyToAssign@1001 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      WITH TempItemChargeAssgntSales DO BEGIN
        SalesLine."No." := "Item No.";
        SalesLine."Item Type" := "Item Type";
        SalesLine."Appl.-to Item Entry" := ItemEntryNo;
        IF NOT ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]) THEN
          SalesLine.Amount := -AmountToAssign
        ELSE
          SalesLine.Amount := AmountToAssign;

        IF SalesLine."Currency Code" <> '' THEN
          SalesLine."Unit Cost" := ROUND(
            -SalesLine.Amount / QuantityBase,Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision")
        ELSE
          SalesLine."Unit Cost" := ROUND(
            -SalesLine.Amount / QuantityBase,GLSetup."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");

        IF SalesHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN
          SalesLine.Amount :=
            CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
              UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",SalesLine.Amount,SalesHeader."Currency Factor");
        SalesLine."Inv. Discount Amount" := ROUND(
          SalesLine."Inv. Discount Amount" / SalesLine.Quantity * QtyToAssign,
          GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision");
        SalesLine.Amount := ROUND(SalesLine.Amount,GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision");
        SalesLine."Unit Cost (LCY)" := ROUND(
          SalesLine.Amount / QuantityBase,GLSetup."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
        SalesLine."Line No." := "Document Line No.";
        PostItemJnlLine(
          SalesLine,
          0,0,-QuantityBase,-QuantityBase,
          SalesLine."Appl.-to Item Entry",
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Item Charge No.");
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CopyPurchCommentLines@148(FromDocumentType@1000 : Integer;ToDocumentType@1001 : Integer;FromNumber@1002 : Code[20];ToNumber@1003 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      PurchCommentLine@1004 : Record 43;
      PurchCommentLine2@1005 : Record 43;
    BEGIN
      // @ Copy Purch Comment Lines
      // Start PA032441
      PurchCommentLine.SETRANGE("Document Type",FromDocumentType);
      PurchCommentLine.SETRANGE("No.",FromNumber);
      IF PurchCommentLine.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          PurchCommentLine2 := PurchCommentLine;
          PurchCommentLine2."Document Type" := ToDocumentType;
          PurchCommentLine2."No." := ToNumber;
          PurchCommentLine2.INSERT;
        UNTIL PurchCommentLine.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA032441
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetNextSalesline@50(VAR SalesLine@1000 : Record 37) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ Get Next Sales line
      // Start PA032441
      IF SalesLine.NEXT = 1 THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      // Start PA036547
      IF TempPrepaymentSalesLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA036547
        SalesLine := TempPrepaymentSalesLine;
        TempPrepaymentSalesLine.DELETE;
      // Start EU.0019839
        SalesHeader.Ship := TRUE;
      // Stop EU.0019839
        EXIT(FALSE);
      END;
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA032441
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InsertICGenJnlLine@150(SalesLine@1000 : Record 37);
    VAR
      ICGLAccount@1001 : Record 410;
      Vend@1002 : Record 23;
      ICPartner@1003 : Record 413;
    BEGIN
      // @ Insert IC General Journal Line
      // Start PA032441
      SalesHeader.TESTFIELD("Sell-to IC Partner Code",'');
      SalesHeader.TESTFIELD("Bill-to IC Partner Code",'');
      SalesLine.TESTFIELD("IC Partner Ref. Type",SalesLine."IC Partner Ref. Type"::"G/L Account");
      ICGLAccount.GET(SalesLine."IC Partner Reference");
      ICGenJnlLineNo := ICGenJnlLineNo + 1;
      TempICGenJnlLine.INIT;
      TempICGenJnlLine."Line No." := ICGenJnlLineNo;
      TempICGenJnlLine.VALIDATE("Posting Date",SalesHeader."Posting Date");
      TempICGenJnlLine."Document Date" := SalesHeader."Document Date";
      TempICGenJnlLine.Description := SalesHeader."Posting Description";
      TempICGenJnlLine."Reason Code" := SalesHeader."Reason Code";
      TempICGenJnlLine."Document Type" := GenJnlLineDocType;
      TempICGenJnlLine."Document No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
      TempICGenJnlLine."External Document No." := GenJnlLineExtDocNo;
      TempICGenJnlLine.VALIDATE("Account Type",TempICGenJnlLine."Account Type"::"IC Partner");
      TempICGenJnlLine.VALIDATE("Account No.",SalesLine."IC Partner Code");
      TempICGenJnlLine."Source Currency Code" := SalesHeader."Currency Code";
      TempICGenJnlLine."Source Currency Amount" := TempICGenJnlLine.Amount;
      TempICGenJnlLine.Correction := SalesHeader.Correction;
      TempICGenJnlLine."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := SalesLine."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      TempICGenJnlLine."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := SalesLine."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code";
      // Start PA035597
      TempICGenJnlLine."Dimension Set ID" := SalesLine."Dimension Set ID";
      // Stop PA035597
      TempICGenJnlLine."Source Code" := SrcCode;
      TempICGenJnlLine."Country/Region Code" := SalesHeader."VAT Country Code";
      TempICGenJnlLine."Source Type" := GenJnlLine."Source Type"::Customer;
      TempICGenJnlLine."Source No." := SalesHeader."Bill-to Customer No.";
      TempICGenJnlLine."Posting No. Series" := SalesHeader."Posting No. Series";
      TempICGenJnlLine.VALIDATE("Bal. Account Type",TempICGenJnlLine."Bal. Account Type"::"G/L Account");
      TempICGenJnlLine.VALIDATE("Bal. Account No.",SalesLine."No.");
      Vend.SETRANGE("IC Partner Code",SalesLine."IC Partner Code");
      IF Vend.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        TempICGenJnlLine.VALIDATE("Bal. Gen. Bus. Posting Group",Vend."Gen. Bus. Posting Group");
        TempICGenJnlLine.VALIDATE("Bal. VAT Bus. Posting Group",Vend."VAT Bus. Posting Group");
      END;
      TempICGenJnlLine."IC Partner Code" := SalesLine."IC Partner Code";
      TempICGenJnlLine."IC Partner G/L Acc. No." := SalesLine."IC Partner Reference";
      TempICGenJnlLine."IC Direction" := TempICGenJnlLine."IC Direction"::Outgoing;
      ICPartner.GET(SalesLine."IC Partner Code");
      IF ICPartner."Cost Distribution in LCY" AND (SalesLine."Currency Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
        TempICGenJnlLine."Currency Code" := '';
        TempICGenJnlLine."Currency Factor" := 0;
        Currency.GET(SalesLine."Currency Code");
        IF SalesHeader."Document Type" IN
           [SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Return Order",SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]
        THEN
          TempICGenJnlLine.Amount :=
            -ROUND(
              CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                SalesHeader."Posting Date",SalesLine."Currency Code",
                SalesLine.Amount,SalesHeader."Currency Factor"))
        ELSE
          TempICGenJnlLine.Amount :=
            ROUND(
              CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                SalesHeader."Posting Date",SalesLine."Currency Code",
                SalesLine.Amount,SalesHeader."Currency Factor"));
      END ELSE BEGIN
        Currency.InitRoundingPrecision;
        TempICGenJnlLine."Currency Code" := SalesHeader."Currency Code";
        TempICGenJnlLine."Currency Factor" := SalesHeader."Currency Factor";
        IF SalesHeader."Document Type" IN [SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Return Order",SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
          TempICGenJnlLine.Amount := -SalesLine.Amount
        ELSE
          TempICGenJnlLine.Amount := SalesLine.Amount;
      END;
      IF TempICGenJnlLine."Bal. VAT %" <> 0 THEN
        TempICGenJnlLine.Amount := ROUND(TempICGenJnlLine.Amount * (1 + TempICGenJnlLine."Bal. VAT %" / 100),
          Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      TempICGenJnlLine.VALIDATE(Amount);
      TempICGenJnlLine.INSERT;

      // Start PA035597
      // Stop PA035597
      // Stop PA032441
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE PostICGenJnl@151();
    VAR
      ICInOutBoxMgt@1001 : Codeunit 427;
      ICTransactionNo@1000 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // @ Post IC General Journal
      // Start PA032441
      TempICGenJnlLine.RESET;
      IF TempICGenJnlLine.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
      // Start PA035597
      // Stop PA035597
          ICTransactionNo := ICInOutBoxMgt.CreateOutboxJnlTransaction(TempICGenJnlLine,FALSE);
      // Start PA035597
          ICInOutBoxMgt.CreateOutboxJnlLine(ICTransactionNo,1,TempICGenJnlLine);
          GenJnlPostLine.RunWithCheck(TempICGenJnlLine);
      // Stop PA035597
        UNTIL TempICGenJnlLine.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA032441
    END;

    END;

    [External]
    PROCEDURE GetPostedDocumentRecord@222(SalesHeader@1000 : Record 36;VAR PostedSalesDocumentVariant@1001 : Variant);
    VAR
      SalesInvHeader@1007 : Record 112;
      SalesCrMemoHeader@1006 : Record 114;
      IsHandled@1002 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      WITH SalesHeader DO
        CASE "Document Type" OF
          "Document Type"::Order:
            IF Invoice THEN BEGIN
              SalesInvHeader.GET("Last Posting No.");
              SalesInvHeader.SETRECFILTER;
              PostedSalesDocumentVariant := SalesInvHeader;
            END;
          "Document Type"::Invoice:
            BEGIN
              IF "Last Posting No." = '' THEN
                SalesInvHeader.GET("No.")
              ELSE
                SalesInvHeader.GET("Last Posting No.");

              SalesInvHeader.SETRECFILTER;
              PostedSalesDocumentVariant := SalesInvHeader;
            END;
          "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
            BEGIN
              IF "Last Posting No." = '' THEN
                SalesCrMemoHeader.GET("No.")
              ELSE
                SalesCrMemoHeader.GET("Last Posting No.");
              SalesCrMemoHeader.SETRECFILTER;
              PostedSalesDocumentVariant := SalesCrMemoHeader;
            END;
          "Document Type"::"Return Order":
            IF Invoice THEN BEGIN
              IF "Last Posting No." = '' THEN
                SalesCrMemoHeader.GET("No.")
              ELSE
                SalesCrMemoHeader.GET("Last Posting No.");
              SalesCrMemoHeader.SETRECFILTER;
              PostedSalesDocumentVariant := SalesCrMemoHeader;
            END;
          ELSE BEGIN
            IsHandled := FALSE;
            OnGetPostedDocumentRecordElseCase(SalesHeader,PostedSalesDocumentVariant,IsHandled);
            IF NOT IsHandled THEN
              ERROR(NotSupportedDocumentTypeErr,"Document Type");
          END;
        END;
    END;

    [Internal]
    PROCEDURE SendPostedDocumentRecord@223(SalesHeader@1000 : Record 36;VAR DocumentSendingProfile@1001 : Record 60);
    VAR
      SalesInvHeader@1007 : Record 112;
      SalesCrMemoHeader@1006 : Record 114;
      SalesShipmentHeader@1002 : Record 110;
      ConfirmManagement@1004 : Codeunit 27;
      IsHandled@1005 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      WITH SalesHeader DO
        CASE "Document Type" OF
          "Document Type"::Order:
            BEGIN
              OnSendSalesDocument(Invoice AND Ship,SuppressCommit);
              IF Invoice THEN BEGIN
                SalesInvHeader.GET("Last Posting No.");
                SalesInvHeader.SETRECFILTER;
      // Start EU.0101361
                CASE "Order Type" OF
                  "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
                    SalesInvHeader.SendProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
                  "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
                    SalesInvHeader.SendVehicleProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
      // Start EU.0114641
                  "Order Type"::Service:
                    SalesInvHeader.SendServiceProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
      // Stop EU.0114641
                END;
              END;
              IF Ship AND Invoice THEN //AND NOT OfficeManagement.IsAvailable THEN
                IF NOT ConfirmManagement.ConfirmProcess(DownloadShipmentAlsoQst,TRUE) THEN
                  EXIT;
              IF Ship THEN BEGIN
                SalesShipmentHeader.GET("Last Shipping No.");
                SalesShipmentHeader.SETRECFILTER;
                CASE "Order Type" OF
                  "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
                    SalesShipmentHeader.SendProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
                  "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
                    SalesShipmentHeader.SendVehicleProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
                END;
              END;
            END;
          "Document Type"::Invoice:
            BEGIN
              IF "Last Posting No." = '' THEN
                SalesInvHeader.GET("No.")
              ELSE
                SalesInvHeader.GET("Last Posting No.");

              SalesInvHeader.SETRECFILTER;
              CASE "Order Type" OF
                "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
                  SalesInvHeader.SendProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
                "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
                  SalesInvHeader.SendVehicleProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
      // Start EU.0111610
                "Order Type"::Service:
                  SalesInvHeader.SendServiceProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
      // Stop EU.0111610
              END;
            END;
          "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
            BEGIN
              IF "Last Posting No." = '' THEN
                SalesCrMemoHeader.GET("No.")
              ELSE
                SalesCrMemoHeader.GET("Last Posting No.");
              SalesCrMemoHeader.SETRECFILTER;
              CASE "Order Type" OF
                "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
                  SalesCrMemoHeader.SendProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
                "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
                  SalesCrMemoHeader.SendVehicleProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
      // Start EU.0114641
                "Order Type"::Service:
                  SalesCrMemoHeader.SendServiceProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
      // Stop EU.0114641
              END;
            END;
          "Document Type"::"Return Order":
            BEGIN
              IF Invoice THEN BEGIN
                IF "Last Posting No." = '' THEN
                  SalesCrMemoHeader.GET("No.")
                ELSE
                  SalesCrMemoHeader.GET("Last Posting No.");
                SalesCrMemoHeader.SETRECFILTER;
                  IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
                    SalesCrMemoHeader.SendVehicleProfile(DocumentSendingProfile)
                  ELSE
                    SalesCrMemoHeader.SendProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
              END;
                IF Receive AND NOT Invoice THEN BEGIN
                  IF "Last Posting No." = '' THEN
                    ReturnRcptHeader.GET("No.")
                  ELSE
                    SalesCrMemoHeader.GET("Last Posting No.");
                    ReturnRcptHeader.SETRECFILTER;
                    IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
                      ReturnRcptHeader.SendVehicleProfile(DocumentSendingProfile)
                    ELSE
                      ReturnRcptHeader.SendProfile(DocumentSendingProfile);
                END;
              END;
      // Stop EU.0101361
          ELSE BEGIN
            IsHandled := FALSE;
            OnSendPostedDocumentRecordElseCase(SalesHeader,DocumentSendingProfile,IsHandled);
            IF NOT IsHandled THEN
              ERROR(NotSupportedDocumentTypeErr,"Document Type");
          END;
        END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GenJnlLineExitPoint@1101342669(VAR GenJnlLineP@1101342643 : Record 81;TriggerP@1109400002 : Integer;TypeP@1109400001 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1109400000 : Text[50]) ReturnR : Boolean;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE PostVehJnlLine@1109400001();
    VAR
      VehJnlLine@1109400000 : Record 5025403;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA035134
      IF NOT TempVehJnlLineG.FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA035134
        EXIT;

      REPEAT
        VehJnlLine := TempVehJnlLineG;
        VehJnlLine.VALIDATE("Item Ledger Entry No.");
        VehicleJnlLinePostG.RUN(VehJnlLine);
      UNTIL TempVehJnlLineG.NEXT = 0;

      TempVehJnlLineG.DELETEALL;
      NextVehJnlLineNoG := 0;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertTempVehJnlLine@1109400005(SalesLineP@1109400000 : Record 37;ItemChargeNoP@1109400001 : Code[20];VINNoP@1109400002 : Code[20];BookNoP@1000 : Code[20];BranchBookNoP@1001 : Code[20];AmountToAssignP@1109400003 : Decimal;QtyToAssignP@1109400004 : Decimal;ItemLedgEntryNoP@1002 : Integer;ValueEntryNoP@1109400005 : Integer);
    VAR
      ValueEntryL@1109400006 : Record 5802;
      SalesShptLineL@1109400007 : Record 111;
      ReturnRcptLineL@1109400008 : Record 6661;
      LocationL@1109400009 : Record 14;
      SalesIncentiveL@1101157045 : Record 5025481;
      TempL@1109400010 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF (VINNoP <> '') AND (QtyToAssignP <> 0) THEN BEGIN
        // Posting of Vehicle Ledger Entries
        TempVehJnlLineG.INIT;
        NextVehJnlLineNoG := NextVehJnlLineNoG + 10000;
        TempVehJnlLineG."Line No." := NextVehJnlLineNoG;
        TempVehJnlLineG."Posting Date" := SalesHeader."Posting Date";
        TempVehJnlLineG."Document Date" := SalesHeader."Document Date";
        TempVehJnlLineG.Type := TempVehJnlLineG.Type::Vehicle;
        TempVehJnlLineG."Document No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
        TempVehJnlLineG."External Document No." := GenJnlLineExtDocNo;
        TempVehJnlLineG."Book No." := BookNoP;
        TempVehJnlLineG."Item Charge No." := ItemChargeNoP;
        TempVehJnlLineG.ExcessiveTradeInPriceSet;
        TempVehJnlLineG.VIN := VINNoP;
      // Start PA041023
        TempVehJnlLineG."License No." := SalLineG."Reference License No.";
      // Stop PA041023
        TempVehJnlLineG."Item Ledger Entry No." := ItemLedgEntryNoP;
        TempVehJnlLineG."Applies-to Value Entry" := ValueEntryNoP;
      // Start PA036728
        TempVehJnlLineG."Salesperson Code 2" := SalesHeader."Salesperson Code 2";
      // Stop PA036728
        ValueEntryL.GET(ValueEntryNoP);
        IF ValueEntryL.Inventoriable THEN BEGIN
          TempVehJnlLineG."Direct Unit Cost" := AmountToAssignP;
          TempVehJnlLineG."Unit Cost" := AmountToAssignP;
      // Start EU.0116400.116480
      // Start EU.0057536
          TempVehJnlLineG."Total Cost" := ValueEntryL.Amount;
      // Stop EU.0057536
      // Stop EU.0116400.116480
        END;
        IF ValueEntryL."Item Ledger Entry Type" = ValueEntryL."Item Ledger Entry Type"::Sale THEN BEGIN
          TempVehJnlLineG."Unit Price" := AmountToAssignP;
      // Start EU.0057536
          TempVehJnlLineG."Total Price" := ValueEntryL.Amount;
      // Stop EU.0057536
        END;
        IF SalesLineP.GET(TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type",
           TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No.",TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No.")
        THEN
          IF (SalesLine.Type = SalesLine.Type::Item) AND
             (SalesLine."Item Type" = SalesLine."Item Type"::Vehicle) AND
             (SalesLine."Allow Item Charge Assignment")
      // Start EU.0116400.116480
          THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0057536
            IF SalesHeader.Invoice AND
               ((SalesLine."Document Type" = SalesLine."Document Type"::"Credit Memo") OR
               (SalesLine."Document Type" = SalesLine."Document Type"::"Return Order"))
            THEN
              TempVehJnlLineG."Vehicle Portion" := -ValueEntryL.Amount
            ELSE
              TempVehJnlLineG."Vehicle Portion" := ValueEntryL.Amount;
          END;
      // Stop EU.0116400.116480
      // Stop EU.0057536
        IF (SalesLine.Type = SalesLine.Type::Item) AND
           (SalesLine."Item Type" = SalesLine."Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer") AND
           (SalesLine."Allow Item Charge Assignment")
        THEN
      // Stop EU.0057536
          TempVehJnlLineG."Veh. Transfer Portion" := ValueEntryL.Amount;
      // Start PA045331
        IF (SalesLine.Type = SalesLine.Type::Item) AND
           (SalesLine."Item Type" = SalesLine."Item Type"::"Own Option") AND
           (SalesLine."Allow Item Charge Assignment")
        THEN
      // Start EU.0057536
          TempVehJnlLineG."Own Option Portion" := ValueEntryL.Amount;
      // Stop EU.0057536
      // Stop PA045331
        IF SalesShptLineL.GET(TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No.",
           TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No.")
        THEN
          IF (SalesShptLineL.Type = SalesShptLineL.Type::Item) AND
             (SalesShptLineL."Item Type" = SalesShptLineL."Item Type"::Vehicle)
          THEN
      // Start EU.0057536
            TempVehJnlLineG."Vehicle Portion" := ValueEntryL.Amount;
      // Stop EU.0057536
        IF (SalesShptLineL.Type = SalesShptLineL.Type::Item) AND
           (SalesShptLineL."Item Type" = SalesShptLineL."Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer")
        THEN
      // Start EU.0057536
          TempVehJnlLineG."Veh. Transfer Portion" := ValueEntryL.Amount;
      // Stop EU.0057536
      // Start PA045331
        IF (SalesShptLineL.Type = SalesShptLineL.Type::Item) AND
           (SalesShptLineL."Item Type" = SalesShptLineL."Item Type"::"Own Option")
        THEN
      // Start EU.0057536
          TempVehJnlLineG."Own Option Portion" := ValueEntryL.Amount;
      // Stop EU.0057536
      // Stop PA045331
        IF ReturnRcptLineL.GET(TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No.",
           TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No.")
        THEN
          IF (ReturnRcptLineL.Type = ReturnRcptLineL.Type::Item) AND
             (ReturnRcptLineL."Item Type" = ReturnRcptLineL."Item Type"::Vehicle)
          THEN
      // Start EU.0057536
            TempVehJnlLineG."Vehicle Portion" := ValueEntryL.Amount;
      // Stop EU.0057536
        IF (ReturnRcptLineL.Type = ReturnRcptLineL.Type::Item) AND
           (ReturnRcptLineL."Item Type" = ReturnRcptLineL."Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer")
        THEN
      // Start EU.0057536
          TempVehJnlLineG."Veh. Transfer Portion" := ValueEntryL.Amount;
      // Stop EU.0057536
      // Start PA045331
        IF (ReturnRcptLineL.Type = ReturnRcptLineL.Type::Item) AND
           (ReturnRcptLineL."Item Type" = ReturnRcptLineL."Item Type"::"Own Option")
        THEN
      // Start EU.0057536
          TempVehJnlLineG."Own Option Portion" := ValueEntryL.Amount;
      // Stop EU.0057536
      // Stop PA045331

        IF TempVehJnlLineG."Branch Book No." = '' THEN
          TempVehJnlLineG."Branch Book No." := BranchBookNoP;
      // Start PA032990.BMW
        IF LocationL.GET(SalesLine."Location Code") THEN
          TempVehJnlLineG."Branch Code" := LocationL."Branch Code"
        ELSE
          TempVehJnlLineG."Branch Code" := CurrBranchCodeG;
      // Stop PA032990.BMW

        TempVehJnlLineG.Description := SalesLineP.Description;
        TempVehJnlLineG."Department Code" := ValueEntryL."Global Dimension 1 Code";
        TempVehJnlLineG."Make Code" := ValueEntryL."Global Dimension 2 Code";
      // Start PA035597
        TempVehJnlLineG."Dimension Set ID" := ValueEntryL."Dimension Set ID";
      // Stop PA035597
        TempVehJnlLineG."Source Code" := ValueEntryL."Source Code";
        TempVehJnlLineG."Assoc. No." := SalesLineP."No.";
        TempVehJnlLineG."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" := SalesLineP."Gen. Prod. Posting Group";
        TempVehJnlLineG."Main Area" := ValueEntryL."Main Area";
        TempVehJnlLineG."No." := SalesLineP."No.";
        TempVehJnlLineG."Source Type" := ValueEntryL."Source Type";
        TempVehJnlLineG."Source No." := ValueEntryL."Source No.";
        TempVehJnlLineG."Document Type" := TempVehJnlLineG."Document Type"::External;
        TempVehJnlLineG."Source No. (Payment)" := ValueEntryL."Source No. (Payment)";
        TempVehJnlLineG."VAT Prod. Posting Group" := SalesLineP."VAT Prod. Posting Group";
        TempVehJnlLineG."Posting No. Series" := SalesHeader."Posting No. Series";
        TempVehJnlLineG."Location Code" := SalesLineP."Location Code";
        IF SalesHeader."Document Type" IN [SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Return Order",
           SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]
        THEN
          TempVehJnlLineG."Credit Memo" := TRUE;
      // Start PA035473
        IF (TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Sales Incentive No." <> '') AND
          (SalesHeader."Document Type" = SalesHeader."Document Type"::Invoice) //must be invoice
        THEN BEGIN
          SalesIncentiveL.GET(TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Sales Incentive No.");
          TempVehJnlLineG."Sales Incentive Group" := SalesIncentiveL."Sales Incentive Group";
          TempVehJnlLineG."Sales Incentive No." := TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Sales Incentive No.";
        END;
      // Stop PA035473
        TempVehJnlLineG.INSERT;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CopyOption@5025351(FromDocumentTypeP@1109400000 : Integer;ToDocumentTypeP@1109400001 : Integer;FromNumberP@1109400002 : Code[20];ToNumberP@1109400003 : Code[20];FromLineNumberP@1109400004 : Integer;ToLineNumberP@1109400005 : Integer);
    VAR
      OptionVariantL@1109400006 : Record 5025424;
      OptionVariantBOML@1101257463 : Record 5205912;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantL.Area::Sale);
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Type",FromDocumentTypeP);
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document No.",FromNumberP);
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", FromLineNumberP);
      IF OptionVariantL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          PostedOptionVariantG.TRANSFERFIELDS(OptionVariantL);
          PostedOptionVariantG."Document Type" := ToDocumentTypeP;
          PostedOptionVariantG."Document No." := ToNumberP;
          PostedOptionVariantG."Document Line No." := ToLineNumberP;
          PostedOptionVariantG.INSERT;
      // Start PA036997
          OptionVariantBOML.TransferToPosted(OptionVariantL, ToDocumentTypeP, ToNumberP, ToLineNumberP);
      // Stop PA036997
        UNTIL OptionVariantL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckDiscToDiffTax@5025367();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF (SalesLine."Order Type" = SalesLine."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND (SalesLine."Line No." <> 0) AND
         (SalesLine."Item Type" = SalesLine."Item Type"::Vehicle) AND
         (SalesLine."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLine."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax") AND
         ((SalesLine."Line Discount %" <> 0) OR (SalesLine."Line Discount Amount" <>0))
      THEN
        ERROR(C_INC036,SalesLine.FIELDCAPTION("Line Discount %"),SalesLine.FIELDCAPTION("VAT Calculation Type"),
          SalesLine."VAT Calculation Type");
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetOptionToZero@5025352();
    VAR
      VehicleL@1109400003 : Record 5025400;
      VehCustL@1109400000 : Record 5025469;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF VehicleL.GET(SalesLine.VIN) THEN BEGIN
        VehicleL.Mileage := SalesLine.Mileage;
        VehicleL."Running Time" := SalesLine."Running Time";
      // Start EU.0128664.128617
        IF VehicleL."Vehicle Status" IN [VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle", VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle"] THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0128664.128617
          VehicleL."Own Sale" := TRUE;
        END;
      // Start PA037592
        IF (VehicleL."Vehicle Status" = VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle") AND
           (VehicleL."Initial Registration" = 0D)
        THEN
          VehicleL.VALIDATE("Initial Registration", SalesLine."Registration Date");
      // Stop PA037592
        IF SalesHeader.Ship THEN BEGIN
          VehCustL.RESET;
          VehCustL.SETRANGE(VIN,VehicleL.VIN);
          VehCustL.SETRANGE(Type,VehCustL.Type::Buyer);
          IF NOT VehCustL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104357.106325
            IF NOT (VehicleL."Vehicle Status" IN [VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle", VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle"]) THEN BEGIN
              VehCustL.VIN := VehicleL.VIN;
              VehCustL.Type := VehCustL.Type::Buyer;
              VehCustL.VALIDATE("Customer No.",SalesHeader."Sell-to Customer No.");
              VehCustL.INSERT(TRUE);
            END;
      // Stop EU.0104357.106325
          END ELSE BEGIN
            VehCustL.VALIDATE("Customer No.",SalesHeader."Sell-to Customer No.");
            VehCustL.MODIFY(TRUE);
          END;
        END;
        VehicleL."License No." := SalesLine."License No.";
        VehicleL."Customer Registration Date" := SalesLine."Registration Date";

        IF IsImporter THEN BEGIN
          VehicleL."Dealer Request Status" := VehicleL."Dealer Request Status"::Sold;
          VehicleStocklistG.RESET;
          VehicleStocklistG.SETRANGE(VIN,VehicleL.VIN);
          IF VehicleStocklistG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            VehicleStocklistG."Dealer Request Status" := VehicleStocklistG."Dealer Request Status"::Sold;
            VehicleStocklistG."Vehicle Status" := VehicleStocklistG."Vehicle Status"::"Customer Vehicle";
            VehicleStocklistG.MODIFY;
          END;
        END;

        VehicleL.MODIFY;
        VehicleL.SearchVehicleOverAllCompanies('/VEHICLE-CHANGE');
        VehicleCollectionUnitG.SetVehicleCrMeAvgSalPrice(VehicleL,SalesHeader."Posting Date", VehicleL."Purchase Invoice Date");
        IF SalesHeader.Invoice THEN BEGIN
          VehCustL.RESET;
          VehCustL.SETRANGE(VIN,VehicleL.VIN);
          VehCustL.SETRANGE(Type,VehCustL.Type::Owner);
          IF NOT VehCustL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            VehCustL.VIN := VehicleL.VIN;
            VehCustL.Type := VehCustL.Type::Owner;
            VehCustL.VALIDATE("Customer No.",SalesHeader."Bill-to Customer No.");
            VehCustL.VALIDATE("Def. Service Bill-to Customer",TRUE);
            VehCustL.INSERT(TRUE);
          END ELSE BEGIN
            VehCustL.VALIDATE("Customer No.",SalesHeader."Bill-to Customer No.");
      // Start EU.0048491
            IF NOT VehCustL."Def. Service Bill-to Customer" THEN
              VehCustL.VALIDATE("Def. Service Bill-to Customer",TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0048491
            VehCustL.MODIFY(TRUE);
          END;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE ReactivateOption@5025353();
    VAR
      VehJnlManagmentL@1109400010 : Codeunit 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      VehJnlManagmentL.SetReceive(SalesHeader.Receive);
      VehJnlManagmentL.SalesReactivateOption(
        SalesLine.VIN,
        SalesLine."Book No.",
        SalesLine."Posting Group",
        SalesLine."Gen. Prod. Posting Group",
        SalesLine."Location Code",
        SalesLine."License No.",
        SalesLine."Vehicle Status" - 1,
        OldDateOfSaleG);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CopyTradeIn@5025355(SalesHdrP@1109400000 : Record 36;ToDocumentTypeP@1109400001 : Integer;ToNumberP@1109400003 : Code[20];FromLineNumberP@1109400004 : Integer;ToLineNumberP@1109400005 : Integer);
    VAR
      SalesTradeInL@1109400006 : Record 5025442;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA033327
      SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Document Type", SalesHdrP."Document Type");
      SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Document No.", SalesHdrP."No.");
      // Stop PA033327
      SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", FromLineNumberP);
      IF SalesTradeInL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
      // Start PA032795
          Vehicle2G.GET(SalesTradeInL.VIN);
      // Stop PA032795
          PostedTradeInG.TRANSFERFIELDS(SalesTradeInL);
      // Start PA032795
          PostedTradeInG."License No." := Vehicle2G."License No.";
      // Stop PA032795
          PostedTradeInG."Document Type" := ToDocumentTypeP;
          PostedTradeInG."Document No." := ToNumberP;
          PostedTradeInG."Document Line No." := ToLineNumberP;
          PostedTradeInG.INSERT;
      // Start PA035801.22361
      // Stop PA035801.22361
        UNTIL SalesTradeInL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckTradeIn@5025356();
    VAR
      SalesTradeInL@1109400000 : Record 5025442;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function is used for Sales Credit Memo to check if Purchase Invoices for Trade-Ins are already created

      // Start PA041187.89985
      SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Document Type", SalesTradeInL."Document Type"::"Credit Memo");
      SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Document No.", SalesLine."Document No.");
      SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", SalesLine."Line No.");
      // Start EU.0076911
      SalesTradeInL.SETFILTER("Purch. Cr. Memo No.", '<>%1', '');
      // Stop EU.0076911
      // Start PA041187.90150
      SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Posted Purch. Cr. Memo No.", '');
      // Stop PA041187.90150
      // Start PA041187.90587
      SalesTradeInL.SETFILTER("Posted Purch. Invoice No.", '<>%1', '');
      // Stop PA041187.90587
      IF NOT SalesTradeInL.ISEMPTY THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_TradeInCreditMemo);
      // Stop PA041187.89985
    END;

    PROCEDURE NoteTradeIn@5025359();
    VAR
      SalTradeInLineL@1109400000 : Record 5025442;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      SalTradeInLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", SalesLine."Document Type");
      SalTradeInLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", SalesLine."Document No.");
      SalTradeInLineL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", SalesLine."Line No.");
      // Start PA041187.87656
      IF SalesLine."Document Type" = SalesLine."Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN
        SalTradeInLineL.SETFILTER("Posted Purch. Cr. Memo No.",'<>%1','')
      ELSE
        SalTradeInLineL.SETFILTER("Posted Purch. Invoice No.",'<>%1','');
      // Stop PA041187.87656
      IF SalTradeInLineL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          IF SalesLine."Document Type" = SalesLine."Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN
            TradeInApplCodeG[LastTradeInG] := SalTradeInLineL."Posted Purch. Cr. Memo No."
          ELSE
            TradeInApplCodeG[LastTradeInG] := SalTradeInLineL."Posted Purch. Invoice No.";
          LastTradeInG := LastTradeInG + 1;
        UNTIL SalTradeInLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE PostTradeIn@5025360();
    VAR
      VendorLedgEntryL@1109400001 : Record 25;
      PurchInvoiceHeaderL@1109400000 : Record 122;
      PurchCreditMemoHeaderL@1109400003 : Record 124;
      TransferBalanceL@1109400002 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      LastTradeInG := 1;
      TradeInSetupG.FIND;

      REPEAT
      // Start PA042846
        IF SalesHeader."Document Type" <> SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN BEGIN
          VendorLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Document Type", VendorLedgEntryL."Document Type"::Invoice);
          IF PurchInvoiceHeaderL.GET(TradeInApplCodeG[LastTradeInG]) THEN
            TransferBalanceL := PurchInvoiceHeaderL."Transfer Balance";
        END ELSE BEGIN
          VendorLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Document Type", VendorLedgEntryL."Document Type"::"Credit Memo");
          IF  PurchCreditMemoHeaderL.GET(TradeInApplCodeG[LastTradeInG]) THEN
            TransferBalanceL := PurchCreditMemoHeaderL."Transfer Balance";
        END;
      // Stop PA042846
        VendorLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Document No.",TradeInApplCodeG[LastTradeInG]);
      // Start PA032990
        IF NOT VendorLedgEntryL.FINDFIRST THEN
      // Stop PA032990
          ERROR(C_INC005, VendorLedgEntryL.TABLECAPTION, TradeInApplCodeG[LastTradeInG]);
      // Start PA032441
        VendorLedgEntryL.CALCFIELDS("Remaining Amount","Remaining Amt. (LCY)");
      // Stop PA032441

      // Start PA042846
        IF (VendorLedgEntryL."Remaining Amt. (LCY)" <> 0) AND TransferBalanceL THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA042846
          //Debitorposten ausgleichen
          GenJnlLine.INIT;
          GenJnlLine."Posting Date" := SalesHeader."Posting Date";
          GenJnlLine."Document Date" := SalesHeader."Document Date";
          GenJnlLine."Account Type" := GenJnlLine."Account Type"::Customer;
          GenJnlLine.VALIDATE("Account No.", SalesHeader."Bill-to Customer No.");
      // Start PA032441
          GenJnlLine."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
          GenJnlLine."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code";
      // Stop PA032441
      // Start EU.0147204.145948
          GenJnlLine."Currency Code" := SalesHeader."Currency Code";
          GenJnlLine."Source Currency Code" := SalesHeader."Currency Code";
          IF SalesHeader."Currency Code" = '' THEN
            GenJnlLine."Currency Factor" := 1
          ELSE
            GenJnlLine."Currency Factor" := SalesHeader."Currency Factor";
      // Stop EU.0147204.145948
      // Start EU.0148673.149899
          GenJnlLine."Source Code" := SrcCode;
      // Stop EU.0148673.149899
          GenJnlLine."Document No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
          GenJnlLine.VALIDATE(Amount,VendorLedgEntryL."Remaining Amount");
          GenJnlLine.VALIDATE("Amount (LCY)",VendorLedgEntryL."Remaining Amt. (LCY)");
          GenJnlLine."Bal. Account Type" := GenJnlLine."Bal. Account Type"::"G/L Account";
          GenJnlLine."Bal. Account No." := TradeInSetupG."Appl. Interim Acc. No.";
          IF TradeInSetupG."Application Text" <> '' THEN
            GenJnlLine.Description := TradeInSetupG."Application Text";
          IF SalesHeader."Document Type" <> SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN
            GenJnlLine."Applies-to Doc. Type" := GenJnlLine."Applies-to Doc. Type"::Invoice
          ELSE
            GenJnlLine."Applies-to Doc. Type" := GenJnlLine."Applies-to Doc. Type"::"Credit Memo";
          GenJnlLine."Applies-to Doc. No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
          GenJnlLine."Branch Code" := CurrBranchCodeG;
          GenJnlLine."Main Area" := DetermineMainArea(SalesHeader."Order Type");
      // Start EU.0106909.117581
          OnBeforePostTradeInWithTransferBalance(GenJnlLine,SalesHeader);
      // Stop EU.0106909.117581
          GenJnlPostLine.RUN(GenJnlLine);

          //Kreditorenposten ausgleichen
          GenJnlLine.INIT;
          GenJnlLine."Posting Date" := SalesHeader."Posting Date";
          GenJnlLine."Document Date" := SalesHeader."Document Date";
          GenJnlLine."Account Type" := GenJnlLine."Account Type"::Vendor;
          GenJnlLine.VALIDATE("Account No.", VendorLedgEntryL."Vendor No.");
      // Start PA032441
          GenJnlLine."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := VendorLedgEntryL."Global Dimension 1 Code";
          GenJnlLine."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := VendorLedgEntryL."Global Dimension 2 Code";
      // Stop PA032441
      // Start EU.0147204.145948
          GenJnlLine."Currency Code" := SalesHeader."Currency Code";
          GenJnlLine."Source Currency Code" := SalesHeader."Currency Code";
          IF SalesHeader."Currency Code" = '' THEN
            GenJnlLine."Currency Factor" := 1
          ELSE
            GenJnlLine."Currency Factor" := SalesHeader."Currency Factor";
      // Stop EU.0147204.145948
      // Start EU.0148673.149899
          GenJnlLine."Source Code" := SrcCode;
      // Stop EU.0148673.149899
          GenJnlLine."Document No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
          GenJnlLine.VALIDATE(Amount,- VendorLedgEntryL."Remaining Amount");
          GenJnlLine.VALIDATE("Amount (LCY)",- VendorLedgEntryL."Remaining Amt. (LCY)");
          GenJnlLine."Bal. Account Type" := GenJnlLine."Bal. Account Type"::"G/L Account";
          GenJnlLine."Bal. Account No." := TradeInSetupG."Appl. Interim Acc. No.";
          IF TradeInSetupG."Application Text" <> '' THEN
            GenJnlLine.Description := TradeInSetupG."Application Text";
          IF SalesHeader."Document Type" <> SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN
            GenJnlLine."Applies-to Doc. Type" := GenJnlLine."Applies-to Doc. Type"::Invoice
          ELSE
            GenJnlLine."Applies-to Doc. Type" := GenJnlLine."Applies-to Doc. Type"::"Credit Memo";
          GenJnlLine."Applies-to Doc. No." := VendorLedgEntryL."Document No.";
          GenJnlLine."Branch Code" := CurrBranchCodeG;
          GenJnlLine."Main Area" := DetermineMainArea(SalesHeader."Order Type");
      // Start EU.0106909.117581
          OnBeforePostTradeIn(GenJnlLine,SalesHeader);
      // Stop EU.0106909.117581
          GenJnlPostLine.RUN(GenJnlLine);
        END;

        LastTradeInG := LastTradeInG + 1;
      UNTIL TradeInApplCodeG[LastTradeInG] = '';
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckOption@5025361();
    VAR
      VehicleOptionL@1109400000 : Record 5025422;
      CheckSalLineL@1109400001 : Record 37;
      OptionVariantL@1109400002 : Record 5025424;
      MissingOptionsL@1109400003 : Integer;
      TooManyOptionsL@1109400005 : Integer;
      OptionTooManyErrorL@1109400006 : Text[250];
      OptionMissingErrorL@1109400007 : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Area, OptionVariantL.Area::Sale);
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Type", SalesLine."Document Type");
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document No.", SalesLine."Document No.");
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", SalesLine."Line No.");

      CheckSalLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.",Type,"No.");
      CheckSalLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesLine."Document Type");
      CheckSalLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesLine."Document No.");

      MissingOptionsL := 0;
      TooManyOptionsL := 0;

      VehicleOptionL.SETRANGE(VIN, SalesLine.VIN);
      VehicleOptionL.SETFILTER("Copy-to Setting",'<>%1', VehicleOptionL."Copy-to Setting"::"Do Not Copy");
      VehicleOptionL.SETFILTER(Type,'<>%1', VehicleOptionL.Type::Vehicle);
      IF VehicleOptionL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          IF VehicleOptionL."Copy-to Setting" = VehicleOptionL."Copy-to Setting"::Copy THEN BEGIN
            OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Type, VehicleOptionL.Type);
            OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Option Code", VehicleOptionL."Option Code");
            OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Internal Code", VehicleOptionL."Internal Code");
            IF NOT OptionVariantL.FINDFIRST THEN
              MissingOptionsL := MissingOptionsL + 1;
          END;
        UNTIL VehicleOptionL.NEXT = 0;

      VehicleOptionL.SETRANGE("Copy-to Setting", VehicleOptionL."Copy-to Setting"::Copy);
      OptionVariantL.SETFILTER(Type,'<>%1', OptionVariantL.Type::Vehicle);
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Option Code");
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Internal Code");
      IF OptionVariantL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          VehicleOptionL.SETRANGE("Option Code", OptionVariantL."Option Code");
          VehicleOptionL.SETRANGE("Internal Code", OptionVariantL."Internal Code");
          IF NOT VehicleOptionL.FINDFIRST THEN
            TooManyOptionsL := TooManyOptionsL + 1;
        UNTIL OptionVariantL.NEXT = 0;
      IF TooManyOptionsL > 0 THEN
        IF TooManyOptionsL = 1 THEN
          OptionTooManyErrorL := C_INC032
        ELSE
          OptionTooManyErrorL := STRSUBSTNO(C_INC033, TooManyOptionsL);
      IF MissingOptionsL > 0 THEN
        IF MissingOptionsL = 1 THEN
          OptionMissingErrorL := C_INC030
        ELSE
          OptionMissingErrorL := STRSUBSTNO(C_INC031, MissingOptionsL);
      IF (TooManyOptionsL > 0) OR (MissingOptionsL > 0) THEN
        IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC006 + OptionMissingErrorL + OptionTooManyErrorL + C_INC010, TRUE,
           SalesLine.TABLECAPTION,
           SalesLine."Document Type",
           SalesLine."Document No.",
           SalesLine."Line No.")
        THEN
          ERROR(C_INC011);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CopyOrderPriceCalc@5025364(InDocumentP@1109400000 : 'Invoice,Credit Memo');
    VAR
      OrderItemPriceCalcL@1109400001 : Record 5025809;
      InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL@1109400002 : Record 5025819;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      OrderItemPriceCalcL.RESET;
      OrderItemPriceCalcL.SETRANGE("Order Type",OrderItemPriceCalcL."Order Type"::"Sales Order");
      OrderItemPriceCalcL.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
      OrderItemPriceCalcL.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
      OrderItemPriceCalcL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",SalesLine."Line No.");
      // Start PA035134
      IF OrderItemPriceCalcL.FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA035134
        REPEAT
          InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL.INIT;
          InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL.TRANSFERFIELDS(OrderItemPriceCalcL);
          CASE InDocumentP OF
            InDocumentP::Invoice:
              BEGIN
                InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL."Document Type" := InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL."Document Type"::Invoice;
                InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL."Document No." := SalesInvHeader."No.";
                InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL."Document Line No." := SalesInvLine."Line No.";
              END;
            InDocumentP::"Credit Memo":
              BEGIN
                InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL."Document Type" := InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL."Document Type"::"Credit Memo";
                InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL."Document No." := SalesCrMemoHeader."No.";
                InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL."Document Line No." := SalesCrMemoLine."Line No.";
              END;
          END;
          InPostedOrderItemPriceCalcL.INSERT;
        UNTIL OrderItemPriceCalcL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CopyDiffTaxText@5025362(FromDocumentTypeP@1109400000 : Integer;ToDocumentTypeP@1109400001 : Integer;FromNumberP@1109400002 : Code[20];ToNumberP@1109400003 : Code[20]);
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      SalDiffTextG.SETRANGE("Document Type",FromDocumentTypeP);
      SalDiffTextG.SETRANGE("Document No.",FromNumberP);
      // Start PA035134
      IF SalDiffTextG.FINDSET THEN
      // Stop PA035134
        REPEAT
          PostedSalDiffTextG.TRANSFERFIELDS(SalDiffTextG);
          PostedSalDiffTextG."Document Type" := ToDocumentTypeP;
          PostedSalDiffTextG."Document No." := ToNumberP;
          PostedSalDiffTextG.INSERT;
        UNTIL SalDiffTextG.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE BookNoToTradeIn@5025363();
    VAR
      VehicleLedgEntryL@1109400000 : Record 5025405;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      VehicleLedgEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Trade-In for VIN","Trade-In for Document No.");
      VehicleLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Trade-In for VIN", SalesLine.VIN);
      VehicleLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Trade-In for Document No.", SalesLine."Document No.");
      IF VehicleLedgEntryL.FINDFIRST THEN
      // Start PA032441
        VehicleLedgEntryL.MODIFYALL("Trade-In for Book No.", SalesLine."Book No.");
      // Stop PA032441
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineMainArea@5025365(ForModuleP@1109400000 : Integer) : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      CASE ForModuleP OF
        SalesHeader."Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
          EXIT(GenJnlLine."Main Area"::"Parts Sales & Purchases");
        SalesHeader."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
          EXIT(GenJnlLine."Main Area"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases");
        SalesHeader."Order Type"::Service:
          EXIT(GenJnlLine."Main Area"::Service);
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE ResetOptionsInOwnInvoice@5025366(SalesHdrP@1109400000 : Record 36;SalesLineP@1109400001 : Record 37);
    VAR
      SalesInvoiceLineL@1109400002 : Record 113;
      OptionVariantL@1109400003 : Record 5025424;
      VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL@1109400004 : Record 5025464;
      SalesHdrL@1109400005 : Record 36;
      SalesLineL@1109400006 : Record 37;
      VehicleL@1109400007 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF (SalesHdrP."Applies-to Doc. Type" = SalesHdrP."Applies-to Doc. Type"::Invoice) AND
         (SalesHdrP."Applies-to Doc. No." <> '')
      THEN BEGIN
        SalesInvoiceLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type", "From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.",
          "From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line", "From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type",
          "From Veh. Option Inv. No.", "From Veh. Opt.Inv. IntCode");

        SalesInvoiceLineL.SETRANGE("From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type", SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type");
        SalesInvoiceLineL.SETRANGE("From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.", SalesLineP."From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.");
        SalesInvoiceLineL.SETRANGE("From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line", SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line");
        SalesInvoiceLineL.SETRANGE("From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type", SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type");
        SalesInvoiceLineL.SETRANGE("From Veh. Option Inv. No.", SalesLineP."From Veh. Option Inv. No.");
        SalesInvoiceLineL.SETRANGE("From Veh. Opt.Inv. IntCode", SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. IntCode");
      // Start PA032990
        IF SalesInvoiceLineL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032990
          IF (SalesInvoiceLineL.Amount = SalesLineP.Amount) AND
             (SalesHdrP."Applies-to Doc. Type" = SalesHdrP."Applies-to Doc. Type"::Invoice) AND
             (SalesHdrP."Applies-to Doc. No." <> '')
          THEN BEGIN
            IF VehicleL.GET(SalesLineP.VIN) THEN BEGIN
              IF OptionVariantL.GET(OptionVariantL.Area::Sale,
                 OptionVariantL."Document Type"::"Purch. Order/Order",
                 SalesLineP."From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.",
                 SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line",
                 OptionVariantL.Type::"Manuf. Option",
                 SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code",
                 VehicleL."Model No.",
                 SalesLineP."From Veh. Option Inv. No.",
                 SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. IntCode")
              THEN BEGIN
                OptionVariantL.Quantity := SalesLineP.Quantity;
                OptionVariantL.VALIDATE("Unit Price", SalesLineP."Unit Price");
                OptionVariantL.MODIFY;
              END;
            END;
            VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.",
              "Document Line No.",Type,"No.","Internal Code");
            VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.SETRANGE("Document Type", VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL."Document Type"::Order);
            VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.SETRANGE("Document No.", SalesLineP."From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.");
            VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line");
            VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.SETRANGE(Type, SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type");
            VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.SETRANGE("No.", SalesLineP."From Veh. Option Inv. No.");
            VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.SETRANGE("Internal Code", SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. IntCode");
            IF VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              IF SalesHdrL.GET(SalesHdrL."Document Type"::Order,SalesLineP."From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.") THEN BEGIN
                VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL."Bill-to Customer No." := SalesHdrL."Bill-to Customer No.";
                VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL."Bill-to Name" := SalesHdrL."Bill-to Name";
                VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL."Bill-to Name 2" := SalesHdrL."Bill-to Name 2";
                VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL."Bill-to Address" := SalesHdrL."Bill-to Address";
                VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL."Bill-to Address 2" := SalesHdrL."Bill-to Address 2";
                VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL."Bill-to City" := SalesHdrL."Bill-to City";
                VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL."Bill-to Contact" := SalesHdrL."Bill-to Contact";
                VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL."Bill-to Post Code" := SalesHdrL."Bill-to Post Code";
              END;
              VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL."Separate Invoice for Line" := FALSE;
              VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.Amount := SalesLineP.Amount;
              VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.VALIDATE("Unit Price", SalesLineP."Unit Price");
              VehicleOrderOptionInvoiceL.MODIFY;
              IF (SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type" = SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::"Own Option") OR
                 (SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type" = SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::"Veh. Transfer") OR
                 (SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type" = SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::Item) OR
                 (SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type" = SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::"G/L Account")
              THEN BEGIN
                IF SalesLineL.GET(SalesLineL."Document Type"::Order,
                   SalesLineP."From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.",
                   SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line")
                THEN BEGIN
                  SalesLineL.Quantity := SalesLineL.Quantity + SalesLineP.Quantity;
                  SalesLineL."Quantity (Base)" := SalesLineL."Quantity (Base)" + SalesLineP."Quantity (Base)";
                  SalesLineL."Quantity Shipped" := SalesLineL."Quantity Shipped" - SalesLineP."Quantity Shipped";
                  SalesLineL."Qty. Shipped (Base)" := SalesLineL."Qty. Shipped (Base)" -
                    SalesLineP."Qty. Shipped (Base)";

                  SalesLineL."Quantity Invoiced" := SalesLineL."Quantity Invoiced" - SalesLineP."Quantity Invoiced";
                  SalesLineL."Qty. Invoiced (Base)" := SalesLineL."Qty. Invoiced (Base)" -
                    SalesLineP."Qty. Invoiced (Base)";

                  SalesLineL."Outstanding Quantity" := SalesLineL."Outstanding Quantity" + SalesLineP.Quantity;
                  SalesLineL."Outstanding Qty. (Base)" := SalesLineL."Outstanding Qty. (Base)" +
                    SalesLineP."Quantity (Base)";
                  SalesLineL."Qty. to Ship" := SalesLineL."Qty. to Ship" + SalesLineP.Quantity;
                  SalesLineL."Qty. to Ship (Base)" := SalesLineL."Qty. to Ship (Base)" + SalesLineP."Quantity (Base)";
                  SalesLineL."Qty. to Invoice" := SalesLineL."Qty. to Invoice" + SalesLineP.Quantity;
                  SalesLineL."Qty. to Invoice (Base)" := SalesLineL."Qty. to Invoice (Base)" + SalesLineP."Quantity (Base)";

                  SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Unit Price", SalesLineP."Unit Price");
                  SalesLineL.MODIFY;
                END;
              END;

              IF SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type" = SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::"Manufacturer Option" THEN BEGIN
                IF SalesLineL.GET(SalesLineL."Document Type"::Order,
                   SalesLineP."From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No.",
                   SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line")
                THEN BEGIN

                  SalesLineL.VALIDATE("Unit Price", SalesLineL."Unit Price" + SalesLineP."Unit Price");
                  SalesLineL.MODIFY;
                END;
              END;

            END;
            SalesInvoiceLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type" := SalesInvoiceLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Type"::"0";
            SalesInvoiceLineL."From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No." := '';
            SalesInvoiceLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Doc. Line" := 0;
            SalesInvoiceLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type" :=
              SalesInvoiceLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::"Manufacturer Option";
            SalesInvoiceLineL."From Veh. Option Inv. No." := '';
            SalesInvoiceLineL."From Veh. Opt.Inv. IntCode" := '';
            SalesInvoiceLineL.MODIFY;
          END;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckTaxFromPurchase@5025368();
    VAR
      VehicleL@1109400000 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF (SalesLine."Order Type" = SalesLine."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND
         (SalesLine."Line No." <> 0)
      THEN BEGIN
        IF VehicleL.GET(SalesLine.VIN) THEN BEGIN
          VATPostingSetupG.GET(VehicleL."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)",VehicleL."VAT Prod. Posting Group");
          IF ((VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type" = VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT") AND
             (SalesLine."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLine."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax"))
          THEN
            ERROR(C_INC037);
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetDescriptionTranslation@1109400000();
    VAR
      ItemTranslationL@1109400000 : Record 30;
      DescriptionL@1109400001 : Text[50];
      Description2L@1109400002 : Text[50];
      PriceStickerLineL@1109400003 : Record 5025433;
      PriceStickerL@1109400004 : Record 5025432;
      OptionTranslationL@1109400005 : Record 5025500;
      VehicleOptionL@1109400006 : Record 5025422;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF SalesHeader."Language Code" = '' THEN
        EXIT;
      PriceStickerL.SETRANGE(VIN,SalesLine.VIN);
      PriceStickerL.SETRANGE("Vehicle Book No.",SalesLine."Book No.");
      // Start PA032990
      IF PriceStickerL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032990
        PriceStickerLineL.SETRANGE(VIN, SalesLine.VIN);
        PriceStickerLineL.SETRANGE("Vehicle Book No.",SalesLine."Book No.");
        PriceStickerLineL.SETRANGE("Vehicle Price Sticker No.",PriceStickerL."Line No.");
      // Start PA032990
        IF PriceStickerLineL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
      // Stop PA032990
          REPEAT
            DescriptionL := '';
            Description2L := '';

            CASE PriceStickerLineL.Type OF
              PriceStickerLineL.Type::Vehicle :
                IF ItemTranslationL.GET(PriceStickerLineL."Model No.",SalesLine."Variant Code",SalesHeader."Language Code") THEN BEGIN
                  DescriptionL := ItemTranslationL.Description;
                  Description2L := ItemTranslationL."Description 2";
                END;
