              PriceStickerLineL.Type::"Manuf. Option" :
                IF OptionTranslationL.GET(PriceStickerLineL."Make Code",PriceStickerLineL."Model No.",
                   PriceStickerLineL."Option Code",PriceStickerLineL."Internal Code",
                   SalesHeader."Language Code")
                THEN BEGIN
                  DescriptionL := OptionTranslationL.Description;
                  Description2L := OptionTranslationL."Description 2";
                END;
            END;

            IF (DescriptionL <> '') OR (Description2L <> '') THEN BEGIN
              PriceStickerLineL."Description Document Language" := DescriptionL;
              PriceStickerLineL."Description2 Document Language" := Description2L;
              PriceStickerLineL.MODIFY;

              VehicleOptionL.RESET;
              VehicleOptionL.SETRANGE(VIN, PriceStickerLineL.VIN);
              VehicleOptionL.SETRANGE("Option Type", PriceStickerLineL."Option Type");
              VehicleOptionL.SETRANGE("Option Code", PriceStickerLineL."Option Code");
              VehicleOptionL.SETRANGE("Internal Code", PriceStickerLineL."Internal Code");

              IF VehicleOptionL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                VehicleOptionL."Description Document Language" := DescriptionL;
                VehicleOptionL."Description2 Document Language" := Description2L;
                VehicleOptionL.MODIFY;
              END;
            END;
          UNTIL PriceStickerLineL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE PostInternalInvoice@1109400006();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF NOT InternalCustomerG THEN
        EXIT;
      ServiceSetupG.GET;
      IF NOT ServiceSetupG."Automatic Internal Charging" THEN
        EXIT;
      IntDocPostG.SetGenJnlPostLine(GenJnlPostLine);
      IntDocPostG.PostServBuffer(SalesHeader);
      IntDocPostG.GetGenJnlPostLine(GenJnlPostLine);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE PostVehicleJnlLine@1109400012(VAR SalesHeaderP@1109400000 : Record 36;VAR SalesLineP@1109400006 : Record 37;QtyToBeShippedP@1109400005 : Decimal;QtyToBeShippedBaseP@1109400002 : Decimal;QtyToBeInvoicedP@1109400003 : Decimal;QtyToBeInvoicedBaseP@1109400004 : Decimal;VAR ItemLedgShptEntryNoP@1109400001 : Integer);
    VAR
      VehJnlLineL@1109400008 : Record 5025403;
      LocationL@1109400007 : Record 14;
      VehicleL@1055600 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF (SalesLineP.VIN = '') OR (SalesLineP."Item Type" = SalesLineP."Item Type"::"Charge (Item)") OR
         ((SalesLineP."Item Type" = SalesLineP."Item Type"::"G/L Account") AND (QtyToBeInvoicedP = 0)) OR
         ((QtyToBeShippedP = 0) AND (QtyToBeInvoicedP = 0))
      THEN
        EXIT;

      IF SalesLine."Item Type" = SalesLine."Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA041187.89985
        CheckTradeIn();
      // Stop PA041187.89985
        CheckOption();
        GetDescriptionTranslation();
      END;

      VehJnlLineL.INIT;
      VehJnlLineL."Posting Date" := SalesHeaderP."Posting Date";
      VehJnlLineL."Book No." := SalesLineP."Book No.";
      VehJnlLineL."Branch Book No." := SalesLineP."Branch Book No.";
      VehJnlLineL."Document Date" := SalesHeaderP."Document Date";
      VehJnlLineL."Location Code" := SalesLineP."Location Code";
      VehJnlLineL."Department Code" := SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      VehJnlLineL."Make Code" := SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code";
      // Start PA035597
      VehJnlLineL."Dimension Set ID" := SalesLineP."Dimension Set ID";
      // Stop PA035597
      VehJnlLineL."Reason Code" := SalesHeaderP."Reason Code";
      VehJnlLineL.VIN := SalesLineP.VIN;
      IF IsImporter THEN
        VehJnlLineL."Factory No." := SalesLineP."Factory No.";
      VehJnlLineL."License No." := SalesLineP."License No.";
      VehJnlLineL.Type := SalesLineType2VehJrnLineType(SalesLineP);
      // Start EU.0021797
      IF SalesLineP."Vehicle Status" <> SalesLineP."Vehicle Status"::" " THEN
        VehJnlLineL."Vehicle Status" := SalesLineP."Vehicle Status" -1
      ELSE
        IF VehicleL.GET(VehJnlLineL.VIN) AND
           (SalesHeaderP."Order Type" = SalesHeaderP."Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases")
        THEN
          VehJnlLineL."Vehicle Status" := VehicleL."Vehicle Status";
      // Stop EU.0021797
      VehJnlLineL."No." := SalesLineP."No.";
      VehJnlLineL."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" := SalesLineP."Gen. Prod. Posting Group";
      VehJnlLineL."VAT Calculation Type" := SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type";
      VehJnlLineL."VAT Prod. Posting Group" := SalesLineP."VAT Prod. Posting Group";
      VehJnlLineL."Gen. Bus. Posting Group" := SalesLineP."Gen. Bus. Posting Group";
      VehJnlLineL."VAT Bus. Posting Group" := SalesLineP."VAT Bus. Posting Group";
      VehJnlLineL."Variant Code" := SalesLineP."Variant Code";
      VehJnlLineL.Description := SalesLineP.Description;
      VehJnlLineL."Department Code" := SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      VehJnlLineL."Make Code" := SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code";
      // Start PA035597
      VehJnlLineL."Dimension Set ID" := SalesLineP."Dimension Set ID";
      // Stop PA035597
      VehJnlLineL."Salespers./Purch. Code" := SalesHeader."Salesperson Code";
      // Start PA036728
      VehJnlLineL."Salesperson Code 2" := SalesHeader."Salesperson Code 2";
      // Stop PA036728
      VehJnlLineL."Entry Type" := VehJnlLineL."Entry Type"::Sale;

      IF QtyToBeInvoicedP <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        VehJnlLineL."Document No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
        VehJnlLineL."External Document No." := GenJnlLineExtDocNo;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF SalesHeaderP."Document Type" IN [
           SalesHeaderP."Document Type"::"Return Order",
           SalesHeaderP."Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]
        THEN BEGIN
          VehJnlLineL."Document No." := ReturnRcptHeader."No.";
          VehJnlLineL."External Document No." := ReturnRcptHeader."External Document No.";
        END ELSE BEGIN
          VehJnlLineL."Document No." := SalesShptHeader."No.";
          VehJnlLineL."External Document No." := SalesShptHeader."External Document No.";
        END;
      END;

      VehJnlLineL."Invoiced Quantity" := QtyToBeInvoicedBaseP;
      VehJnlLineL."Quantity Shipped" := QtyToBeShippedBaseP;

      VehJnlLineL."Unit Cost" := SalesLineP."Unit Cost (LCY)";
      VehJnlLineL."Total Cost" :=
        ROUND(SalesLineP."Unit Cost (LCY)" * ABS(QuantityCalc(QtyToBeInvoicedBaseP,QtyToBeShippedBaseP)));

      VehJnlLineL."Unit Price" := ROUND(ABS(SalesLineP.Amount) / ABS(SalesLineP."Quantity (Base)"));
      VehJnlLineL."Total Price" := VehJnlLineL."Unit Price" * QtyToBeInvoicedBaseP;
      // Start EU.0092205
      OnInside1PostVehicleJnlLineEvent(VehJnlLineL,SalesHeaderP,SalesLineP);
      // Stop EU.0092205
      IF SalesLineP."Item Type" = SalesLineP."Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
        CLEAR(OptionVariantG);
      // Start PA035613
        OptionVariantG.RESET;
      // Stop PA035613
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantG.Area::Sale);
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeaderP."Document Type");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesLineP."Document No.");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",SalesLineP."Line No.");
      // Start PA032990
        IF OptionVariantG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032990
          OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Type,OptionVariantG.Type::Vehicle);
      // Start PA032990
          IF OptionVariantG.FINDFIRST THEN
      // Stop PA032990
            VehJnlLineL."Vehicle Portion" := OptionVariantG."Amount (LCY)" * QtyToBeInvoicedBaseP;
          OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Type, OptionVariantG.Type::"Manuf. Option");
          OptionVariantG.CALCSUMS("Amount (LCY)");
          VehJnlLineL."Manuf. Option Portion" := OptionVariantG."Amount (LCY)" * QtyToBeInvoicedBaseP;
          OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Type, OptionVariantG.Type::"3");
          OptionVariantG.CALCSUMS("Amount (LCY)");
          VehJnlLineL."Own Option Portion" := OptionVariantG."Amount (LCY)" * QtyToBeInvoicedBaseP;
          VehJnlLineL."Misc. Portion" := VehJnlLineL."Total Price" - VehJnlLineL."Vehicle Portion" -
            VehJnlLineL."Manuf. Option Portion" - VehJnlLineL."Own Option Portion";
        END ELSE BEGIN
          VehJnlLineL."Vehicle Portion" := VehJnlLineL."Total Price" * QtyToBeInvoicedBaseP;
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF SalesLineP."Unit Price" < 0 THEN
          VehJnlLineL."Total Price" := -VehJnlLineL."Total Price";
        IF SalesLineP."Item Type" = SalesLineP."Item Type"::"Own Option" THEN
          VehJnlLineL."Own Option Portion" := VehJnlLineL."Total Price"
        ELSE
          IF SalesLineP."Item Type" = SalesLineP."Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer" THEN
            VehJnlLineL."Veh. Transfer Portion" := VehJnlLineL."Total Price"
          ELSE
            VehJnlLineL."Misc. Portion" := VehJnlLineL."Total Price";
      END;

      IF (SalesLineP."From Veh. Option Inv. Doc. No." <> '') AND
         (SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type" = SalesLineP."From Veh. Opt.Inv. Line Type"::"Manufacturer Option")
      THEN BEGIN
        VehJnlLineL."Misc. Portion" := 0;
        VehJnlLineL."Vehicle Portion" := 0;
        VehJnlLineL."Own Option Portion" := 0;
        VehJnlLineL."Veh. Transfer Portion" := 0;
        VehJnlLineL."Manuf. Option Portion" := VehJnlLineL."Total Price";
      END;
      // Start PA032441
      VehJnlLineL."Source Code" := SrcCode;
      // Stop PA032441
      VehJnlLineL."Posting No. Series" := SalesHeaderP."Posting No. Series";

      VehJnlLineL."Credit Memo" := SalesLineP."Document Type" IN
        [SalesLineP."Document Type"::"Return Order",SalesLineP."Document Type"::"Credit Memo"];
      VehJnlLineL."Source Type" := VehJnlLineL."Source Type"::Customer;
      VehJnlLineL."Source No." := SalesHeaderP."Sell-to Customer No.";
      VehJnlLineL."Source No. (Payment)" := SalesLineP."Bill-to Customer No.";
      VehJnlLineL."Source Group Code" := CustG."Customer Group Code";
      // Start PA038126
      // Start EU.0041636
      // Stop EU.0041636
      // Stop PA038126
      CASE SalesLineP."Order Type" OF
        SalesLineP."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
          VehJnlLineL."Main Area" := VehJnlLineL."Main Area"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases";
        SalesLineP."Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
          VehJnlLineL."Main Area" := VehJnlLineL."Main Area"::"Parts Sales & Purchases";
        SalesLineP."Order Type"::Service:
          VehJnlLineL."Main Area" := VehJnlLineL."Main Area"::Service;
      END;

      VehJnlLineL."Document Type" := VehJnlLineL."Document Type"::External;
      VehJnlLineL."Main Customer" := TRUE;
      IF (SalesHeaderP."Document Type" = SalesHeaderP."Document Type"::Invoice) AND
         (SalesLineP."Service Order No." <> '') AND
         (SalesLineP."Service Order Line No." <> 0)
      THEN BEGIN
        IF ServiceLineG.GET(ServiceLineG."Document Type"::Order,SalesLineP."Service Order No.",
           SalesLineP."Service Order Line No.")
        THEN BEGIN
          IF ServiceLineG."Bill-to Customer No." <> SalesLineP."Bill-to Customer No." THEN
            VehJnlLineL."Main Customer" := FALSE;
          CASE ServiceLineG.Type OF
            ServiceLineG.Type::Item:
              VehJnlLineL."Line Type" := VehJnlLineL."Line Type"::Item;
            ServiceLineG.Type::Labor:
              VehJnlLineL."Line Type" := VehJnlLineL."Line Type"::Labor;
            ServiceLineG.Type::"Ext. Service":
              VehJnlLineL."Line Type" := VehJnlLineL."Line Type"::"Ext. Service";
            ServiceLineG.Type::"G/L Account":
              VehJnlLineL."Line Type" := VehJnlLineL."Line Type"::"G/L Account";
          END;
          VehJnlLineL."Assoc. No." := ServiceLineG."No.";
          VehJnlLineL."Service Order No." := ServiceLineG."Document No.";
          VehJnlLineL."Service Order Line No." := ServiceLineG."Line No.";
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        VehJnlLineL."Line Type" := SalesLineIType2VehJrnLineLType(SalesLineP);
        VehJnlLineL."Assoc. No." := SalesLineP."No.";
      END;
      VehJnlLineL."Branch Code" := CurrBranchCodeG;
      // Start PA032990.BMW
      IF LocationL.GET(SalesLine."Location Code") THEN
        VehJnlLineL."Branch Code" := LocationL."Branch Code"
      ELSE
        VehJnlLineL."Branch Code" := CurrBranchCodeG;
      // Stop PA032990.BMW

      // Start EU.0038938
      IF SalesLineP."Document Type" IN [SalesLineP."Document Type"::"Credit Memo", SalesLineP."Document Type"::"Return Order"] THEN BEGIN
        VehJnlLineL."To Parking Lot" := SalesLineP."Parking Lot";
        VehJnlLineL."To Parking Bay" :=  SalesLineP."Parking Bay";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        VehJnlLineL."From Parking Lot" := SalesLineP."Parking Lot";
        VehJnlLineL."From Parking Bay" :=  SalesLineP."Parking Bay";
      END;
      // Stop EU.0038938

      VehJnlLineL."Item Ledger Entry No." := ItemLedgShptEntryNoP;
      ItemLedgShptEntryNoP := 0;
      IF Vehicle2G.GET(SalesLineP.VIN) THEN
        OldDateOfSaleG := Vehicle2G."Date of Sale";
      VehicleJnlLinePostG.RUN(VehJnlLineL);
      IF SalesLineP."Item Type" = SalesLineP."Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
        IF (SalesHeaderP."Document Type" = SalesHeaderP."Document Type"::"Credit Memo") OR
           (SalesHeaderP."Document Type" = SalesHeaderP."Document Type"::"Return Order")
        THEN
          ReactivateOption()
        ELSE BEGIN
          SetOptionToZero();
          BookNoToTradeIn();
        END;
        NoteTradeIn();
      END;
      // Stop INC
      // Start EU.0009764
      OnAfterPostVehicleJnlLineEvent(VehJnlLineL,SalesLineP);
      // Stop EU.0009764
    END;

    PROCEDURE SalesLineType2VehJrnLineType@1109400011(VAR SalesLineP@1109400000 : Record 37) : Integer;
    VAR
      VehicleJnlLineL@1109400001 : Record 5025403;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      CASE SalesLineP."Item Type" OF
        SalesLineP."Item Type"::Vehicle: EXIT(VehicleJnlLineL.Type::Vehicle);
      END;
      CASE SalesLineP.Type OF
        SalesLineP.Type::Item: EXIT(VehicleJnlLineL.Type::Item);
        SalesLineP.Type::"Account (G/L)": EXIT(VehicleJnlLineL.Type::"G/L Account");
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE SalesLineIType2VehJrnLineLType@1109400010(VAR SalesLineP@1109400000 : Record 37) : Integer;
    VAR
      VehicleJnlLineL@1109400001 : Record 5025403;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      CASE SalesLineP."Item Type" OF
        SalesLineP."Item Type"::Item: EXIT(VehicleJnlLineL."Line Type"::Item);
        SalesLineP."Item Type"::Vehicle: EXIT(VehicleJnlLineL."Line Type"::Vehicle);
        SalesLineP."Item Type"::"Own Option": EXIT(VehicleJnlLineL."Line Type"::"Own Option");
        SalesLineP."Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer": EXIT(VehicleJnlLineL."Line Type"::"Veh. Transfer");
        SalesLineP."Item Type"::"G/L Account": EXIT(VehicleJnlLineL."Line Type"::"G/L Account");
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE QuantityCalc@1109400042(QtyInvoiceP@1109400000 : Decimal;QtyShipmentP@1109400001 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF QtyInvoiceP <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(QtyInvoiceP);
      EXIT(QtyShipmentP);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateVehicleOwnOptions@1109400007(SalesLineP@1109400000 : Record 37);
    VAR
      VehicleOwnOptL@1109400001 : Record 5045386;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF ItemJnlLine."Item Type" <> ItemJnlLine."Item Type"::"Own Option" THEN
        EXIT;
      VehicleOwnOptL.RESET;
      VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE(VIN, SalesLineP.VIN);
      VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Option Code", SalesLineP."No.");
      VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Book No.", SalesLineP."Book No.");
      IF SalesLineP."Document Type" IN [
         SalesLineP."Document Type"::"Return Order",
         SalesLineP."Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]
      THEN BEGIN
        VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Sales Order No.", SalesLineP."Order No.");
        VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Sales Order Line No.", SalesLineP."Order Line No.");
      END ELSE BEGIN
        VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Sales Order No.", SalesLineP."Document No.");
        VehicleOwnOptL.SETRANGE("Sales Order Line No.", SalesLineP."Line No.");
      END;
      // Start PA032990
      IF VehicleOwnOptL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032990
        IF SalesLineP."Document Type" IN [
           SalesLineP."Document Type"::"Return Order",
           SalesLineP."Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]
        THEN BEGIN
          IF SalesLineP.Quantity > 0 THEN BEGIN
            IF (SalesLineP."Document Type" = SalesLineP."Document Type"::"Credit Memo") OR
               (SalesLineP."Quantity Invoiced" + SalesLineP."Qty. to Invoice" > 0)
            THEN BEGIN
              IF (VehicleOwnOptL."Service Order No." = '') AND (VehicleOwnOptL."Option Line No." = 0) THEN
                VehicleOwnOptL.DELETE
              ELSE BEGIN
                VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Posted" := FALSE;
                VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Order No." := '';
                VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Order Line No." := 0;
                VehicleOwnOptL.MODIFY(TRUE);
              END;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Posted" := FALSE;
              VehicleOwnOptL.MODIFY(TRUE);
            END;
          END ELSE
            IF SalesLineP.Quantity < 0 THEN BEGIN
              VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Posted" := TRUE;
              VehicleOwnOptL.MODIFY(TRUE);
            END;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          IF SalesLineP.Quantity < 0 THEN BEGIN
            IF (SalesLineP."Document Type" = SalesLineP."Document Type"::Invoice) OR
               (SalesLineP."Quantity Invoiced" + SalesLineP."Qty. to Invoice" <> 0)
            THEN BEGIN
              VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Posted" := FALSE;
              VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Order No." := '';
              VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Order Line No." := 0;
              IF (VehicleOwnOptL."Service Order No." = '') AND (VehicleOwnOptL."Option Line No." = 0) THEN
                VehicleOwnOptL.DELETE
              ELSE
                VehicleOwnOptL.MODIFY(TRUE);
            END;
          END ELSE
            IF SalesLineP.Quantity > 0 THEN BEGIN
              VehicleOwnOptL."Sales Posted" := TRUE;
              VehicleOwnOptL.MODIFY(TRUE)
            END;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE DelWtyClaims@1109400013();
    VAR
      WarrantyClaimHeaderL@1109400000 : Record 5025790;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF IsImporter THEN
        EXIT; // IMS does not delete warranty claims

      IF SalesHeader."Document Type" = SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN BEGIN
        WarrantyClaimHeaderL.SETCURRENTKEY(Status,VIN);
        WarrantyClaimHeaderL.SETRANGE(Status, WarrantyClaimHeaderL.Status::" ");
      // Start EU.0012448.13245
        WarrantyClaimHeaderL.SETRANGE("Service Order No.",SalesHeader."Service Order No.");
      // Stop EU.0012448.13245
        WarrantyClaimHeaderL.SETRANGE("Make Code",SalesHeader."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
      // Start PA032990
        IF NOT WarrantyClaimHeaderL.ISEMPTY THEN
      // Stop PA032990
          WarrantyClaimHeaderL.DELETEALL(TRUE);
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE ItemChargeAssignFind@1109400017(VAR SalesLineP@1109400000 : Record 37) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      ClearItemChargeAssgntFilter;
      TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETCURRENTKEY("Applies-to Doc. Type");
      TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETFILTER("Applies-to Doc. Type",'<>%1',SalesLineP."Document Type");
      TempItemChargeAssgntSales.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",SalesLineP."Line No.");
      // Start PA032990
      EXIT(TempItemChargeAssgntSales.FINDFIRST);
      // Stop PA032990
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdatePostBufferItemCharge@1109400016(VAR SalesLineP@1109400000 : Record 37;VAR SalesHeaderP@1109400001 : Record 36) : Boolean;
    VAR
      SalesLineTotalL@1109400004 : Record 37;
      SalesLineOrgTotalL@1109400003 : Record 37;
      ScrCurrLineTotalL@1109400006 : Record 37;
      ScrCurrLineOrgTotalL@1109400005 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF (SalesLineP.Type <> SalesLineP.Type::"Charge (Item)") OR
         (GLSetup."Charge (Item) Dimension" <> GLSetup."Charge (Item) Dimension"::"Item Ledger")
      THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      IF NOT ItemChargeAssignFind(SalesLineP) THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);

      CLEAR(InvPostingBuffer[1]);
      REPEAT
        CASE TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type" OF
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type"::Shipment:
            IF NOT PostBufferPerSalesShpt(
               SalesLineP,SalesHeaderP,SalesLineTotalL,SalesLineOrgTotalL,ScrCurrLineTotalL,ScrCurrLineOrgTotalL)
            THEN
              EXIT(FALSE);
          TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Type"::"Return Receipt":
            IF NOT PostBufferPerRetRcpt(
               SalesLineP,SalesHeaderP,SalesLineTotalL,SalesLineOrgTotalL,ScrCurrLineTotalL,ScrCurrLineOrgTotalL)
            THEN
              EXIT(FALSE);
        END;
      UNTIL TempItemChargeAssgntSales.NEXT = 0;
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE PostBufferPerSalesShpt@1109400023(SalesLineP@1109400006 : Record 37;SalesHeaderP@1109400005 : Record 36;VAR SalesLineTotalP@1109400004 : Record 37;VAR SalesLineOrgTotalP@1109400003 : Record 37;VAR ScrCurrLineTotalP@1109400001 : Record 37;VAR ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP@1109400000 : Record 37) : Boolean;
    VAR
      ItemLedgerEntryL@1109400002 : Record 32;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA035979
      IF NOT SalesShptLine.GET(TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No.",TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No.") THEN
      // Stop PA035979
        EXIT(FALSE);
      // Start PA031882
      // Stop PA031882
      IF NOT ItemLedgerEntryL.GET(SalesShptLine."Item Shpt. Entry No.") THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);

      SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := ItemLedgerEntryL."Global Dimension 1 Code";
      SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := ItemLedgerEntryL."Global Dimension 2 Code";

      PostBufferItemCharge(SalesLineP,SalesHeaderP,SalesLineTotalP,SalesLineOrgTotalP,ScrCurrLineTotalP,ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP);
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE PostBufferPerRetRcpt@1109400024(SalesLineP@1109400007 : Record 37;SalesHeaderP@1109400006 : Record 36;VAR SalesLineTotalP@1109400005 : Record 37;VAR SalesLineOrgTotalP@1109400004 : Record 37;VAR ScrCurrLineTotalP@1109400001 : Record 37;VAR ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP@1109400000 : Record 37) : Boolean;
    VAR
      ItemLedgerEntryL@1109400002 : Record 32;
      ReturnRcptLineL@1109400003 : Record 6661;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF NOT ReturnRcptLineL.GET(
         TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. No.",TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Applies-to Doc. Line No.")
      THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      // Start PA031882
      // Stop PA031882
      IF NOT ItemLedgerEntryL.GET(ReturnRcptLineL."Item Rcpt. Entry No.") THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);

      SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := ItemLedgerEntryL."Global Dimension 1 Code";
      SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := ItemLedgerEntryL."Global Dimension 2 Code";

      PostBufferItemCharge(SalesLineP,SalesHeaderP,SalesLineTotalP,SalesLineOrgTotalP,ScrCurrLineTotalP,ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP);
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE PostBufferItemCharge@1109400026(SalesLineP@1109400007 : Record 37;SalesHeaderP@1109400006 : Record 36;VAR SalesLineTotalP@1109400005 : Record 37;VAR SalesLineOrgTotalP@1109400004 : Record 37;VAR ScrCurrLineTotalP@1109400001 : Record 37;VAR ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP@1109400000 : Record 37) : Boolean;
    VAR
      SrcCurrSalesLineL@1109400003 : Record 37;
      FactorL@1109400002 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      FactorL := TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Qty. to Assign" / TempSalesLine."Qty. to Invoice";

      SalesLineP.Amount := SalesLineP.Amount * FactorL;
      SalesLineP."Amount Including VAT" := SalesLineP."Amount Including VAT" * FactorL;
      SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" := SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" * FactorL;
      SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base" := SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base" * FactorL;
      SalesLineP."Inv. Discount Amount" := SalesLineP."Inv. Discount Amount" * FactorL;
      SalesLineP."Line Discount Amount" := SalesLineP."Line Discount Amount" * FactorL;

      IncrementAmtPostItemCharge(SalesLineOrgTotalP,SalesLineP);

      SalesLineP.Amount :=
        ROUND(SalesLineOrgTotalP.Amount,GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision") - SalesLineTotalP.Amount;
      SalesLineP."Amount Including VAT" :=
        ROUND(SalesLineOrgTotalP."Amount Including VAT",GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision") -
        SalesLineTotalP."Amount Including VAT";
      SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" :=
        ROUND(SalesLineOrgTotalP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount",GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision") -
        SalesLineTotalP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount";
      SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base" :=
        ROUND(SalesLineOrgTotalP."Exch. Parts Tax Base",GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision") -
        SalesLineTotalP."Exch. Parts Tax Base";
      SalesLineP."Inv. Discount Amount" :=
        ROUND(SalesLineOrgTotalP."Inv. Discount Amount",GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision") -
        SalesLineTotalP."Inv. Discount Amount";
      SalesLineP."Line Discount Amount" :=
        ROUND(SalesLineOrgTotalP."Line Discount Amount",GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision") -
        SalesLineTotalP."Line Discount Amount";

      IncrementAmtPostItemCharge(SalesLineTotalP,SalesLineP);

      SrcCurrSalesLineL := SrcCurrSalesLine;

      SrcCurrSalesLineL.Amount := SrcCurrSalesLineL.Amount * FactorL;
      SrcCurrSalesLineL."Amount Including VAT" := SrcCurrSalesLineL."Amount Including VAT" * FactorL;
      SrcCurrSalesLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" := SrcCurrSalesLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" * FactorL;
      SrcCurrSalesLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Base" := SrcCurrSalesLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Base" * FactorL;
      SrcCurrSalesLineL."Inv. Discount Amount" := SrcCurrSalesLineL."Inv. Discount Amount" * FactorL;
      SrcCurrSalesLineL."Line Discount Amount" := SrcCurrSalesLineL."Line Discount Amount" * FactorL;

      IncrementAmtPostItemCharge(ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP,SrcCurrSalesLineL);

      SrcCurrSalesLineL.Amount :=
        ROUND(ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP.Amount,Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") - ScrCurrLineTotalP.Amount;
      SrcCurrSalesLineL."Amount Including VAT" :=
        ROUND(ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP."Amount Including VAT",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
        ScrCurrLineTotalP."Amount Including VAT";
      SrcCurrSalesLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" :=
        ROUND(ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
        ScrCurrLineTotalP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount";
      SrcCurrSalesLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Base" :=
        ROUND(ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP."Exch. Parts Tax Base",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
        ScrCurrLineTotalP."Exch. Parts Tax Base";
      SrcCurrSalesLineL."Inv. Discount Amount" :=
        ROUND(ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP."Inv. Discount Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
        ScrCurrLineTotalP."Inv. Discount Amount";
      SrcCurrSalesLineL."Line Discount Amount" :=
        ROUND(ScrCurrLineOrgTotalP."Line Discount Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
        ScrCurrLineTotalP."Line Discount Amount";

      IncrementAmtPostItemCharge(ScrCurrLineTotalP,SrcCurrSalesLineL);
      InvPostingBuffer[1].Type := SalesLineP.Type;
      IF SalesLineP.Type = SalesLineP.Type::"Account (G/L)" THEN
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."G/L Account" := SalesLineP."No."
      ELSE
        IF SalesHeaderP."Document Type" = SalesHeaderP."Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN BEGIN
          GenPostingSetup.TESTFIELD("Sales Credit Memo Account");
          InvPostingBuffer[1]."G/L Account" := GenPostingSetup."Sales Credit Memo Account";
          IF SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN  BEGIN
            GenPostingSetup.TESTFIELD("Sales Cr. Memo Acc. Inc. Surp.");
            InvPostingBuffer[1]."Sales Income Surplus Account" := GenPostingSetup."Sales Cr. Memo Acc. Inc. Surp.";
          END;
          IF SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax" THEN  BEGIN
            VATSetupTestG.GET(SalesLineP."VAT Bus. Posting Group",SalesLineP."VAT Prod. Posting Group");
      // Start PA032441
      // Stop PA032441
          END;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          GenPostingSetup.TESTFIELD("Sales Account");
          InvPostingBuffer[1]."G/L Account" := GenPostingSetup."Sales Account";
          IF SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN BEGIN
            GenPostingSetup.TESTFIELD("Sales Income Surplus Account");
            InvPostingBuffer[1]."Sales Income Surplus Account" := GenPostingSetup."Sales Income Surplus Account";
          END;
          IF SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax" THEN  BEGIN
            VATSetupTestG.GET(SalesLineP."VAT Bus. Posting Group",SalesLineP."VAT Prod. Posting Group");
      // Start PA032441
      // Stop PA032441
          END;
        END;
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."System-Created Entry" := TRUE;
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."Gen. Bus. Posting Group" := SalesLineP."Gen. Bus. Posting Group";
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" := SalesLineP."Gen. Prod. Posting Group";
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Bus. Posting Group" := SalesLineP."VAT Bus. Posting Group";
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Prod. Posting Group" := SalesLineP."VAT Prod. Posting Group";
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Calculation Type" := SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type";
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."Global Dimension 1 Code" := SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."Global Dimension 2 Code" := SalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code";
      // Start PA031882
      // Stop PA031882
      InvPostingBuffer[1].Amount := SalesLineP.Amount;
      InvPostingBuffer[1].VIN := SalesLineP.VIN;
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."Book No." := SalesLineP."Book No.";
      // Start PA041187.92988
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."Branch Code" := CurrBranchCodeG;
      // Stop PA041187.92988
      IF SalesLineP."Order Type" = SalesLineP."Order Type"::Service THEN BEGIN
        IF ServiceHdrG.GET(ServiceLineG."Document Type"::Order,SalesLineP."Service Order No.") THEN BEGIN
          InvPostingBuffer[1].VIN := ServiceHdrG.VIN;
          IF ServiceHdrG."Post with Book No." THEN
            InvPostingBuffer[1]."Book No." := ServiceHdrG."Book No."
          ELSE
            InvPostingBuffer[1]."Book No." := '';
      // Start PA043152
        END ELSE
          IF ArchServHdrG.GET(ServiceLineG."Document Type"::Order,SalesLineP."Service Order No.") THEN BEGIN
            InvPostingBuffer[1].VIN := ArchServHdrG.VIN;
            IF ArchServHdrG."Post with Book No." THEN
              InvPostingBuffer[1]."Book No." := ArchServHdrG."Book No."
            ELSE
              InvPostingBuffer[1]."Book No." := '';
          END;
      // Stop PA043152
      END;
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."Veh. Source Code" := InvPostingBuffer[1]."Veh. Source Code"::" ";
      IF (SalesLineP."Item Type" = SalesLineP."Item Type"::Vehicle) AND
         (SalesLineP."Order Type" = SalesLineP."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases")
      THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA035979
        IF (SalesLineP."Document Type" = SalesLineP."Document Type"::Order) OR
           (SalesLineP."Document Type" = SalesLineP."Document Type"::Invoice)
      // Stop PA035979
        THEN
          InvPostingBuffer[1]."Veh. Source Code" := InvPostingBuffer[1]."Veh. Source Code"::"Sales Invoice";
        IF SalesLineP."Document Type" = SalesLineP."Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN
          InvPostingBuffer[1]."Veh. Source Code" := InvPostingBuffer[1]."Veh. Source Code"::"Sales Credit Memo";
      END;

      IF FirstLineG THEN BEGIN
        IF InvPostingBuffer[1].VIN <> '' THEN BEGIN
          CurrentVING := InvPostingBuffer[1].VIN;
          CurrentBookNoG := InvPostingBuffer[1]."Book No.";
          FirstLineG := FALSE;
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
      // Start PA035979
        IF (InvPostingBuffer[1].VIN <> '') AND (CurrentVING <> InvPostingBuffer[1].VIN) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA035979
          CurrentVING := '';
          CurrentBookNoG := '';
        END;
      END;

      IF SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Base Amount" := SalesLineP."VAT Base Amount"
      ELSE
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Base Amount" := SalesLineP.Amount;
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Amount" := ROUND(SalesLineP."Amount Including VAT" -
        SalesLineP.Amount - SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      // Start PA032441
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."Amount (ACY)" := SrcCurrSalesLineL.Amount;
      IF SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type" IN [SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax",
         SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax"]
      THEN
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Base Amount (ACY)" := SrcCurrSalesLineL."VAT Base Amount"
      ELSE
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Base Amount (ACY)" := SrcCurrSalesLineL.Amount;
      InvPostingBuffer[1]."VAT Amount (ACY)" := SrcCurrSalesLineL."Amount Including VAT" - SrcCurrSalesLineL.Amount;
      // Stop PA032441
      IF SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax" THEN BEGIN
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Exch. Parts Tax Base" :=
          ROUND(SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Exch. Parts Tax %" := SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax %";
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Exch. Parts Tax Amount" :=
          ROUND(SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Orig. Exch. Parts VAT Tax Base" :=
          ROUND(SrcCurrSalesLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Base",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Orig. Exch. Parts VAT Amount" :=
          ROUND(SrcCurrSalesLineL."Exch. Parts Tax Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      END;

      IF SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN BEGIN
        VATSetupTestG.GET(SalesLineP."VAT Bus. Posting Group",SalesLineP."VAT Prod. Posting Group");
        VATSetupTestG.TESTFIELD("Diff Tax VAT Prod Posting Grp");
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Diff Tax VAT Prod Posting Grp" := VATSetupTestG."Diff Tax VAT Prod Posting Grp";
      END;

      IF SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLineP."VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax" THEN BEGIN
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Tax Area Code" := SalesLineP."Tax Area Code";
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Tax Group Code" := SalesLineP."Tax Group Code";
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Tax Liable" := SalesLineP."Tax Liable";
        InvPostingBuffer[1]."Use Tax" := FALSE;
        InvPostingBuffer[1].Quantity := SalesLineP."Qty. to Invoice";
      END;
      CASE SalesSetup."Discount Posting" OF
        SalesSetup."Discount Posting"::"Invoice Discounts":
          BEGIN
            InvPostingBuffer[1].Amount := InvPostingBuffer[1].Amount + SalesLineP."Inv. Discount Amount";
      // Start PA032441
            InvPostingBuffer[1]."Amount (ACY)" :=
              InvPostingBuffer[1]."Amount (ACY)" + SrcCurrSalesLineL."Inv. Discount Amount";
      // Stop PA032441
            IF (SalesLineP."Inv. Discount Amount" <> 0) OR
               (SrcCurrSalesLineL."Inv. Discount Amount" <> 0)
            THEN BEGIN
              GenPostingSetup.TESTFIELD("Sales Inv. Disc. Account");
      // Start PA032441
      // Stop PA032441
            END;
          END;
        SalesSetup."Discount Posting"::"Line Discounts":
          BEGIN
            InvPostingBuffer[1].Amount := InvPostingBuffer[1].Amount + SalesLineP."Line Discount Amount";
      // Start PA035979
            InvPostingBuffer[1]."Amount (ACY)" := InvPostingBuffer[1]."Amount (ACY)" + SrcCurrSalesLineL."Line Discount Amount";
            IF (SalesLineP."Line Discount Amount" <> 0) OR (SrcCurrSalesLineL."Line Discount Amount" <> 0) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA035979
              GenPostingSetup.TESTFIELD("Sales Line Disc. Account");
      // Start PA032441
      // Stop PA032441
            END;
          END;
        SalesSetup."Discount Posting"::"All Discounts":
          BEGIN
            InvPostingBuffer[1].Amount :=
              InvPostingBuffer[1].Amount +
              SalesLineP."Line Discount Amount" + SalesLineP."Inv. Discount Amount";
      // Start PA032441
            InvPostingBuffer[1]."Amount (ACY)" :=
              InvPostingBuffer[1]."Amount (ACY)" +
              SrcCurrSalesLineL."Line Discount Amount" + SrcCurrSalesLineL."Inv. Discount Amount";
      // Stop PA032441
      // Start PA035979
            IF (SalesLineP."Line Discount Amount" <> 0) OR (SrcCurrSalesLineL."Line Discount Amount" <> 0) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA035979
              GenPostingSetup.TESTFIELD("Sales Line Disc. Account");
      // Start PA032441
      // Stop PA032441
            END;
      // Start PA035979
            IF (SalesLineP."Inv. Discount Amount" <> 0) OR (SrcCurrSalesLineL."Inv. Discount Amount" <> 0) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA035979
              GenPostingSetup.TESTFIELD("Sales Inv. Disc. Account");
      // Start PA032441
      // Stop PA032441
            END;
          END;
      END;
      UpdInvPostingBuffer;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE IncrementAmtPostItemCharge@1109400015(VAR SalesLineTotalP@1109400001 : Record 37;VAR SalesLineP@1109400000 : Record 37);
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      Increment(SalesLineTotalP.Amount,SalesLineP.Amount);
      Increment(SalesLineTotalP."VAT Base Amount",SalesLineP."VAT Base Amount");
      Increment(SalesLineTotalP."Amount Including VAT",SalesLineP."Amount Including VAT");
      Increment(SalesLineTotalP."Line Discount Amount",SalesLineP."Line Discount Amount");
      Increment(SalesLineTotalP."Inv. Discount Amount",SalesLineP."Inv. Discount Amount");

      Increment(SalesLineTotalP."Exch. Parts Tax Base",SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base");
      Increment(SalesLineTotalP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount",SalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount");
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE IsImporter@5025800() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      EXIT(CompanyInfoG.IMSCheck());
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetSkipOnlyAssgntPostingG@1109400003(ValueP@1109400000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      // Start PA033011.5857175
      SkipOnlyAssgntPostingG := ValueP;
      // Stop PA033011.5857175
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreatePrepaymentLine@1101219227(SalesHeaderP@1101219230 : Record 36;VAR TempPrepmtSalesLineP@1101219229 : Record 37;CompleteFunctionalityP@1101219227 : Boolean);
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1101219233 : Record 37;
      CustLedgEntryL@1101219240 : Record 21;
      CustL@1101219238 : Record 18;
      SalesInvHdrL@72000 : Record 112;
      SalesInvLineL@1109400000 : Record 113;
      SalesCrMemoLineL@1055600 : Record 115;
      ServPreviewL@1101219236 : Codeunit 5025638;
      RecordRefL@1055602 : RecordRef;
      NextLineNoL@1101219231 : Integer;
      TotalAmtToInvoiceL@1101219232 : Decimal;
      AmountLCYL@1101219239 : Decimal;
      TextL@1101219234 : Text[30];
      PrepaymTextL@1101219237 : TextConst 'ENU=Prepayment';
      RunLoopL@1055601 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ Function creates additional line with a prepayment amount which is calculated as a sum of all posted prepayment invoices for
      // @ and a specific sales or service order. This amount is always negative.
      // Start PA034291
      IF NOT SalesHeaderP."Prepayment Assignment" THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start PA034291.I002243
      IF NOT ((SalesHeaderP."Document Type" = SalesHeaderP."Document Type"::Order) OR
         (SalesHeaderP."Document Type" = SalesHeaderP."Document Type"::Invoice))
      THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA034291.I002243
      SalesLineL.RESET;
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeaderP."Document Type");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeaderP."No.");
      IF SalesLineL.FINDLAST THEN
        NextLineNoL := SalesLineL."Line No." + 10000
      ELSE
        EXIT;

      // Start PA034291
      // Start PA034291.I002257
      CustLedgEntryL.RESET;
      CustLedgEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Customer No.",Open,"Document No.");
      CustLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Customer No.",SalesHeaderP."Bill-to Customer No.");
      CustLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(Prepayment,TRUE);
      IF SalesHeaderP."Order Type" = SalesHeaderP."Order Type"::Service THEN
      // Start EU.0012448.13245
        CustLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Prepayment Order No.",SalesHeaderP."Service Order No.")
      // Stop EU.0012448.13245
      ELSE
        CustLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Prepayment Order No.",SalesHeader."Prepayment Order No.");
      IF CustLedgEntryL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA043087
        TempPrepmtSalesLineP.SetSalesHeader(SalesHeaderP);
      // Stop PA043087
      // Start PA041187.73133
        // create Begin Total
        IF SalesHeaderP."Order Type" = SalesHeaderP."Order Type"::Service THEN BEGIN
          TempPrepmtSalesLineP.INIT;
          TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Document Type" := SalesHeaderP."Document Type";
          TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Document No." := SalesHeaderP."No.";
          TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Line No." := NextLineNoL;
          NextLineNoL += 10000;
          TempPrepmtSalesLineP."System-Created Entry" := TRUE;
          TempPrepmtSalesLineP.VALIDATE(Type,TempPrepmtSalesLineP.Type::"Begin-Total");
          TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := SalesHeaderP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code";
          TempPrepmtSalesLineP.Description := PrepaymTextL;
          TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Prepayment Line" := TRUE;
          TempPrepmtSalesLineP.INSERT;
        END;
        REPEAT
      // Start PA045632
          RunLoopL := FALSE;
          CASE CustLedgEntryL."Document Type" OF
            CustLedgEntryL."Document Type"::Invoice:
              BEGIN
                SalesInvLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", CustLedgEntryL."Document No.");
                SalesInvLineL.SETRANGE("No.", SalesSetup."Default Prepmt. GL Account");
                IF NOT SalesInvLineL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                  RecordRefL.GETTABLE(SalesInvLineL);
                  RunLoopL := TRUE;
                END;
              END;
            CustLedgEntryL."Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
              BEGIN
                SalesCrMemoLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", CustLedgEntryL."Document No.");
                SalesCrMemoLineL.SETRANGE("No.", SalesSetup."Default Prepmt. GL Account");
                IF NOT SalesCrMemoLineL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                  RecordRefL.GETTABLE(SalesCrMemoLineL);
                  RunLoopL := TRUE;
                END;
              END;
          END;
          IF RunLoopL THEN
            RunLoopL := NOT CustLedgEntryL.CheckPrepaymentClosedCredit();
          IF RecordRefL.FINDSET AND RunLoopL THEN
            REPEAT
              // In case when entry type is not invoice, copy current record type to SalesInvLineL in order to use values.
              CASE CustLedgEntryL."Document Type" OF
                CustLedgEntryL."Document Type"::Invoice:
                  RecordRefL.SETTABLE(SalesInvLineL);
                CustLedgEntryL."Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
                  BEGIN
                    RecordRefL.SETTABLE(SalesCrMemoLineL);
                    SalesInvLineL.TRANSFERFIELDS(SalesCrMemoLineL);
                    SalesInvLineL.Amount *= -1;
                  END;
              END;
      // Stop PA045632
              AmountLCYL := SalesInvLineL.Amount;
      // Start EU.0093002
              SalesInvHdrL.GET(SalesInvLineL."Document No."); // The posted prepayment invoice header
              IF SalesHeaderP."Currency Code" <> SalesInvHdrL."Currency Code" THEN BEGIN
                CASE TRUE OF
                  (SalesHeaderP."Currency Code" <> '') AND (SalesInvHdrL."Currency Code" <> ''):
                    AmountLCYL := ROUND(CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToFCY(
                      SalesHeaderP."Posting Date",SalesInvHdrL."Currency Code",
                      SalesHeaderP."Currency Code",SalesInvLineL.Amount),
                      Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                  (SalesInvHdrL."Currency Code" = ''):
                    AmountLCYL := ROUND(CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
                      SalesHeaderP."Posting Date",SalesHeaderP."Currency Code",
                      SalesInvLineL.Amount,SalesHeaderP."Currency Factor"),
                      Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                  (SalesHeaderP."Currency Code" = ''):
                    AmountLCYL := ROUND(CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                      SalesHeaderP."Posting Date",SalesInvHdrL."Currency Code",
                      SalesInvLineL.Amount,SalesInvHdrL."Currency Factor"),
                      Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                END;
              END;
      // Stop EU.0093002
              IF SalesHeaderP."Currency Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0093002
      // Stop EU.0093002
                TotalAmtToInvoiceL := TotalAmtToInvoiceL + AmountLCYL;
              END ELSE
                TotalAmtToInvoiceL := TotalAmtToInvoiceL + CustLedgEntryL."Sales (LCY)";
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP.INIT;
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Document Type" := SalesHeaderP."Document Type";
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Document No." := SalesHeaderP."No.";
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Line No." := 0;
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP."System-Created Entry" := TRUE;
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP.VALIDATE(Type,TempPrepmtSalesLineP.Type::"Account (G/L)");
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP.VALIDATE("No.",SalesSetup."Default Prepmt. GL Account");
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP.VALIDATE("VAT Prod. Posting Group",SalesInvLineL."VAT Prod. Posting Group");
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP.VALIDATE(Quantity,-1);
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Qty. to Ship" := TempPrepmtSalesLineP.Quantity;
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Qty. to Invoice" := TempPrepmtSalesLineP.Quantity;
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Prepayment Line" := TRUE;
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP.VALIDATE("Unit Price",AmountLCYL);
              TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Line No." := NextLineNoL;
              IF TempPrepmtSalesLineP.INSERT THEN
                NextLineNoL += 10000;
      // Start PA045632
            UNTIL RecordRefL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA045632
        UNTIL CustLedgEntryL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA041187.73133
      END;
      // Stop PA034291.I002257
      IF TotalAmtToInvoiceL = 0 THEN
        EXIT;

      // Start PA041187.73133
      // Stop PA041187.73133

      IF SalesHeaderP."Order Type" = SalesHeaderP."Order Type"::Service THEN BEGIN
        NextLineNoL += 10000;
      // create End Total
        TempPrepmtSalesLineP.INIT;
        TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Document Type" := SalesHeaderP."Document Type";
        TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Document No." := SalesHeaderP."No.";
        TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Line No." := NextLineNoL;
        TempPrepmtSalesLineP."System-Created Entry" := TRUE;
        TempPrepmtSalesLineP.VALIDATE(Type,TempPrepmtSalesLineP.Type::"Begin-Total");
        TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := SalesHeaderP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code";
      // Start PA040837
        TextL := ServPreviewL.GetTextTranslation(SalesHeaderP."Bill-to Customer No.",3); // 3=Sum
      // Stop PA040837
        TempPrepmtSalesLineP.Description := TextL + ' ' + PrepaymTextL;
        TempPrepmtSalesLineP."Prepayment Line" := TRUE;
        TempPrepmtSalesLineP.INSERT;
      END;
      // Stop PA034291
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateTempBlanketOrder@1101221269(SalesLineP@1101221267 : Record 37);
    BEGIN
      // Start PA035134
      IF NOT TempBlanketOrderG.GET(SalesLine."Document Type",SalesLine."Document No.") THEN BEGIN
        TempBlanketOrderG.INIT;
        TempBlanketOrderG."Document Type" := SalesLine."Document Type";
        TempBlanketOrderG."No." := SalesLine."Document No.";
        TempBlanketOrderG.INSERT;
      END;
      // Stop PA035134
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateBlanketOrderStatus@1101221273();
    BEGIN
      // Start PA035134
      IF TempBlanketOrderG.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          SalesHdrG.GET(TempBlanketOrderG."Document Type",TempBlanketOrderG."No.");
          SalesHdrG.UpdateStatus;
          SalesHdrG.MODIFY;
        UNTIL TempBlanketOrderG.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA035134
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InsertTempSalIncVehJnlLine@1101157049(SalesLineP@1101314647 : Record 37;ItemChargeNoP@1101157056 : Code[20];VINNoP@1101157055 : Code[20];BookNoP@1101157054 : Code[20];BrachBookNoP@1101157053 : Code[20];AmountToAssignP@1101157052 : Decimal);
    VAR
      VehicleJournalTemplateL@1101157045 : Record 5025402;
      VehicleJournalBatchNameL@1101157046 : Record 5025404;
      VehLedgEntryL@1101157047 : Record 5025405;
    BEGIN
      // @ Create Vehicle Journal Line based on Sales Order/Line to post a balance to the existing Sales Incentive G/L Postings
      // @ use the same Accounts as in the Ledger Entry, but reverse the signs.
      // @ Param SalesLineP: Sales Line
      // @ Param ItemChargeNoP: No. of the Item Charge
      // @ Param VINNoP: VIN of the vehicle in question
      // @ Param BookNoP: Book No. of the Vehicle in Question
      // @ Param BranchBookNoP: Branch Book No. of the Vehicle in Question
      // @ Param AmountToAssignP: the amount has been assigned by the Charge Item
      // @ retval TRUE, if VehicleJnlLineL was created

      // Start PA033985
      // @ Step 1: Fill the Vehicle Journal Line
      IF SalesHeader."Order Type" <> SalesHeader."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
        EXIT;
      IF TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Appl.-to Sales Incentive Entry" = 0 THEN
        EXIT;
      IF NOT VehLedgEntryL.GET(TempItemChargeAssgntSales."Appl.-to Sales Incentive Entry") THEN
        EXIT;
      IF VINNoP <> VehLedgEntryL.VIN THEN
        EXIT;
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.INIT;
      NextVehJnlLineNoG := NextVehJnlLineNoG + 10000;
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Line No." := NextVehJnlLineNoG;
      VehicleSetupG.GET();
      VehicleJournalTemplateL.GET(VehicleSetupG."Sales Incentive Jnl. Template");
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Journal Template Name" := VehicleSetupG."Sales Incentive Jnl. Template";
      VehicleJournalBatchNameL.GET(VehicleSetupG."Sales Incentive Jnl. Template",VehicleSetupG."Sales Incentive Jnl. Name");
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Journal Batch Name" := VehicleSetupG."Sales Incentive Jnl. Name";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Main Area" := TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Main Area"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Entry Type" := VehLedgEntryL."Entry Type";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Credit Memo" := SalesHeader."Document Type" = SalesHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.VALIDATE("Posting Date",SalesHeader."Posting Date");
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Document No." := GenJnlLineDocNo;
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."External Document No." := GenJnlLineExtDocNo;
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Source Type" := VehLedgEntryL."Source Type";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Document Type" := VehLedgEntryL."Document Type";

      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.VALIDATE(VIN,VINNoP);
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Book No." := BookNoP;
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.VALIDATE("Location Code",SalesLineP."Location Code");
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Sales Incentive No." := VehLedgEntryL."Sales Incentive No.";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Sales Incentive Group" := VehLedgEntryL."Sales Incentive Group";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Appl.-to Sales Incentive Entry" := VehLedgEntryL."Entry No.";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.Description := VehLedgEntryL.Description;
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.Type := VehLedgEntryL.Type;
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.VALIDATE("No.",VehLedgEntryL."No.");
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.VALIDATE("Bal. Account No.",VehLedgEntryL."Bal. Account No.");
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Gen. Posting Type" := TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Gen. Posting Type"::Sale;
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" := VehLedgEntryL."Gen. Prod. Posting Group";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Gen. Bus. Posting Group" := VehLedgEntryL."Gen. Bus. Posting Group";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."VAT Calculation Type" := VehLedgEntryL."VAT Calculation Type";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."VAT Prod. Posting Group" := VehLedgEntryL."VAT Prod. Posting Group";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."VAT Bus. Posting Group" := VehLedgEntryL."VAT Bus. Posting Group";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Bal. Acc.-Gen. Posting Type" := TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Bal. Acc.-Gen. Posting Type"::Sale;

      // Start PA035473
      IF TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Credit Memo" THEN BEGIN
        TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Invoiced Quantity" := -1; // will be automatically corrected during Posting
        IF VehLedgEntryL."Unit Cost" <> 0 THEN
      // Start PA035473.26139
          TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.VALIDATE("Unit Cost",AmountToAssignP);
      // Stop PA035473.26139
        IF VehLedgEntryL."Unit Price" <> 0 THEN
          TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.VALIDATE("Unit Price",-AmountToAssignP);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Invoiced Quantity" := 1;// will be automatically corrected during Posting
        IF VehLedgEntryL."Unit Cost" <> 0 THEN
      // Start PA035473.26139
          TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.VALIDATE("Unit Cost",AmountToAssignP);
      // Stop PA035473.26139
        IF VehLedgEntryL."Unit Price" <> 0 THEN
          TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.VALIDATE("Unit Price",-AmountToAssignP);
      END;
      // Stop PA035473
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Assoc. No." := TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."No.";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Department Code" := VehLedgEntryL."Department Code";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Make Code" := VehLedgEntryL."Make Code";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Source Code" := VehLedgEntryL."Source Code";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Reason Code" := VehLedgEntryL."Reason Code";
      // overwrite values with values from Purchase Header
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Salespers./Purch. Code" := SalesHeader."Salesperson Code";
      // Start PA036728
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Salesperson Code 2" := SalesHeader."Salesperson Code 2";
      // Stop PA036728
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Posting No. Series" := SalesHeader."Posting No. Series";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Source Type" := VehLedgEntryL."Source Type";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Source No." := SalesHeader."Sell-to Customer No.";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG."Source No. (Payment)" := SalesHeader."Bill-to Customer No.";
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.INSERT;
      // Stop PA033985
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE PostSalIncJnlLine@1101157059();
    VAR
      VehJnlLineL@1109400000 : Record 5025403;
    BEGIN
      // @ function to post all temporary Vehicle Journal Lines that are related to Sales Incentives
      // Start PA033985
      IF TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          VehJnlLineL := TempSalIncVehJnlLineG;
          VehicleJnlLinePostG.RUN(VehJnlLineL);
          SalesIncentivePostG.UpdatePostedSalesIncentive(TempSalIncVehJnlLineG,SalesHeader."Currency Code",SalesHeader."Currency Factor");
      // Start PA036549.33101
          IF SalesIncentivePostG.AutomaticPostDifferences(VehJnlLineL) THEN
            VehicleJnlLinePostG.RUN(VehJnlLineL);
      // Stop PA036549.33101
        UNTIL TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.NEXT = 0;
      TempSalIncVehJnlLineG.DELETEALL;
      NextVehJnlLineNoG := 0;
      // Stop PA033985
    END;

    PROCEDURE CopyEmmRelLogText@1000000000(FromDocumentTypeP@1109400000 : Integer;ToDocumentTypeP@1109400001 : Integer;FromNumberP@1109400002 : Code[20];ToNumberP@1109400003 : Code[20]);
    BEGIN
      // @ function to transfer emission related logical text from unposted to posted documents
      // @ Param FromDocumentTypeP: Document Type of Sales Header
      // @ Param ToDocumentTypeP: Documnt Type of Sales Invoice Header
      // @ Param FromNumberP Code: Document No. from Sales Header
      // @ Param ToNumberP: Document No. of Sales Invoice Header

      // Start PA042665
      EmissionsRelevantLegalTextsG.SETRANGE("Document Type",FromDocumentTypeP);
      EmissionsRelevantLegalTextsG.SETRANGE("Document No.",FromNumberP);
      IF EmissionsRelevantLegalTextsG.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          PostdEmissnRelLegalTxtsG.TRANSFERFIELDS(EmissionsRelevantLegalTextsG);
          PostdEmissnRelLegalTxtsG."Document Type" := ToDocumentTypeP;
          PostdEmissnRelLegalTxtsG."Document No." := ToNumberP;
          PostdEmissnRelLegalTxtsG.INSERT;
        UNTIL EmissionsRelevantLegalTextsG.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA042665
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetTotalSalesLineByVAT@10430600(RecP@10430602 : Record 37;VAR TotalRecP@10430601 : Record 37;OffsetP@10430603 : Integer);
    VAR
      VATLineNoL@10430600 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      VATLineNoL := RecP."VAT %" * 100 + OffsetP;
      IF NOT TempTotalsByVATBufferG.GET(RecP."VAT Calculation Type", RecP."VAT Identifier", VATLineNoL) THEN
        CLEAR(TempTotalsByVATBufferG);
      TotalRecP := TempTotalsByVATBufferG;
      TotalRecP."Document Type" := RecP."VAT Calculation Type";
      TotalRecP."Document No." := RecP."VAT Identifier";
      TotalRecP."Line No." := VATLineNoL;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SetTotalSalesLineByVAT@10430601(TotalRecP@10430601 : Record 37);
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0104306
      TempTotalsByVATBufferG := TotalRecP;
      IF NOT TempTotalsByVATBufferG.MODIFY THEN
        TempTotalsByVATBufferG.INSERT;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetDistributionBuffer@5321003(VAR VATDistributionBufferP@1117700000 : Record 5204940);
    BEGIN
      // @ The function copy the global VAT Distribution Buffer to another
      // @ param VATDistributionBufferP destination VAT Distribution Buffer

      // Start EU.0104306
      VATDistributionBufferP.DELETEALL;
      IF VATDistributionBufferG[1].FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          VATDistributionBufferP := VATDistributionBufferG[1];
          VATDistributionBufferP.INSERT;
        UNTIL VATDistributionBufferG[1].NEXT = 0;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdVATDistributionBuffer@5321001();
    BEGIN
      // @ The function updates the values on second array index of VATDistributionBuffer variable
      // @ that contains the total amounts

      // Start EU.0104306
      VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Prod. Posting Group":='';
      VATDistributionBufferG[2] := VATDistributionBufferG[1];
      IF VATDistributionBufferG[2].FIND THEN BEGIN
        VATDistributionBufferG[2].Amount := VATDistributionBufferG[2].Amount + VATDistributionBufferG[1].Amount;
        VATDistributionBufferG[2]."VAT Amount" := VATDistributionBufferG[2]."VAT Amount" + VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Amount";
        VATDistributionBufferG[2]."VAT Difference" := VATDistributionBufferG[2]."VAT Difference" + VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Difference";
        VATDistributionBufferG[2]."Amount LCY" := VATDistributionBufferG[2]."Amount LCY" + VATDistributionBufferG[1]."Amount LCY";
        VATDistributionBufferG[2]."VAT Amount LCY"  := VATDistributionBufferG[2]."VAT Amount LCY" + VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Amount LCY";
        VATDistributionBufferG[2].MODIFY;
      END ELSE
        VATDistributionBufferG[1].INSERT;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE EnhancedAmountRounding@1116500002(VAR GlobTotalSalesLineP@10430604 : Record 37;SalesLineQtyP@1109400000 : Decimal;VAR OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP@10430602 : Record 37;VAR TotalByVATSalesLineP@10430601 : Record 37;VAR TotalByVATSalesLineLCYP@10430600 : Record 37);
    VAR
      NoVATL@1109400001 : Boolean;
      DesiredVATAmountL@1117700002 : Decimal;
      TempAmountL@1117700003 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function replaces the original one RoundAmount
      // @ param GlobTotalSalesLineP = Global TotalSalesLine variable from AmountRounding function.
      // @ param SalesLineQtyP indicates the quantity for which the calculation must be done
      // @ param OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP = local OrgTotalSalesLine variable from AmountRounding function. It is separated by VAT %
      // @ param TotalByVATSalesLineP = local TotalSalesLine variable from AmountRounding function. It is separated by VAT %
      // @ param TotalByVATSalesLineLCYP = local TotalSalesLineLCY variable from AmountRounding function. It is separated by VAT %

      // Start EU.0104306
      WITH SalesLine DO BEGIN
        IF ("Calculated VAT Amount" = 0) OR
           NOT ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Invoice,"Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]) OR
           ("Original Amount" = 0) OR
           ("Original Amount Incl. VAT" = 0)
        THEN BEGIN
          "Original Amount" := Amount;
          "Original Amount Incl. VAT" := "Amount Including VAT";
        END;
        Amount := "Original Amount";
        "Amount Including VAT" := "Original Amount Incl. VAT" + "VAT Difference Amount";
        IF GLSetup.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(SalesHeader."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN
          "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND("Amount Including VAT",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
        "VAT Difference Amount" := ROUND("VAT Difference Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
        IF ("VAT Bus. Posting Group" <> VATPostingSetupG."VAT Bus. Posting Group") OR
           ("VAT Prod. Posting Group" <> VATPostingSetupG."VAT Prod. Posting Group")
        THEN BEGIN
          VATPostingSetupG.GET("VAT Bus. Posting Group","VAT Prod. Posting Group");
        END;

        IF NOT VATDistributionBufferG[1].GET(VATPostingSetupG."VAT Identifier",VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type",FALSE) THEN BEGIN
          VATDistributionBufferG[1].INIT;
          VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Identifier" := VATPostingSetupG."VAT Identifier";
          VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Calculation Type" := VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type";
          VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Bus. Posting Group" := "VAT Bus. Posting Group";
          VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Prod. Posting Group" := "VAT Prod. Posting Group";
          VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT %" := VATPostingSetupG."VAT %";
        END;

        NoVATL := Amount = "Amount Including VAT";

        IF NOT GLSetup.EnhancedVATCalculationLogicInDocActive(SalesHeader."VAT Calculation Logic") THEN BEGIN
          IF (VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type" = VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT") AND NOT NoVATL THEN BEGIN
            TempAmountL := ROUND(OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP.Amount + Amount,Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") - TotalByVATSalesLineP.Amount;
            CASE GLSetup."VAT Rounding Type" OF
              GLSetup."VAT Rounding Type"::Nearest:
                DesiredVATAmountL := ROUND((VATDistributionBufferG[1].Amount + TempAmountL) * VATPostingSetupG."VAT %" / 100,
                Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") - VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Amount" + "VAT Difference Amount";
              GLSetup."VAT Rounding Type"::Up:
                DesiredVATAmountL := ROUND((VATDistributionBufferG[1].Amount + TempAmountL) * VATPostingSetupG."VAT %" / 100,
                Currency."Amount Rounding Precision",'>') - VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Amount" + "VAT Difference Amount";
              GLSetup."VAT Rounding Type"::Down:
                DesiredVATAmountL := ROUND((VATDistributionBufferG[1].Amount + TempAmountL) * VATPostingSetupG."VAT %" / 100,
                Currency."Amount Rounding Precision",'<') - VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Amount" + "VAT Difference Amount";
            END;
            "Amount Including VAT" := TempAmountL + DesiredVATAmountL + (OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP."Amount Including VAT" - TotalByVATSalesLineP."Amount Including VAT");
          END;
        END;

        IncrAmount(OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP,FALSE);

        NoVATL := Amount = "Amount Including VAT";
        "Amount Including VAT" :=
          ROUND(OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP."Amount Including VAT",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
          TotalByVATSalesLineP."Amount Including VAT";
        IF NoVATL THEN BEGIN
          Amount := "Amount Including VAT";
          "VAT Base Amount" := "Amount Including VAT";
        END ELSE BEGIN
          Amount :=
            ROUND(OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP.Amount,Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
            TotalByVATSalesLineP.Amount;
          "VAT Base Amount" :=
            ROUND(OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP."VAT Base Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
            TotalByVATSalesLineP."VAT Base Amount";
        END;

        VATDistributionBufferG[1].Amount := Amount;
        VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Amount" := "Amount Including VAT" - Amount - "VAT Difference Amount";
        VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Difference" := "VAT Difference Amount";
        VATDistributionBufferG[1]."Amount LCY" := 0;
        VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Amount LCY" := 0;
        VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Difference LCY" := 0;
        UpdVATDistributionBuffer();
        "Line Discount Amount" :=
          ROUND(
            OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP."Line Discount Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
            TotalByVATSalesLineP."Line Discount Amount";
        "Inv. Discount Amount" :=
          ROUND(
            OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP."Inv. Discount Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
            TotalByVATSalesLineP."Inv. Discount Amount";
        "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" :=
          ROUND(
            OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
            TotalByVATSalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount";
        "Exch. Parts Tax Base" :=
          ROUND(
            OrgTotalByVATSalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
            TotalByVATSalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base";

        IncrAmount(TotalByVATSalesLineP, FALSE);
        IncrAmount(GlobTotalSalesLineP, FALSE);
        Increment(GlobTotalSalesLineP."Net Weight",ROUND(SalesLineQtyP * "Net Weight",0.00001));
        Increment(GlobTotalSalesLineP."Gross Weight",ROUND(SalesLineQtyP * "Gross Weight",0.00001));
        Increment(GlobTotalSalesLineP."Unit Volume",ROUND(SalesLineQtyP * "Unit Volume",0.00001));
        Increment(GlobTotalSalesLineP.Quantity,SalesLineQtyP);

        IF "Units per Parcel" > 0 THEN
          Increment(GlobTotalSalesLineP."Units per Parcel", ROUND(SalesLineQtyP / "Units per Parcel",1,'>'));

        TempSalesLine := SalesLine;
        SrcCurrSalesLine := SalesLine;

        IF SalesHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
          IF SalesHeader."Document Type" = SalesHeader."Document Type"::Quote THEN
            UseDate := WORKDATE
          ELSE
            UseDate := SalesHeader."Posting Date";
          IF NOT VATDistributionBufferG[1].GET(VATPostingSetupG."VAT Identifier",VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type",FALSE) THEN BEGIN
            VATDistributionBufferG[1].INIT;
            VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Identifier" := VATPostingSetupG."VAT Identifier";
            VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Calculation Type" := VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type";
            VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Bus. Posting Group" := "VAT Bus. Posting Group";
            VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Prod. Posting Group" := "VAT Prod. Posting Group";
            VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT %" := VATPostingSetupG."VAT %";
          END;
          NoVATL := Amount = "Amount Including VAT";
          "Amount Including VAT" :=
            ROUND(
              CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                TotalByVATSalesLineP."Amount Including VAT",SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                TotalByVATSalesLineLCYP."Amount Including VAT";
          IF NoVATL THEN
            Amount := "Amount Including VAT"
          ELSE BEGIN
            Amount :=
              ROUND(
                CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                  UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                  TotalByVATSalesLineP.Amount,SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                  TotalByVATSalesLineLCYP.Amount;
            "VAT Amount":=
              ROUND(
                CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                  UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                  (TotalByVATSalesLineP."Amount Including VAT" - TotalByVATSalesLineP.Amount),SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                  (TotalByVATSalesLineLCYP."Amount Including VAT" - TotalByVATSalesLineLCYP.Amount);
            "Amount Including VAT":= Amount + "VAT Amount";
            "VAT Difference Amount" :=
              ROUND(
                CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                  UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code","VAT Difference Amount",SalesHeader."Currency Factor"),GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision");
          END;
          VATDistributionBufferG[1].Amount := 0;
          VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Amount" := 0;
          VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Difference" := 0;
          VATDistributionBufferG[1]."Amount LCY" := Amount;
          VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Amount LCY" := "Amount Including VAT" - Amount - "VAT Difference Amount";
          VATDistributionBufferG[1]."VAT Difference LCY" := "VAT Difference Amount";
          UpdVATDistributionBuffer();

          "Line Discount Amount" :=
            ROUND(
              CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                TotalByVATSalesLineP."Line Discount Amount",SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                TotalByVATSalesLineLCYP."Line Discount Amount";
          "Inv. Discount Amount" :=
            ROUND(
              CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                TotalByVATSalesLineP."Inv. Discount Amount",SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                TotalByVATSalesLineLCYP."Inv. Discount Amount";
          "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" :=
            ROUND(
              CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                TotalByVATSalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount",SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                TotalByVATSalesLineLCYP."Exch. Parts Tax Amount";
          "Exch. Parts Tax Base" :=
            ROUND(
              CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                UseDate,SalesHeader."Currency Code",
                TotalByVATSalesLineP."Exch. Parts Tax Base",SalesHeader."Currency Factor")) -
                TotalByVATSalesLineLCYP."Exch. Parts Tax Base";
        END;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;

    PROCEDURE SalesBillVATCalculation@1117700004(QtyTypeP@14535500 : 'General,Invoicing,Shipping';VAR SalesHeaderP@1117700005 : Record 36;VAR VATDistributionBufferP@1116500001 : Record 5204940;AmountRoundingPrecisionP@1116500003 : Decimal;WriteSalesLineP@1117700006 : Boolean;WriteDistributionBufferP@1117700007 : Boolean) : Decimal;
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1116500000 : Record 37;
      VATDistribuitionBufferL@10430600 : TEMPORARY Record 5204940;
      TotalAmountL@1117700009 : Decimal;
      VehicleUnitPriceL@14535501 : Decimal;
      SalesLineQtyL@14535502 : Decimal;
      SalesLinesFoundL@1116500009 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function recalc the amount and VAT amount from the document totals
      // @ param VATDistribuitionBufferP original VAT Distribuition Buffer
      // @ param AmountRoundingPrecisionP precision for VAT rounding
      // @ param WriteSalesLineP modify the last document line
      // @ param WriteDistributionBufferP recreate all the VAT Distribuition Buffer

      // Start EU.0104306
      SalesLinesFoundL := FALSE;
      SalesLineL.RESET;
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeaderP."Document Type");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeaderP."No.");
      IF SalesLineL.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
        SalesLinesFoundL := TRUE;
        REPEAT
          IF NOT VATDistribuitionBufferL.GET(SalesLineL."VAT Identifier",SalesLineL."VAT Calculation Type",FALSE) THEN BEGIN
            CLEAR(VATDistribuitionBufferL);
            VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT Identifier" := SalesLineL."VAT Identifier";
            VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT Calculation Type" := SalesLineL."VAT Calculation Type";
            VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT Bus. Posting Group" := SalesLineL."VAT Bus. Posting Group";
            VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT Prod. Posting Group" := SalesLineL."VAT Prod. Posting Group";
            VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT %" := SalesLineL."VAT %";
            VATDistribuitionBufferL.INSERT;
          END;
      // Start EU.0145355.145511
          CASE QtyTypeP OF
            QtyTypeP::General:
              SalesLineQtyL := SalesLineL.Quantity;
            QtyTypeP::Invoicing:
              SalesLineQtyL := SalesLineL."Qty. to Invoice";
            QtyTypeP::Shipping:
              IF SalesHeaderP."Document Type" IN [SalesHeaderP."Document Type"::"Return Order", SalesHeaderP."Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
                SalesLineQtyL := SalesLineL."Return Qty. to Receive"
              ELSE
                SalesLineQtyL := SalesLineL."Qty. to Ship";
          END;
          IF SalesLineQtyL <> 0 THEN BEGIN
            DivideAmount(SalesLineQtyL, SalesLineL);
      // Stop EU.0145355.145511
            VATDistribuitionBufferL."Amount Incl. VAT" += ROUND(SalesLineL."Amount Including VAT",AmountRoundingPrecisionP);
            VATDistribuitionBufferL.Amount += SalesLineL.Amount;
            VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT Amount" += VATDistribuitionBufferL."Amount Incl. VAT" - VATDistribuitionBufferL.Amount;
      // Start EU.0126935.128630
      // Start EU.0145355.145511
            IF VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT Calculation Type"= SalesLineL."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
              IF SalesLineL."Item Type" = SalesLineL."Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
                IF SalesLineL.Quantity = 1 THEN
                  IF SalesLineL.Amount <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                    VehicleUnitPriceL := SalesLineL."Unit Cost";
                      IF SalesLineL."Unit Cost" > SalesLineL."Unit Price" THEN
                        VehicleUnitPriceL := SalesLineL."Unit Price";
                    VATDistribuitionBufferL.Amount -= VehicleUnitPriceL;
                    VATDistribuitionBufferL."Amount Incl. VAT" -= VehicleUnitPriceL;
                    VATDistribuitionBufferL."Differential Unit Cost" += VehicleUnitPriceL;
                  END;
      // Stop EU.0145355.145511
      // Stop EU.0126935.128630
            VATDistribuitionBufferL.MODIFY;
      // Start EU.0145355.145511
          END;
      // Stop EU.0145355.145511
        UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      IF (SalesLinesFoundL) THEN BEGIN
        IF (WriteDistributionBufferP) THEN
          VATDistributionBufferP.DELETEALL;

        VATDistribuitionBufferL.RESET;
        IF VATDistribuitionBufferL.FIND('-') THEN
          REPEAT
            VATDistribuitionBufferL."Calculated Amount" += ROUND((VATDistribuitionBufferL."Amount Incl. VAT" * 100) / (100 + VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT %"), 0.01,'=');
            VATDistribuitionBufferL."Calculated VAT Amount" += (VATDistribuitionBufferL."Amount Incl. VAT" - VATDistribuitionBufferL."Calculated Amount");
            VATDistribuitionBufferL.MODIFY;
            // Write changes on Sales Lines
            IF ((VATDistribuitionBufferL."Calculated Amount" - VATDistribuitionBufferL.Amount) <> 0) AND (WriteSalesLineP) THEN BEGIN
              SalesLineL.SETRANGE("VAT Prod. Posting Group",VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT Prod. Posting Group");
              SalesLineL.FIND('+');
              SalesLineL.Amount += (VATDistribuitionBufferL."Calculated Amount" - VATDistribuitionBufferL.Amount);
              SalesLineL."Line Discount Amount" += -(VATDistribuitionBufferL."Calculated Amount" - VATDistribuitionBufferL.Amount);
              SalesLineL."Line Discount %" := ROUND(SalesLineL."Line Discount Amount" * 100 / (SalesLineL."Line Discount Amount" + SalesLineL.Amount),0.00001);
              SalesLineL."Original Amount" := SalesLineL.Amount;
              SalesLineL."VAT Base Amount" := SalesLineL.Amount;
              SalesLineL.MODIFY;
            END;
            //Write changes on Distribution Buffer
            IF (WriteDistributionBufferP) THEN BEGIN
              CLEAR(VATDistributionBufferP);
              VATDistributionBufferP."VAT Identifier" := VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT Identifier";
              VATDistributionBufferP."VAT Calculation Type" := VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT Calculation Type";
              //VATDistributionBufferP.Positive := (VATDistribuitionBufferL."Calculated Amount" >= 0);
              VATDistributionBufferP."VAT Prod. Posting Group" := VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT Prod. Posting Group";
              VATDistributionBufferP."VAT Bus. Posting Group" := VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT Bus. Posting Group";
              VATDistributionBufferP."VAT %" := VATDistribuitionBufferL."VAT %";
      // Start EU.0126935.128630
              VATDistributionBufferP.Amount := VATDistribuitionBufferL."Calculated Amount" + VATDistribuitionBufferL."Differential Unit Cost";
      // Stop EU.0126935.128630
              VATDistributionBufferP."VAT Amount" := VATDistribuitionBufferL."Calculated VAT Amount";
              VATDistributionBufferP."Amount LCY" := VATDistributionBufferP.Amount;
              VATDistributionBufferP."VAT Amount LCY" := VATDistributionBufferP."VAT Amount";
              VATDistributionBufferP.INSERT;
            END;
            TotalAmountL += VATDistribuitionBufferL."Calculated Amount";
      // Start EU.0126935.128630
            TotalAmountL += VATDistribuitionBufferL."Differential Unit Cost";
      // Stop EU.0126935.128630
          UNTIL VATDistribuitionBufferL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      EXIT(TotalAmountL);
      // Stop EU.0104306
    END;
